# 上清道宝经

**The Supreme Clarity Scripture of the Treasured Dao**

**Scripture Title:** *The Supreme Clarity Scripture of the Treasured Dao*
**Author:** Anonymous
**Volume:** Five
**Source Text:** *Zhengtong Daoist Canon*, Orthodox Section, Part One

---

**The Supreme Clarity Scripture of the Treasured Dao, Volume One**
**Chapter One**

Upon yellow brocade it is laid,
Inscribed in cinnabar gold,
Bordered with purple gold,
Enclosed in a brocade pouch.

From the High Antiquity,
This scripture spans Middle and Lower Antiquity.
Whoever possesses this text shall have:
The Five Thearchs’ defense,
Jade lads and jade maidens—three each—holding the scripture at their sides,
The Nine Stars’ dark canopy,
And the assembly of perfected immortals, the Five Marchmounts’ numinous officials, attending the chamber day and night.

**The Celestial August Inner Writ**
May be used to guard the household.

**The Three Augusts’ Vermilion Writs in Five Chapters**
Refined in the Cavern-Yang Lodge,
Presented in the Flowing Fire Court,
They give rise to Heaven and establish Earth,
Awakening the numinous spirits.

Should the Son of Heaven obtain them, phoenixes shall come in homage, and the Five Stars align in harmony.
Should feudal lords obtain them, the constellations shall contain their radiance.
Should kings, nobles, or common folk obtain them, their jade-like essence shall ring clear.
Should women obtain them, their countenance shall glow like the Great Sun, their complexion flowing with the Three Lights—fit for empresses and queens.
They soar into the clouds,
The true writs.

**The Jade-Inscribed Writs**
Emerge from the Nine Profound and Nine Heavens,
Dividing governance into Three Dao.
When the Celestial Origin employs these writs,
The Three Luminaries scatter their veils,
The Five Thearchs fall from their stations,
The Nine Revolutions overturn,
The Seven Lodges flee their essences.
When the Terrestrial Origin employs these writs,
The Nine Lands sink into ruin,
The Five Peaks collapse,
Mountains and rivers invert their courses.

**The Three Origins’ Method**
Encompasses the numinous chapters of *The Perfect Scripture of the Great Cavern in Thirty-Nine Scrolls*.
These are the secret signs of the Three and Five,
The utmost essence of the true Dao,
The supreme chapters of the Three Ones,
The forbidden records of Jade Purity.

**The Three Marvels’ Chapters**
The Jade Emperor’s precious writs,
Concealed within the Palace of Great Existence above the Nine Heavens,
In the Jade Chamber of the Great Profound Numinous Terrace.

**The Three Registers**
The Three Origins’ graded admonitions:
Golden Register, Yellow Register, Jade Register.

**The Three Scriptures**
Received under triple oversight.

**The Three Caverns**
Jade Purity Cavern-Real,
Highest Purity Cavern-Mystery,
Supreme Purity Cavern-Spirit.

**The Perfect Scripture of the Great Cavern**
The loftiest resonance of Highest Purity,
The subtlest phrases of utmost reality.

**The Numinous Treasure Scriptures**
The supreme rank of transcendent immortals,
The utmost truth of the Void Origin,
The profound treasure of the Great Dao,
The celestial writs of the Three Augusts.
Some call them the *Jade Tablets of the Most High*.

These Three Cavern scriptures and talismans are the warp and weft of the Dao,
The profound lineage of the Great Void,
The foremost scriptures of the highest perfected,
How could they be heard by middling immortals?

**The Cavern-Spirit, named the Dao of Immortal Treasures**
Connects to the era of the Three Augusts.
**The Cavern-Mystery, named the Dao of Numinous Treasures**
Rescues and delivers the age of the Five Thearchs.
**The Cavern-Real, named the Dao of Heavenly Treasures**
Aids the generations after the Three Dynasties.

**The Seven and Ten Divisions**
The wondrous scriptures of the Primordial Beginning,
Composed in the Dragon Han era.

**The Golden Patterns and Jade Writs of the Most High in the Purple Tenuity Palace**
The secret texts of the supreme sages.

**The Vermilion Gold Writs on Azure Jade Tablets**
The *Jade Instructions of the Most High*.
Thirty-six scrolls.
The Ten Division Scriptures are all inscribed in gold characters,
Written upon jade tablets,
Their chapter titles recorded at the Southern Pavilion of Purple Tenuity in the Great Profound Capital of Jade Metropolis.

**The Five Thearchs Receive the Talismans, Guiding the Three Luminaries**
The Five Thearchs hold the talismans,
The myriad mouths of the *Fixed Register*.
The noble one goes all day without seeing—
Even when seeing, nothing is perceived.
Goes all day without hearing—
Even when hearing, nothing is heard.

**The Transformation of the Profound Capital’s Orthodox Unity**
The Perfected of Orthodox Unity expounds *The Thousand Perfected Disciplinary Scriptures*.
The Most High is wordless;
The noble one goes all day without speaking—
Even when speaking, nothing is conveyed.
Those who excel in transmission must grasp its words,
Must grasp its meaning.
The Perfected listen with spirit—
Such listening is venerable.
The Sage teaches with the body—
Such teaching is precious.
The traces of the Sage may vanish, but the Yellow must endure;
You have yet to distinguish this.
Words may lack what is certain, yet what is certain must exist;
You have yet to decide this.

**The Dao has truth and falsehood; fortune has misfortune and good fortune. Offenses have public and private; clarity has fine and subtle distinctions.** The Three Worlds’ immortals—Ji Facheng and others—**observe rank in their dealings, the worthy and foolish overthrow one another, good and evil reveal each other.** There is no "other," no "self"; no going, no coming. **Encompassing the ten thousand kalpas, all empty space—even the numberless stars of the constellations—are as I, since attaining the Dao and becoming immortal, have likewise been.** Empty space cannot be measured by steps, yet one who knows its mileage—so too is my lifespan. **Taking the Dharma as the source—*Dongxuan* and *Shengxuan* are both of this.** The beings of Heaven and Earth **originate entirely from the Dao, the essence and radiance of primordial chaos, the subtlest mystery of the Supreme Profundity.**

**Silent contemplation:** neither empty nor not-empty, neither Dharma nor not-Dharma, neither thing nor not-thing, neither person nor not-person, neither cause nor not-cause, neither effect nor not-effect, neither beginning nor not-beginning, neither end nor not-end. **Lucidly** behold the perfected Primordial True One.

The two halves make one—being and non-being are the two halves, neither being nor non-being is the true and correct Way. Depart from these four halves and return to ascend the non-vacuous. Realizing non-being is not non-being, knowing being is not being, one dwells securely in the city of the Middle Way’s right contemplation. Turning back to my two halves, abiding in spontaneity, the Dao’s work renews daily, thoughts accumulate in benefit, and the Dharma-heart is seen, the heart’s form mutually perceived.

**Drawing the Dao forth:**
A pure breeze sweeps away the dust of worldly cares.

**The Most High again sounds the Heavenly Drum thirty-six times.**
Looking up to heaven, he invokes:
Mountains and rivers, all waters and lands, every hidden spirit,
the demon kings of the Three Realms, the demon kings of the Six Palaces,
kings and princes of states—whoever can receive and uphold this scripture
shall be joined in strength and together treasured and protected.

**Within formless primordial chaos, before the separation of heaven and earth:**
What Heaven repays comes not swiftly yet is swift; what is sought through resonance arrives without movement.

The Golden Portal’s Supreme Sage commanded the Perfected of the Great Ultimate, dispatching the Jade Lad of the Supreme Profundity and the Orthodox Unity, Wang Zhong, Bao Qiu, and others, to present to Mao Ying the four-jointed *Yantai Luminescent Divine Mushroom*, the *Ever-Radiant Flying Night-Glowing Grotto Grass*, bearing seals and wearing robes and caps, all facing north to complete the rite.

The four messengers addressed Ying:
“He who consumes the four-jointed *Hidden Mushroom* of the Great Ultimate shall be ranked as a Perfected Minister;
he who consumes the *Yantai Jade Mushroom* of the Golden Portal shall be ranked as Controller of Destinies;
he who consumes the *Flowing Brilliance Golden Essence* of the Eastern Palace shall be ranked as Controller of Prosperity;
he who consumes the *Ever-Radiant Flying* shall be ranked as Perfected Earl;
he who consumes the *Night-Glowing Grotto Grass* shall be ranked as Master of the Left and Right Censors’ Office.
You have consumed them all—your lifespan shall be as heaven and earth, and your rank shall be Controller of Destinies, Supreme Perfected of the Eastern Peak, Minister of the Upper Court, commanding the immortals of Wu and Yue, and overseeing the mountain sources of Jiangzuo.”

In an instant, the Five Emperors each arrived riding chariots of their directional colors, descending from the Weaving Palace to receive the Great Emperor’s command, appointing Ying as Controller of Destinies and Supreme Perfected Lord of the Eastern Court. The decree was inscribed on purple jade, its text reading:
*“From his youth, Ying roamed the northern mountains with unbound hair, his heart summoning the Supreme Emperor, moved by the Great Profundity to devotion. Now he is appointed Perfected of the Great Profundity, Divine Lord Controller of Destinies. His conduct is firm as metal and stone, his cinnabar heart steadfast among the multitudes—now he is rewarded with the Jade Yue, the Green Banner, and the Eight Might’s staff, to subdue the sources of marshes and vanquish the myriad spirits. He once dwelt in the cold valleys of Eastern Grove—now he is rewarded with the Purple Tassel’s staff, the Lotus-Blossom Crown, to summon a thousand spirits and command clouds upon the mountains. He forsook his home to wander alone—thus he is granted the embroidered feathers, the purple mantle, the cinnabar and azure flying skirts, to ascend the celestial steps at ease, bearing the mandate of the Jade Perfected. He traversed deep thickets—thus he is rewarded with the Spotted Dragon’s chariot, the White Tiger’s plow, to float in revelry through the great void, his flying wheels gracing the imperial court. He endured frost and snow—thus he is granted the Curved Dawn’s precious canopy, the Jasper Curtains, the Crimson Chamber, to roam and gaze upon the Nine Palaces in serene warmth. He concealed his form in secluded peaks, his spirit contemplating the myriad groves—thus he is rewarded with the Divine Flowing Fire Bell, the Twin Pearls of Bright Moon, to ascend and report to the Great Ultimate, to convey his voice to the Supreme Clarity. His true heart is lofty and still—thus he is granted the brocade banner, the embroidered pennant, the white feathered black staff, to summon the Six Yin and the Jade Maidens to attend his carriage. His kindness extends to all things, his hidden virtue governs the myriad beings—thus he is rewarded with the Phoenix’s flute, the golden bell, the jade chime, to harmonize the spirits in the empty halls, to delight the Perfected and dance with the numinous. No being can disrupt his resonance, no thousand evils can enslave his purity—thus he is rewarded with the Purple Essence’s marrow, the Jade Nectar, the Golden Infant, to share the lifespan of the Three Luminaries, to inscribe his name upon the Cinnabar Jade. Ying’s heart shines with the radiance of the sun, his spirit leaps with the great aurora—he has redeemed the longevity of others, thus he is styled ‘Great Profundity.’ With the nine virtues complete, he is now instructed in nine affairs, granted forty Jade Boys and forty Jade Maidens to attend his comings and goings in the Great Reverence, to receive affairs from the Great Ultimate, and to govern the office of the Red City Jade Grotto’s府. His movements and stillness shall be reported.”*

Ying prostrated himself to receive the decree, bowing twice to the Perfected of the Great Profundity.

**The Inner Transmission of Lord Mao**

**Before Heaven and After Heaven:**
One beginning, one end—minor kalpas and great kalpas.

**Merits inscribed on jade tablets:**
Ascension to heaven in broad daylight.

Seeking to overturn the bitter sea,
Ever cause the river of desire to run dry.
The Dao has no form or shape—
It borrows words and images as its ford.

Harmony is the source of all affairs.
True rectitude within rectitude:
Dispelling what is to be dispelled,
Attaining what is to be attained—
Both reliance and relinquishment are forgotten,
The mind vanishes in what it forgets.

Knocking my head at the window of scripture masters,
I beg to unseal the gate of the Double Mystery.
All open the true mark,
All enter the Mystery Gate—
Like the Jade City of the Dark Capital,
Opened through eight gates,
Where people of the eight directions each enter through their gate.

The heavens are vast and boundless,
Myriad paths all return to one.
The Two Exhaustions—
Still the realm of the two deaths:
Within lies the death-realm of the great appointed end,
Without, the death-root of thought-moment after thought-moment.

*The Record of the Supreme Ultimate and the Immortal Duke’s Daily Observances*

Transcending the two death-realms,
Surpassing the three foundations of the Three Clarities—
The Heavenly Elder posed a question.

The dark name is inscribed on the green register and white tally:
The wondrous Dao of yin and yang,
The supreme art of ingestion and adornment—
All are divine formulas and secret instructions.

What you heard before was not yet true seeing;
What you hear now is true hearing.

Above heaven, below heaven.

All attain radiance, the earth becomes lapis lazuli and the seven treasures. Along the roads stand rows of trees, each side identical, and beneath every tree stand jade maidens and immortal youths, holding fragrant flowers in their hands. In the empty void, divine immortals perform myriad forms of music and dance. Within each land resides the Supreme Divine Lord, seated upon a golden couch within a seven-jeweled terrace.

The *Sutra of the Wondrous Dharma Wheel* emerges from boundless eons, vast as the kalpas of the Ganges, its brilliance shining like stars across the cosmos. This sutra is like the moon’s full radiance, illuminating the ten directions; as the three realms lie in darkness, this sutra rises like the sun, universally illuminating all heavens. Like the flow of ten thousand rivers, this sutra is the abyss of the Scorching Valley, the source of the Lü Sea, to which all return; like the height of Mount Sumeru, this sutra is the Jade Capital Mountain, encompassing all.

Above, it governs the Three Luminaries; in the middle, it harmonizes yin and yang; below, it unfolds the myriad lives. Those who cultivate this sutra without weariness will swiftly summon the dragon chariot and ascend in broad daylight.

The *Dao De Jing* speaks of its virtue: like spring, it gives life to the myriad things; like summer, it nurtures and ripens them; like autumn, it brings them to majesty. Its virtue is like the seven treasures, prized by all things; like a bright mirror, reflecting the myriad things; like a great kingdom, lacking nothing; like a mountain, upon which all things depend; like the sea, containing all things; like the moon, casting its light upon all things; like the sun’s rays, illuminating all things. Its virtue is like the earth’s thickness, bearing the myriad things; like heaven’s vastness, covering all. Thus it pervades heaven and earth, giving rise to the four seasons. The upper scripture is heaven, the lower scripture is earth.

The heart is like lapis lazuli—
The Supreme resolves all doubts.
Above, nothing is unilluminated;
Below, nothing is unpenetrated.
Penetration reaches the numinous.

The *Numinous Treasure* spans the great Dharma Bridge,
Revealing the Dao,
Guiding with the Dharma,
To deliver beings from the Three Calamities and Eight Difficulties.
It opens the gates of sweet dew and immortality,
Extending my entry into the Dharma,
Abiding in the chamber of non-action.

The Mind-King
Dwells in the city of the Middle Way,
With Dharma as its sincere teaching,
Forming the walls and moats of the Dharma.

The Three Supreme Dharmas—
The Perfected of the Supreme Ultimate, Xu Laile, gathers the assembly.
All the great sages of the heavens convene at Penglai.
Bowing before the Dao,
The Supreme Lord of the Dao sits upon a jeweled lotus,
Flanked by tens of thousands of jade maidens and immortal youths.

The Lord of the Dao wears a nine-colored feathered robe,
A gown of flying frost and floating pearls,
A crown of ten thousand transformations,
A belt with the Morning Sun Sword and the Bell of the Sun.
The dark chant resounds in four directions,
The phoenix’s wings stir with a single stroke,
Dragon patterns gleam in the azure abyss,
Crimson splendor shines upon rivers and marshes,
The pheasant’s celestial form adorns orchid and jade,
Golden essence emerges from secluded valleys.
Riding the Great Compliance to command the supreme image,
Roaming the pure spirit to merge the Five Turbidities,
Emptily emitting the Nine Falls,
Profoundly feasting the Nine Awakenings,
Dancing with shadows to fan the void,
Riding the void to grasp the mist.

Through the cultivation of the Ten Practices,
With all lamps and torches,
Illuminating the darkness of evil,
Journeying toward the royal city.

Amidst the surging clouds of the Great Dharma,
A single chariot of sweet dew descends,
Dharma’s sprouts arise along the Dao’s path.
The One Flavor rains upon the Ten Directions,
The Two-by-Two Dharma Seal
Establishes my Dharma Gate.
The Palace of Undying—
The Southern Pole’s Songling Palace.
The Great Dharma of human-making,
The world’s finest physician.
The Numinous Treasure’s First Gate—
The stairway of virtue and practice.
Enter its gate, and the Dao’s chambers may be fathomed;
Ascend its steps, and merit and achievement grow daily.

From ancient past to present—
The True One’s natural Dao.
Most subtle, most wondrous, most profound, most mysterious,
Neither being nor non-being, neither mortal nor sage,
Wisdom serves as the boat and oar,
Shaking off the Ten Entanglements.
Ascend the ever-abiding shore,
Where celestial wondrous blossoms rain—
The blossoms of the Kānā Forest.
Strike the music of the Heavenly Musicians—
The melodies of Heavenly Hooks.

The Supreme Ultimate and Great Void Perfected One
Addressed the Left Immortal Duke, saying:
"Formerly, I received from the Most High Golden Sun
The True One’s Ascending Mystery Inner Teaching,
The First Gate of the Primary Gate,
Practiced by the Five Thearchs.
This scripture is the parent of all karmic deeds of the Perfected Ones—
The *Hidden Writ of Jade Purity*.

**The Master-Disciple Rank, Second**
Without a master, one does not proceed;
Without a master, one is not born;
Without a master, one is not delivered;
Without a master, one does not ascend as an immortal.
The Eightfold Radiance Dragon Chariot—
Therein one may transcend the Jade Pass of the Supreme Ultimate.
Ascend high, and there is no above;
Delve deep, and there is no limit.
Great sages and great worthies:
First serve a minor master, seeking the minor Dao;
Then serve a middling master, seeking the middling Dao;
Then serve a great master, seeking the great Dao.
Tread the Dao’s path as the plumb line and inked cord,
As law and standard—
Divine Masters, True Masters, Dao Masters,
Immortal Masters, Sage Masters, Worthy Masters.

Beside the master stand the Nine:
First, Great Compassion;
Second, Great Mercy;
Third, Great Joy;
Fourth, Great Renunciation;
Fifth, Great Goodness;
Sixth, Great Dharma;
Seventh, Great Merit;
Eighth, Great Transformation;
Ninth, Great Virtue.

Within a single heaven—
Numbered as the Perfected Immortals and Sages, twenty-seven ranks.
The Three Ones mirror within,
Master and friend smooth the path without—
The Three Primes’ True One.

At the Kunlun’s Mystic Orchard Palace,
Meet the Orthodox Unity Perfected One,
The Three Heavens’ Dharma Master,
The Highest Clarity Perfected One,
The Grand Overseer of All Immortals.

The Longevity Dharma Master,
Who fathered the Three Lords,
Surnamed Bo Cheng, styled Zhi Hao,
Was a man of the Middle August era.
In the year of the Eastern Well’s conjunction,
He was born beneath the cypress groves of Beihai Zhongshan,
Where sweet dew, purple mushrooms, luminous pearls,
And the triple confluence of dragon blossoms
Sprouted at his resting place.
His mother conceived by the white dew’s touch.
At fourteen, he served the Duke of Xigui as minister,
Fearing neither Yi nor Ju,
And studied under Master Huanggu.
Later, he encountered the Jade Purity’s Wenchang,
The Eastern Jade Radiance Immortal Duke,
And was styled the Jade Sovereign.

The Second Dao Lord bestowed the *Great Cavern Perfected Scripture*.
All ghosts shun the Three Caverns Dharma Master—
Those who receive the Three Caverns Dharma’s transmission,
All ghosts and spirits turn in retreat.

Reciting the *Great Cavern Perfected Scripture’s* thirty-nine chapters—
A task of the highest Perfected Ones.
One who can uplift the Most High,
Seize the Nine Perfected’s mandate,
Rank among the lofty immortals,
And stand equal with the Directors of Destinies,
Following the Most High’s Yellow Simplicity,
Is called the Fourteen Expedients.
Such a one is named a Great Cavern Dharma Master,
Radiant among the myriad Perfected,
Ranking as a Supreme Ultimate High Immortal.

Reciting the *Great Elixir’s Hidden Writ*, the *Golden Flower’s Cavern Chamber*,
And the *Feminine One’s Treasure Scripture*—
With refined sincerity, the Supreme Simplicity responds,
The master descends with the Nine Utensils,
The Five Thearchs follow the Most High’s Yellow Simplicity,
Called the Fourteen Affairs’ Expedients.
Such a one is named a Three Primes Dharma Master,
A Primal Radiance Perfected One,
A High Immortal of the Nine Thearchs.

Reciting the *Cavern Mystery’s Mystic Scripture*—
Penetrating the numinous, reaching the spirit,
Dispersing the Seven Scriptures,
Following the Most High’s Yellow Simplicity’s forty-four expedients,
One is named a Cavern Mystery Dharma Master,
A Highest Radiance Perfected One,
Ranking among the Nine Palaces’ Earthly Immortals.
One’s name enters the Southern Palace—
The Perfected One’s rank,
Recorded in the Most High’s cinnabar and ink registers.

The Peerless Primal Lord, the Great Mystery Youth,
The Wondrous Practice Perfected One, the Boundless Master.
The *Illuminating Might*.

The Three Primes’ Palaces—
Transforming and responding as the Nine,
Nine Palaces, Nine Spirits,
Three Nines making twenty-seven steps,
Nine Sages, Nine Perfected, Nine Immortals,
The Most High Jade Emperor,
The Ninefold Refined Highest Perfected.

Three ranks—
The highest are Sages, the lowest are Immortals, the middle are Perfected.
Ten transformations—
The body is altered.

Sages have nine grades:
Highest Sage, Lofty Sage, Great Sage,
Divine Sage, Mystic Sage, True Sage,
Immortal Sage, Numinous Sage, Ultimate Sage.

Serpents obtaining the Numinous Treasure
Transform into divine dragons.
Birds obtaining it
Become phoenixes.
Beasts obtaining it
Become qilin.
Ordinary folk obtaining it
Are called sages.

The Perfected have nine grades—
As the nine sages.
The highest grade is Sage—
Practicing the Great Mystery, ascending to Highest Clarity.
The middle grade is Perfected—
Practicing the Great Peace, ascending to Highest Clarity.

The Embryonic Dao and Womb Spirit—
The Jade Clarity Palace’s lower Perfected,
Are the Highest Clarity Palace’s higher Perfected.
The Supreme Ultimate Palace’s higher Perfected,
Are the Highest Clarity Palace’s lower Perfected.
The Supreme Ultimate Palace’s lower Perfected,
Next attain the Nine Palaces’ Flying Immortals.

The Most High’s Dao has three:
*The Jade Purity’s Hidden Writ*,
*The Divine Tiger’s Great Talisman*,
*The Golden Tiger’s True Talisman*.
Practicing this Dao,
One becomes the Most High’s Perfected,
Granted three thousand Jade Lads and Jade Maidens each,
Ranking as the Jade Sovereign of the Highest Perfected.

The Highest Perfected’s Dao has six:
*The Most High’s Yuyi Rushing Sun Text*,
*The Most High’s Jielin Rushing Moon Chapter*,
*The Celestial Thearch of the Great Tenuity’s Flying Heaven Scripture*,
*The Great Cavern Perfected Scripture’s Thirty-Nine Chapters*,
*The Golden Watchtower’s Numinous Writ of Purple Text*,
*The Yellow Elder’s Eight Dao Nine Perfected Central Scripture*.
Practicing these in totality,
One becomes a Highest Clarity Perfected One,
Granted three thousand Jade Lads and Jade Maidens each,
Ranking as an Emperor of All Heavens,
Preceded by the myriad Perfected,
Followed by phoenix songs,
The Dark Pact’s White Emperor,
And the soaring dragons that open the path.
*The Winged Axle*.

The Middle Perfected’s Dao has seven:
*The Great Elixir’s Hidden Writ*,
*The Audience with the Perfected’s High Scripture*,
*The Jade Emperor’s Divine Talismans*,
*The Three Heavens’ Orthodox Dharma Phoenix Perfected Text*,
*The Four Perfected’s Chapters*,
*The Most High’s Golden Writs’ Methods*,
*The Cavern Chamber’s Jade Characters*,
*The High Scripture of the Six Jia’s Numinous Flight*,
*The Three August Ones’ Inner Writ*,
*The Celestial Writ’s Great Characters*,
*The Azure Waist’s Purple Writ*,
*The Curved Silk’s Secret Verses*.
Practicing these in totality,
One becomes a Highest Clarity Middle Dao Perfected One,
Granted three thousand Jade Lads and Jade Maidens each,
Ranking as the Highest Clarity’s Left and Right Ministers’ Master,
Proceeding with the purple tassels’ regalia,
Followed by the myriad spirits and thousand Perfected,
Phoenix flutes leading the way,
Heavenly Hooks playing behind.

The Dark Dragon Initiates the Dao,
The Five Thearchs attend in chariots,
Soaring through the Great Void.

The Lower Perfected’s Dao comprises eight:
*The Highest Clarity’s Nine Transformations and Ten Changes’ Three-Nine Plain Speeches*,
*The Cinnabar Scenery’s Dao Essence Concealed in Earth’s Eight Guards*,
*The Heavenly Pass’ Three Charts*,
*The Dark-Yellow Jade Writ*,
*The Divine Continent’s Seven Changes and Seven Turns’ Cavern Scripture in Crimson and Green*,
*The Yellow Dao’s Jade-White Dragon Writ*,
*The Multitude of Writs’ Plain Memorials in Central Chapters*,
*The Five Phases’ Secret Talismans*,
*The Five Jade-Dark Chapters*,
*The Upper Prime’s Jade Writ*.

Practicing these in totality,
One becomes a Highest Clarity Lower Prime Perfected One,
Proceeding with the five-colored regalia,
Jade Maidens chanting ahead,
Nine Phoenixes playing behind,
Eight Simurghs and White Dragons initiating the Dao,
The Supreme Ultimate attending in chariots,
Soaring in inverted light,
Roaming and wandering the Purple Chamber.

Bathing in the blossoms of the Ox Clouds,
Pouring the five-colored qi from above the crown.

The Upper Void’s Purple Radiance Nine Empyrean Perfected King—
His form spans ninety million leagues,
In the third month of winter, he stabilizes and establishes the Golden Flower’s Flying Heavenly Stronghold,
Wearing a robe inscribed with the flowing essence of sun and moon,
Adorned with the Flowing Gold Phoenix Seal,
Girded with the Hundred-Transformations Interlocking Gold Sword,
Standing amidst nine-colored lotus and purple clouds,
His luminosity penetrating and illuminating the Jade Clarity above.

In the third month of spring, he transforms his form,
Wearing the Nine Clarities upon his head,
Holding a golden coin in his mouth,
Grasping the solar emblem in his hand,
Standing upon purple clouds,
His mouth radiating azure above.

In the third month of summer, he transforms into nine figures,
All clad in azure-feathered robes,
Each wearing a moon upon their heads,
Wielding nine-colored banners,
Upon the purple clouds.

In the third month of autumn, he transforms into a luminous tri-color of azure, white, and dark,
His radiance penetrating and illuminating.

*The Highest Clarity Primordial Beginning’s Transformations Turtle Mountain’s Primordial Record Scripture*

Left Mystery, Right Mystery—
The Perfected One stabilizes his resolve.

The Four Venerable Perfected Ones—
Within sunlight, they cast no shadow.

The Most High Perfected One—
Descends upon the River’s banks.

The Azure Thearch of the East, Lesser Yang Ninefold Numinous Perfected,
The Vermilion Thearch of the South, Greater Yang Southern Culmen Perfected,
The White Thearch of the West, Lesser Yin Numinous Simplicity Perfected,
The Black Thearch of the North, Greater Yin Mysterious Numinous Perfected,
The Yellow Thearch of the Center, Threefold Numinous Perfected—
The Twenty-Four Perfected receive their commissions from the Azure Lads of the Four Quarters.

*The Arrayed Records of the Ninefold Mysterious Dao Lords of Later Sagacity*

Wandering freely amid the Three Clarities.

*The Jade Numinous Purple Radiance Scripture of the Highest Highest Clarity*

Immortals possess nine ranks,
Corresponding to the Nine Perfected.
The lowest rank, Solar Immortals,
Study the Great Clarity’s Golden Elixir and Jade Essence,
Ascending to the Great Clarity’s Luminous Might.
Souls perfected, spirits completed,
They become guests in the Purple Court.

The upper immortals ascend to heaven in broad daylight.
The middle immortals govern grotto-chambers in famous mountains,
Innately aligned with the True One.
The Golden Towers and Orchid Terraces bear jade texts and vermilion graphs,
Resonant with the upper immortals.
Transforming in the Southern Palace,
Shedding their bones, transmuting their embryos.

Golden Immortals—
Their hue like golden radiance.
On the Eastern Marchmount and Southern Marchmount,
Three thousand nine hundred leagues across the sea,
To the east dwell ninety thousand immortals,
And twenty-four myriad jade maidens.
The immortals reside in the Yang Offices of Gradation,
Three thousand leagues from Knife-Script Mountain,
Where three million divine dragons dwell,
And immortals ascend to heaven riding them.

Those who cultivate the Dao of the Great One
All attain ascent through the Three Heavens,
Bathe in the Eastern Well,
Master the Three Principles and Six Disciplines,
Adorned in gold and purple, their vermilion seals resplendent,
Transforming without end.
With the divine elixir long refined,
The golden liquor ninefold transmuted—
The method of the Returning Elixir lies in the Golden Book’s *Ren* Scripture.

The Jade Clarity illumines the Mysterious Capital,
Ten Sages revolve through the Purple Tenuity,
Parting clouds to emerge from the Ten Heavens,
Soaring through the sky on flying heavens,
Their cinnabar auroras bearing light canopies,
Sun and moon bathing them in numinous splendor.

*From the Twenty-Four Images of Life*

Wielding sun and moon in their hands,
The Five Penetrations Immortals, Supreme Perfected—
Exhaling and inhaling to refine the Five Spirits,
Illuminating the *Canons of Perfected Clarity*.
Their essence gathered in the Seven Treasures Grove,
Their eyes gleaming with the essence of sun and moon,
The Most High governs the Purple Terrace,
All Perfected chant the Grotto Scriptures.

Riding dragons,
Mounting dragons to tread the dark waves,
Washing their feet in the Eight Heavens’ River—
Thus they loosen the celestial nets and earthly snares,
Having already transcended them.
Preserving their offspring on the flying dark path,
The Five Numinous tally their registers.

The great barges—
A metaphor for the Great Vehicle.
The middle ferries—
Compared to the Middle Vehicle.
The small boats—
Likened to the Lesser Vehicle.
The purple brocade—
Using purple’s abundance to represent the Three Vehicles.

Ten lamps, a thousand lamps—
Their light illumining the ten directions,
Shining upon all heavens.
The Three Flowers—
The name of the Great One’s golden chamber.

The superior adept—
Achieving perfection in a single lifetime,
Their resolve unwavering,
They turn their bodies to ascend the Great Ultimate,
Their rank elevated to Immortal Minister.
The Dharma Wheel.

The middle adept—

The *Oral Transmission on Numinous Writings*—
Three extinctions, three rebirths,
Their resolve firm and unwavering,
They ascend to the Grand Clarity,
Becoming the Nine Palaces’ Perfected.

The inferior adept—
Loving mountains and delighting in waters,
Their heart like a cinnabar elixir held within,
In seated stillness, they face the master’s sacred treasures,
In coming and going, they companion with birds and beasts.
Nine extinctions, nine rebirths,
Their aspiration unyielding,
They roam the dark realms of the Five Peaks,
Soaring through the Great Primordium.

Refining gold for profit—
This is the superior adept.

The superior person—
A celestial adept.
The middle person—
A human adept.
The inferior person—
An earthly adept.

Heaven and earth open the gate of Dao and virtue.
The superior adept receives qi in its pure and true form,
Earning the title of "Flying Chariot."
The middle adept responds to the numinous and the Jade Constellations,
Attaining the art of middle longevity and deathlessness.
The inferior adept gains a lifespan of five hundred years.

The spirit-listener—
Penetrates the formless.
The heart-listener—
Knows the inner truth.

The Heavenly Treasure Venerable—
The primordial qi of the Most High Jade Emperor,
Born in the first kalpa of Dragon Han as the Heavenly Treasure Lord.

The Primordial August Supreme Venerable—
His form spans ninety million *zhang*.
In the three months of spring,
He wears a crown of flowing essence and purple radiance,
Robes of nine-light brocade,
A sash of seamless, self-arisen nine colors,
And a belt of Six-Mountain Fire Jade.
Ever riding clouds of azure and dark green,
Seated upon a nine-colored lion,
His light resplendent,
He dwells above the Grand Clarity, within the Jade Void.

In the three months of summer,
He transforms into a single body with nine heads,
A thousand *zhang* in length,
Wearing a crown of nine-colored clouds,
Robes of moon-brocade with boundless shifting hues,
A seamless embrace of light,
And a sword of Nine Heavens’ immortal refinement.
Riding clouds of cinnabar and purple,
Seated upon a nine-colored dragon,
He abides within the Jade Void’s purple clouds.

In the three months of autumn,
He transforms into a single body with nine phoenix heads,
Five thousand *zhang* in length,
Clad in nine-colored, variegated tiger robes,
Riding seven-colored clouds,
Dwelling above the Highest Clarity.

In the three months of winter,
He transforms into hues of blue-black,
His light blazing like a solar eclipse.

The Jade Perfected Nine Heavens Venerable—
His form spans ninety million *zhang*.
In the three months of spring,
He transforms into a phoenix,
A single body with nine heads,
Wearing a crown of nine qi and dark essence,
Robes of nine-colored, variegated feathers,
Riding a twelve-colored flying *lin*,
Seated upon a five-colored lotus,
Dwelling within the Grand Clarity’s Purple Void.

In the three months of summer,
He transforms into a dragon’s body with a human head,
Wearing a crown of two-colored light,
Robes of blue, yellow, and purple feathered garments,
His mouth holding a plain sash,
Riding five-colored clouds,
Seated upon a five-colored lion,
His light illuminating the Earthly Clarity.

In the three months of autumn,
He transforms into a radiance of purple and green,
Like the sun and moon overlapping.

In the three months of winter,
He wears a crown of flying essence with boundless transformations,
Robes of nine-colored, flowing-light, self-arisen brocade,
And a sash of penetrating truth,
Riding five-colored clouds,
Seated upon five-colored clouds.

The August Elder of the Three Heavens—
His form spans thirty million *zhang*.
In the three months of spring,
He wears a crown of seven treasures and penetrating essence,
Robes of flying-cloud, flowing-light purple brocade,
A sash bearing the sacred seal of the August Mandate,
Ever seated upon a writhing, shifting light of dark hues,
Resplendent and luminous,
Dwelling above the Highest Clarity, within the Cavernous Void.
When contemplated, he returns to a length of three *cun* and three *fen*.

In the three months of summer,
He transforms into a single body with three heads,
Wearing a crown of blue, yellow, and green clouds,
Robes of three-colored, variegated patterns,
Seated upon twelve-flowered radiance.
When contemplated, he reverts to his true form.

In the three months of autumn,
He transforms into a body of golden hue,
His neck bearing twelve-colored national light,
Robes of sudden-bursting, boundless-light brocade,
A sash of golden tiger and phoenix patterns,
Seated upon threefold plain luminous clouds.
When contemplated, he reverts to his true form.

In the three months of winter,
He transforms into a radiance of blue-green and purple,
Intertwined like the moon’s essence.
This is the Three Heavens Venerable returning the qi of the Cavernous Void,
Further receiving the refinement of the August Elder of the Three Heavens.
When contemplated, he reverts to his true form.

The Highest Numinous Treasure Nine Heavens Venerable—
His form spans nine thousand *zhang*.
In the three months of spring,
He transforms into nine figures,
Each like a youth,
Clad in robes of a single color,
Their mouths holding the sun,
All seated upon nine-colored clouds,
Illuminating the Three Clarities.

In the three months of summer,
He transforms into a nine-colored light,
Like rising clouds.

In the three months of autumn,
He wears a crown of purple origin and flowing light with nine transformations,
Robes of cinnabar brocade with seven-colored patterned radiance,
A sash bearing the three treasures’ awakening numen,
And a seal of seven-leaping origin.

In the three months of winter,
He transforms into nine-headed youths,
Seated upon crimson clouds.

The Venerable of Dao and Virtue—
The father and mother of Dao and virtue.

The Heavenly Treasure Lord—
The august deity of the Great Cavern.

The *Nine Heavens’ Chapters of Spirit Generation*—

The Numinous Treasure Lord—
The august deity of the Cavernous Mystery.

The Spirit Treasure Lord—
The august deity of the Cavernous Spirit.

The Upper Palace of Green Yang—
The Middle Primordial Record-Keeper of the Office of Scenic Radiance,
Lord of the Dao in the Green Yang Palace,
His feet shod in five-colored shoes,
Holding the staff of awe-inspiring spirit,
Riding the flying-turtle, dark-cloud chariot,
Drawn by a team of green dragons.

The Palace of Green Yang—
The Great Dao Lord of the Primordial Scenic Elder in the Mysterious Micro Palace,
Holding the sacred seal of life’s mandate,
Riding the human-scene and blue-cloud chariot,
Drawn by a team of azure dragons.

The Upper Palace of Lesser Yang—
The Boundless Jade Radiance Lord of the Dao in the Grand Tenuity Palace,
Surnamed Wang, named Yuan Ying,
Holding the summoning numinous seal,
Riding the dark-scene, green-canopied, five-colored cloud chariot,
Drawn by a team of phoenixes.

The Upper Palace of Greater Yang—
The Grand Void Scenic Grand Marshal and Radiant Lord of the Dao in the Purple Tenuity Palace,
Surnamed Xuan, named Bo Yang,
Wearing a crown of level-heaven luminous essence and jade,
Holding the seal of demon-subduing,
Riding the light-bright Dao chariot and crimson-cloud chariot.

The Upper Palace of Lesser Yin—
The Great Heavenly One Lord of the Dao in the Numinous Micro Yang Palace,
Holding the staff of life’s mandate,
Riding the jade-pennant, five-hued canopy, vermilion-purple cloud chariot,
Drawn by a team of six dragons.

The Upper Palace of Greater Yin—
The Grand Harmony Lord of the Dao in the Essence Micro Dui Palace,
Clad in white-twisted, plain numinous sashes,
Holding the jade seal of life-preserving mandate,
Riding the crimson-jade, azure-pennant, white-cloud chariot,
Drawn by a team of white tigers.

The Upper Palace of Yin Radiance—
The Dao Lord of Grand Yang in the Cavern Radiance Registry of the Pristine Subtlety Palace,
Clad in dark-cloud green sashes,
Riding the dark-radiance eight-light cinnabar palanquin and purple-cloud chariot,
Drawn by a team of Dark Warriors.

The Upper Palace of Yin Essence—
The Dao Lord of Refined Harmony in the Dao Subtlety Palace,
Clad in dark-cloud five-hued sashes,
Holding the jade pennant of non-regression,
Drawn by a team of dark phoenixes.

The Supreme Void Sovereign Lord—
Wearing a vermilion robe of flying brocade,
Crowned with seventy-two hues of sun-cradling, moon-bearing light,
And clad in a luminous brocade robe of a hundred transformations,
Like the drifting clouds of Grand Simplicity.
The Primal Origin’s metamorphoses.

The Purple Cloud Supreme Primal Sovereign Lord of the Dao—
Girded with the phoenix insignia of flowing light,
Riding twin clouds of purple and azure,
Clad in a nine-hued flying celestial dharma robe,
Abiding in the Purple Void.

The Supreme Jade Void Lord—
Crowned with the nine-transformations flower coronet of Dao essence,
Clad in nine-hued flying clouds,
Resembling floating clouds,
Within the Purple Void.

The Three Heavens Grand Radiance Supreme Lord—
Adorned with seventy-two transformations of flowing-gold fire bells.

The Supreme Lord Master of the Purple Dawn—
Bearing the talisman of the Supreme Minister’s numinous control,
Girded with the Eastern Meng strategy of primordial chaos,
Seated upon a nine-hued azure dragon,
Above the Terrace of Responsibility,
Illuminating the Upper Clarity.

The Supreme Emperor Lord of the Purple Void—
Wearing the nine-qi flowing-essence purple-luminance coronet,
Clad in the nine-hued primal-seam spontaneous robe,
Adorned with the seven-origin night-luminous seal,
Girded with the Primal Sovereign’s mandate-strategy.

The Supreme Elder Lord of the Purple Void—
Clad in the sun-essence robe of numinous script,
Standing amidst dark clouds,
Seated upon a nine-hued numinous tortoise,
Within azure clouds.

The Pristine Subtlety Cavern Radiance Lord of Grand Darkness—
Girded with the cinnabar sovereign’s imperial belt,
Clad in the tortoise-script robe,
Transforming into a numinous tortoise with three hundred sixty patterns,
Holding the seven stars in its mouth,
Seated beneath the canopy of splendor.

The Supreme Simplicity Lofty Void Supreme Purple Void Lord—
Adorned with six-mountain fire jade,
Girded with the numinous-flying purple sash,
Clad in a thirty-two-hued dharma robe,
Within the Upper Clarity Palace.

The Central Origin Lofty Maiden of Purple Orchid in the Void Radiance—
Clad in golden-purple insignia,
Girded with the golden-light sword,
Standing upon azure mist,
Transforming into purple-azure radiance,
Like the sun’s ascent.

The Three Origins Purple Essence Lord of the Purple Void—
Adorned with the imperial script of the Nine Heavens’ dragon script,
Girded with the sun-essence sword,
Transforming into a youth with cloud-tousled topknot.

The True Yang Primal Elder Lord of Dark Unity—
Crowned with a five-hued floral canopy,
Holding the five sacred mushrooms,
Transforming into sunlight,
Verdant and lush,
Within purple clouds.

The Celestial Emperor Lord of the Grand Tenuity—
Girded with the night-luminous treasure herb,
His body emanating thirty-two hues of precious light,
Holding golden bells,
Transforming into sunlit purple rays,
Within the Jade Void.

The Supreme Simplicity Three Origins Lord of the Grand Origin—
Clad in floating-vacuity purple-gas brocade,
Wearing a nine-hued dragon-brocade feathered skirt,
Girded with the imperial talisman and dragon script,
Seated within the Grand Chamber,
Like the sun’s brilliance,
Like gold’s essence.

The Azure Numinosity Lord of Yang Peace—
Clad in cinnabar brocade robes,
Crowned with a flying dragon,
Holding the moon in his mouth,
Grasping the purple sash.

The Supreme Simplicity Lord—
The image of the three suns,
Within the primordial qi,
Above the Purple Empyrean.

The Three Essences Lord of Purple Essence in the Upper Clarity—
Clad in azure, azure-green, and purple feathered robes,
Intertwined in primordial chaos,
Like ascending clouds.

The Sovereign Clarity Cavern Truth Lord—
Within the Grand Void,
Illuminating the Ten Heavens.

The Four Elders Lord of the Dao in the Imperial Clarity—
Clad in phoenix-script patterned robes,
Holding the seven lives in his mouth.

The Grand Dao Lord of the Jade Dawn—
Girded with the bright-moon bells,
Crowned with a horned headscarf,
Holding the golden talisman,
Upon the Five Mushrooms Flower Mountain.

The Central Yellow Elder Lord—
Girded with the intertwining-numinous sash,
Clad in a flying celestial feathered robe.

The Grand Origin Cavern Radiance Lord of the Supreme Ultimate Dao—
Girded with the treasure immortal’s sword,
His head emanating flowing-gold light,
Illuminating seventy-four directions,
Standing upon a dark tortoise,
Hair unbound to his waist,
Within purple qi.

The Central Pristine Elder Lord of the Supreme Origin—
Standing upon a nine-hued lion,
Holding a golden branch.

The Central Yellow Elder Lord—
Disciple of the Celestial Emperor Lord of the Grand Tenuity,
Born spontaneously in the second year of the Supreme Void’s reign,
Sunlight doubled in radiance,
Intertwining brilliance with clouds,
Five-hued misty canopy,
Jubilant smoke and dark stillness,
From the portal of the Primal Darkness,
Hand-parting the myriad chambers’ courts,
The Supreme One bestowed upon him the Nine Perfected Oral Scriptures and the Eight Dao Secret Talismans,
Making him the Perfected of the Supreme Ultimate.

The Azure Waist Emperor Lord—
Disciple of the Nine Yangs Primal Jade Emperor,
Born in the first year of the Central Sovereign’s reign,
In the eastern quadrant,
Nurtured within the Jade Country’s Heavenly Precipice,
Beneath the Seven Treasures of the Heavenly Jasper Grove,
By the shores of the Nine Domains’ vast expanse,
Manifesting in accordance with the charts of transformations,
At the third dawn’s first light,
Nine dragons flanked his sides,
Seven-hued jasper phoenixes shaded his body,
Divine unicorns bearing sacred mushrooms fed him in darkness,
Heavenly maidens exhaled essence to bathe him,
Jade lads scattered flowers to dispel filth,
Divine consorts strewed blossoms to ward off dust,
His body like crowned jade,
His face radiating golden countenance,
His form bearing all signs,
His words like golden scriptures,
Dark clouds and purple canopies arose from his chamber,
Flying essence and flowing light illuminated his court,
His heart roamed the radiant-mist realm,
He wandered the jasper ruins of the Jade Country,
Taking purple clouds as his dwelling,
Azure mist as his city,
Yellow gold as his palace,
White jade as his form,
Golden halls and jade steps,
Phoenix towers spread in four directions,
Golden lads attending at his side,
Jade maidens holding their silence,
Celestial immortals arrayed in guard,
Over five thousand strong,
Feathered riders like unicorns,
Dark qi in ninefold assembly,
Numinous phoenixes trailing mist,
Azure Waist is also styled the Azure Emperor Lord,
Receiving the Jade Emperor’s golden, jade, and purple scriptures of wondrous secrets,
All the writings above the Nine Heavens,
The hidden texts of the Eight Assemblies.

The Celestial Emperor Lord of the Grand Tenuity—
Born at the inception of the Azure Origin,
Purple clouds flashing like lightning,
Dark mist veiling the canopy,
Cinnabar radiance entwining,
Nowhere too obscure to perceive,
Nothing above unseen,
Nothing below unobserved,
At fourteen years of age,
Golden countenance inwardly radiant,
Jade splendor outwardly shining,
Stilling the nine empyrean’s mists,
Thereupon receiving the title of Supreme Emperor.

The Supreme Perfected Lord of the Southern Culmen’s Compendium of Settled Records—
In the first year of the First August Emperor, the year *wushen*, on the seventh day of the seventh month at midday, within the Jeweled Grove beneath the Jasper Forest of the Purple Terrace in the Phoenix Capital of the Void, the Jade Realm of the Immeasurable Longevity Heaven above all heavens,
He bowed his head at the Jade Portico,
And the Void Sovereign Dao Lord proclaimed:
“The scripture for delivering life and reversing years is concealed above the Nine Heavens,
Within the Golden Terrace of the Grand Existence,
The Nine-Bend Chamber of the Jade Hall—
A path not traversed by median perfected ones.
This method shares a single root with the nine qi,
Its three luminaries revolving as one wheel.
Cultivate it ten thousand times,
And your rank shall ascend to that of Immortal Minister.”

The Grand Obscurity, the Grand Void, the Grand Origin—
The Primordial Beginning, the Primordial Inception,
The Great Unity, the Great Spirit.
Ascending to heaven, descending to earth,
Operating within the six directions,
Dispersed, they become qi;
Gathered, they form a mouth.
Coming and going without gate,
Exiting and entering without gap,
Arriving without movement,
Responding without call—
Thus is it called the entry of the spirit.

The Jade Casket of the Nine Shades—
From the *Statutes of Illuminating Perfection*.

The Eastern Limitless Flying Heavenly Divine King, Great Sage of Longevity—
The perfected ones of the ten directions all ride flying clouds and cinnabar chariots, green brush in hand,
Myriad millions of mounted riders arriving upon the void.

In the Fragrant Grove Garden—
For the enlightened youths, the mind of all methods is at ease,
The Five Refinements of the Numinous Treasure give life to the corpse.

The Azure Radiance Youth of the East—
Named Azure Supreme, styled Flying Upright,
His body the color of blue-green mist.

The Vermilion Radiance Youth of the South—
Named Cinnabar Splendor, styled Mystic Record,
His body the color of crimson mist.

The White Radiance Youth of the West—
Named Vast Florescence, styled Returning Spirit,
His body the color of pale mist.

The Black Radiance Youth of the North—
Named Mystic Brightness Supreme, styled Grand Yin,
His body inscribed, the color of black mist.

The Yellow Radiance Youth of the Center—
Named Holding the Cloth, styled Yellow Register,
His body the color of yellow mist,
Like the essence of yellow gold.

The *Scripture of the Golden Florescence Holding the Cavern Canon*—
Bearing incense, the perfected youths,
Whose whistling songs resound through the Mystic Capital,
Striking jade and sounding jasper bells.

The Golden Radiance Youth, the Lesser Wilderness Youth, the Primordial Inception Youth—
The recorded lineages of the Three Heavens of Highest Clarity.

The perverse cannot encroach upon the upright,
Evil cannot overcome virtue.

Those born of celestial purity and virtue—
Daoist priests of the Orthodox Unity,
Expounding the thousandfold statutes of the perfected.

Probing the profound, attaining the distant—
One may be styled Master of Mystic Stillness,
Or Master of Mystic Endeavor,
Or Master of Propagating the Dao,
Or Master of Expounding the Mysteries.

The Master of Mystic Antiquity—
The Supreme Dao Lord received his scriptures,
Transmitting them to the Immortal King of the Mystic Capital.

The Master of the Purple Mansion—
Three thousand years of age,
Roaming the cavern chambers.

The *Seventy-Four Methods of Highest Clarity Transformation*

The Primordial Inception Sovereign Master—
Adorned with phoenix-embroidered sashes, riding white clouds.

The Supreme August Master, Purple Dawn Lord—
Descended from the twin radiance, essence of the conjoined dawn,
Nurturing dragon mists in the great void,
Passing through the Purple Emptiness to commune with spirits,
Entrusted to the Nine Mysteries to contain luminous splendor,
Congealing vast numen to become divine,
Refining the Three Qi to purify himself,
Studying under the Mystic Mother to attain dharma-life.
Abiding through kalpas to receive transformation,
Responding to the auspicious solar day to bathe—
In the first year of the Supreme August era,
Heavenly Jia inaugurated the dawn,
Born in the Central City of the Eight Yangs of Divine Continent,
Upon the shores of the Cavernous Abyss.
His face emanated golden countenance,
His body reflected jade radiance,
Five-colored purple patterns,
Seventy-two transformations,
His essence illumined his jade visage.
Divine dragons disgorged mushrooms to anoint him,
Simurghs and phoenixes spread their wings to shade the mystic.
The Twin Effulgences paused their brilliance in the Eight Clarities,
The Seven Origins returned their essence to the Encompassing Dawn.
Golden immortals scattered incense to blend qi,
Divine consorts cast flowers to emit mist.
The Five Wefts wove their net,
Divine splendor suffused the purple heavens.
Cold rosy clouds swallowed qi,
Exhaling and inhaling numinous mist.
He received the title of Primordial August,
His position emanated from the Purple Dawn.
The Wei Immortals opened the path,
The Three Ways merged their light.
Flowing rosy clouds exhaled majesty,
His transcendent chariot soared through the Nine Mysteries.
Ascending the jade steps again,
Thrice he paid homage at the Purple Court,
Roaming and gazing upon the jasper towers,
Seeking the effulgence of the Three Origins.
Escorting the Five Elders,
He became an honored guest of the Jade Empyrean.
Golden lads raised clouds to attend his wheels,
Jade maidens trod the void to guard him.

The Five Marchmounts Master—
Received the dharma from the Perfected of the Supreme August,
With cinnabar tablets and ink-black seals.

The Heavenly Person, Supreme Person—
His name entered the Mystic Register of the Supreme August.

The Lesser Palace Master of the Dongting Immortal King—
A transcendent scholar,
Inhaling and exhaling mystic essence.

The Accomplished Scholar—
Disciplined by the mystic precepts, styled as such.

The Southern Marchmount Daoist—
Refining his po before ascending.

The Sacred Artisan—
Master of the mystic dharma.

Disciples of the Highest Study, Disciples of Middle Virtue—
Ten-Turned Disciples ascend as Flying Celestials.

Disciples of the Three Luminaries—
Having delivered two, they earn the title of Masters of the Three Luminaries’ Dharma.
In broad daylight they soar,
Riding flower-canopied chariots, mounting winged dragons,
Ascending the Great Ultimate, roaming the Nine Palaces.

*The Jade Characters of the Golden Tablets of the Grand Tenuity*—
Concealing the Three Lights, the sun sinks beneath the earth.

Those who achieve liberation through simulated death—
A lesser path of transcendence.
*The Flying Immortal’s Precious Sword of the Great Ultimate Perfected*—
Their names inscribed on the Purple Tablets,
The Three Offices unobstructed—this is called "liberation through the door."

Those of utmost loyalty and filial piety—
Receive the teachings of the Lesser Transcendents.

Those of utmost integrity and chastity—
Upon their passing, after two hundred and eighty years, they ascend one rank,
Filling the offices of the Immortal Bureaucracy.

Virtue is the origin of the ten thousand things—
A decree from Lord Lao.

The Four Virtues—
The gateway to practicing the Dao, the canon of attaining the Way.

Kings, marquises, and the highly noble—
With gold and treasures, they receive the true scriptures,
Copying and wearing the sacred texts.

The ancients achieved transcendence not through the heart alone;
In the degenerate age, one cannot cross over without wealth.
Ten thousand catties of gold, a single scripture of transcendence—
Bestowed upon the barren mountains of the degenerate age,
Would they consume gold or feast upon the scriptures?

The celestial regulations prescribe incense-burning at the six hours;
With the sun held in the heart’s contemplation,
Seeing the master is like encountering the scriptures after four hundred million kalpas—
True virtue and power are perfected.

Names inscribed in the Mystic Register—
Among the middle ranks of the Upper Transcendents,
Seven generations of ancestors ascend to carefree existence,
Their names recorded in the scriptures of the Seven Treasures.

The Primal Simplicity gives rise to the Five Viscera;
The Seven Numinous Spirits enter the Mud-Pill Palace.
The bones bear the jade radiance of the Five Thearchs,
The face shines with the flowing golden majesty.

Prostrating at the master’s gate—
Kowtowing to the characters of virtue and power.

The middle section of the Ink Register—
The wondrous scriptures of the Three Treasures,
The luminous regulations of the Four Poles.

The Golden Mouth of the Supreme August—
The central dharma of the four assemblies.

A pair of golden clasps, nine feet of azure silk—
On the eight seasonal days, present the scriptures at the Mystic Marchmount,
Facing north, memorialize the Azure Bureau to receive the precious scriptures.

Perfected officials, numinous functionaries,
Jade lads and jade maidens, perfected attendants—
Through sincere and secret resonance,
The heart communes with the Mystic Capital.

On the jiǎzǐ day, enter the chamber in purity after the dawn fast;
At midnight, when the generative qi stirs, recite the incantation:
"Supreme August Nine Numinous Spirits, Primordial Essence of the Three Luminaries,
Great Gods of the Immortal Capital, Three Purities of the Four Poles,
Eight Vows and Nine Unions—soar to the Jade Purity!"

The Dao is originally formless—
The Void and Primordial are spontaneous.

Masters in tens, hundreds, thousands, and myriad—
Those complete in attainment are the great vehicle’s adepts.
Clutching mugwort to ward off fire—
This speaks of lesser sincerity meeting calamity, as gods and humans admonish.

Amidst the love of throngs and kin, the heart abides in the treasury of Daoist precepts;
Amidst the heart of woe and peril, it dwells in the hall of benevolent salvation.
Seated in the land of vipers and adders, the mind contemplates the path of renunciation and distance;
Dwelling in the lair of tigers and leopards, the heart rests in the temple of fortune and virtue.

The Great Void, the Great Origin, the Great Emptiness—
These are the roots of precepts.
Discarding wealth to dispel stagnation, saving beings to perfect compassion.

**Essential Precepts**
The *Essential Precepts of Laozi’s Eternal Abiding*—
Once the precepts are upheld, one becomes a person of the Dao and virtue for life,
Ascending to supplement the ranks of immortal officials.

Receiving the Three Precepts and Five Precepts,
Refining ignorance into wisdom, riding the boat of deathlessness.

**Nine Vermilion Talismans**
Also called the *Nine Talismans of the White Feather Central Grove’s Flying Immortals*—
They are the qi of the Nine Origins,
Celestial script of soaring mystery and feathered splendor,
Woven into jade texts.
To obtain and wear the true talismans:
Command the Nine Vermilions to seal the mounds,
Summon the Five Agents to invoke the spirits.
Meditate on the Water Emperor to erase transgressions,
Gather the sea’s numina to open the source.

**Erasure of Sin and Inscription of Life**
The ledgers of sin are obliterated in the Nine Treasuries,
The records of life are engraved in the Three Clarities.
Qi shakes the vast expanse, its might subduing the ten thousand spirits,
Wielding the tally of the Six Jias to command the celestial soldiers.

From the *Inner True Scripture of the Five Emperors*:
The *Primordial Five Elders’ Three Origins Jade Talismans*—
Issued from the Purple Tenuity Palace of Jade Capital Mountain,
This script shares the primal qi of the Three Heavens,
Averting the calamities of nine hundred and six kalpas at the Yang convergence.
To wear it is to ascend in broad daylight,
To ascend and pay court at the Dark Metropolis.

*The Numinous Treasure Vermilion Script*
The Duke of Ninefold Completion—
Nine feet in stature, with round eyes and a square mouth,
His voice like thunder, a purple radiance crowning his head,
Twenty-four handmaidens attending him on either side,
The Duke clad in a nine-colored, speckled fur robe.
In the reign of Emperor Wen of Han,
The Duke rode a flying phoenix and cloud-wheel to the Whitewater Sands and the Hollow Mountain,
Where he answered Pei Xuanren, saying:
“Yesterday I saw in the Azure Florescence a memorial bearing your jade name,
Marking you as a candidate for the Azure Bureau of the Pure Numinous Perfected.
This is no idle matter.
Your jade splendor and mystic elegance are inscribed in the Azure Register.
I received from the Primordial Beginning the *Jade Talisman of the Precious True Scripture for Deliverance from Tribulation*;
To wear it is to attain transcendence and command five Jade Lads of the Grand Mystery.
Once a century, a perfected one is permitted to transmit this scripture.”

*The Twenty-Four Transmissions of the Seven Thousand Kalpas*—
This talisman coeval with the Nine Heavens,
Coexisting with sun and moon,
Unscathed by a hundred blades,
Vigorous even at ten thousand years.
After nine years of preparation, the body emits wondrous radiance.

*The Yellow Register of the Supreme Five Emperors*
The Five Talismans—
On the first day of the latter half of the month, in vermilion ink inscribe:
The *Spontaneously Replete Jade Treasure Talisman of the Celestial Vacuity Primordial Beginning Perfected One*,
The *Ninefold Mystery Jade Talisman of the Primordial Celestial Jade Vacuity’s Congealed Essence*,
The *True Talisman of the Numinous Treasure Congealed from the Jade Essence of the Grand Vacuity Nine Heavens Perfected One*,
The *Precious Transcendent Talisman of the Spontaneously Flowing Essence of the Jade Eye of the Nine Heavens True Perfected One*,
The *Primordial Talisman of the Nine Heavens’ Nine Fathers’ Guiding Essence for Celestial Communication through the Vacuous Fusion*.
Face heaven and ingest them.
After ten days, the countenance will glow with five-colored essence-light;
After nine days, one may command five Jade Maidens of the Five Emperors, one for each.
After nine years, ascend to the Great Clarity as an immortal official of the Five Marchmounts.

*The Golden Chamber Lifeguarding Talisman*
Recite the scripture ten times to complete one cycle,
Then ingest one talisman.
This enables communion with the true, sitting and perceiving the eight directions,
Ordering the hundred joints,
Living as long as heaven and earth,
And sharing the lifespan of the Three Luminaries.

*The Nine Heavens’ Grand Simplicity Yang-Generating Talisman*

**The Ancient Register of the Mysterious Capital Purple Tenuity Palace**, also called *The Eight Dragon Script*. *The Numinous Treasure Vermilion Writ* for "Opening the Heart and Dispelling Delusion" is to be inscribed in cinnabar on an auspicious day and ingested. The incantation reads:

*"Five spirits open the heart,
Three souls gather essence."*

Master Han Zhong of the Nine Doubts received this scripture from Song Dexuan of Mount Song. Dexuan, having ingested the *Six Jia Spirit-Flight Talisman*, could traverse over three thousand *li* in a single day.

**The Four Transformative Talismans**
In spring, ingest the *Eastern Brilliance Communion-with-the-True Transformative Radiant Yang Mist Talisman*;
In summer, ingest the *Southern Radiance Eightfold-Refinement Elixir Transformative Fourfold Clarity Talisman*;
In autumn, ingest the *Western Essence Vast-Spirit Transformative Radiance Talisman*;
In winter, ingest the *Northern Mystery Profound-True Refinement Transformative Whistling Wind Talisman*.

To practice the Way of the Yellow Emperor, ingest the *Yellow Supreme Eight Scriptures Life-Radiance Jade Gate Talisman* on the days of the *li* months.

**Eastern Brilliance Communion-with-the-True Talisman**
The essence of the Eastern Azure Radiant Yang Mist, *Opening Brilliance and Communing with Light*, is the primal glow of the origin’s dawn, illuminating the Eastern Heaven. It surges through ninety-nine myriad million layers, where flocks of jade-green fowl perch in verdant groves. Above lies the *Origin Azure* abode; within stands the *Azure Splendor* palace. The abode is graced by the *Nine Qi Primordial Elders*; the palace houses the *Azure Perfected Sage Lords*. To their right attend the *Azure Waist Jade Maidens*; to their left, the *Kingfisher-Feather Divine Lads*. They ever ride the sacred beasts of Mount Tai, driving and guiding the nine-light divine dragons. In the third month of spring, they descend to guide the qi of the Nine Heavens, congealing qi into names and condensing essence into talismans. He who swallows this qi may instantly establish a divine body; he who cools this essence may transform into ninefold radiance—its wonders defy full description.

**Southern Radiance Eightfold-Refinement Talisman**
The essence of the Southern *Fourfold Clarity* is the primal glow of the eight heavens’ trigrams, scattering through eighty-eight myriad million layers like flourishing auspicious clouds, resplendent in the court of the *Great Mystery*. Jade nectar cascades in the land of flowing fire, where the *Great Yang* holds the *Gushing Mouth* cavern, and the *Flowing Fire* abounds with deathless ones. Above stands the *Southern Culmen* terrace; within lies the *Cavern Yang* palace. The terrace is governed by the *Controller of Immortals and Life Mandates*; the palace contains the *Supreme Harmony Perfected*. To their right attend the *Great Perfected Jade Maidens*; to their left, the *Vermilion Brilliance Divine Lads*. They ever ride the sacred beasts of Mount Huo, driving and guiding the nine-colored phoenixes. In the third month of summer, they ascend to guide the qi of the Nine Heavens and descend to draw the brilliance of the *Crimson Palace*. The two qi intersect in responsive transformation, their changes emerging from subtle glimmers. Essence condenses into script; qi congeals into stars. He who swallows this qi will have numinous lords descend to his chamber; he who cools this essence may soar through the eight voids, command the *Six Jia*, and dispatch the *Six Ding*.

**Western Essence Vast-Spirit Transformative Radiance Supportive Talisman**
Its script is the essence-qi of the Western *Vast-Spirit Metal Soul Sun Gate*, the primal glow of the sixfold golden radiance. Brightly it illumines the Western Rong, vast and flowing through sixty-six myriad million layers. Its essence falls like jade, driving light and streaming luster, pouring into the *Smelting Refinement* court. There lies the *Returning Countenance* pool, the *Refined Immortal* gem, and the *Gold Gate* with its azure-gold cinnabar. Above stands the *Dragon Mountain* divine tower; within lies the *Plain Spirit* palace. The tower is graced by the *Twelve King Immortals*; the palace shelters the *Western Florescence Perfected*. To their right attend the *Plain Spirit Jade Maidens*; to their left, the *Gold Florescence Lads*. They ever ride the sacred beasts of Mount Che, driving and guiding the *White Emperor’s* kings. In the third month of autumn, they ascend to guide the qi of the Nine Heavens. The two qi respond and intersect, congealing essence into talismans and condensing qi into spirits. He who swallows this qi will instantly summon a divine countenance; he who cools this essence may soar through the *Gold Gate*, sit and summon the ten directions, and summon clouds to bring forth dragons.

**Northern Mystery Refinement Transformative Talisman**
The essence of the Northern *Profound-True Whistling Wind Florescence Dawn* is the primal glow of the opening of yin and yang. Its radiance is chaotic, now merging, now parting, scattering and flowing through fifty-five myriad million layers. Its essence is profoundly interwoven, like the dark clouds’ distant smoke merging with blossoms yet unshining. It engenders the five phases and establishes the *Mysterious Beginning*, where yin generates the *Refined Immortal Jade Paste* and the *Cold Water* holds the *Demon-Quelling King*. Above stands the *Sevenfold Divine Flower Canopy*; within lies the *Crossing Spirit* hall, which shelters the *August Jade Dawn*. To their right attend the *Great Mystery Jade Maidens*; to their left, the *Jade Dawn Lads*. They ever ride the sacred beasts of Mount Da, driving and guiding the flying tortoises and purple wheels. In the third month of winter, they ascend to guide the qi of the Nine Heavens, congealing essence into script and condensing qi into immortals. He who swallows this qi will have the *Seven Dawns* descend to his chamber; he who ingests this essence may reverse and transform yin and yang. Such are the wonders of the *August Numinous Script*.

**Yellow Supreme Eight Scriptures Talisman**
The essence of the *Central Yellow Supreme Divine Mother Jade Gate Life-Radiance Communing Brilliance* is the primal glow of heaven and earth’s warp and woof, the twelve celestial stems. It illumines the eight directions, its mist wafting and scattering, its light brilliant and merging with the void. It surges and rises in the capital of the *Great Mystery*, threading through twelve myriad million layers, its flowing nectar overflowing in the land of the four seasons. Above stands the *Royal Capital* palace; within lies the *Leather Canopy* palace. The former is governed by the *Supreme Dao Lord*; the latter contains the *Wood Dawn Lord*. To their left attend the *Flying Immortals with Feathered Staffs* and the *Azure Florescence Jade Maidens*; to their right, the *Commanding Immortal Jade Gentlemen* and the *Golden Bell Divine Lads*. They ever ride the sacred beasts of the *Nine Wastes*, driving and guiding the *Yellow Supreme* dragons. They gather the five qi to revolve the celestial stems, commanding the twelve *Polar Arrays*, ascending to guide the source and flow of the Nine Heavens, and descending to draw the yellow spirit of the spleen. The two qi intersect above the *Muddy Pellet*, refining and transforming in the chamber of the *Three Cinnabar Fields*. Essence congeals to transform spirits; qi condenses to refine immortals. He who swallows this qi will have the *Yellow Elder* descend in form; he who cools this essence will radiate the color of *vajra*. Myriad marvels transform, and one may soar through the Great Void. The wondrous efficacy of this numinous script defies measure.

Virtue is the father;
Spiritual illumination, the mother.
Purity and quiescence, the teacher;
Supreme harmony, the friend.
The horse and tiger are dragons,
And one becomes coeval with heaven and earth.
To be mysterious and silent
Is to exhaust the Dao.
Without goodness, one does not act;
Without harmony, one does not speak.

Thus, those who do good awaken of themselves; those who commit evil punish themselves. A heart upright knows no doubt; a heart pure bears no defilement. The Most High August Emperor refines the Supreme Perfected through ninefold refinement.

The mouth and tongue are the palace of calamity, the mansion of peril and ruin. Speech is the repository of great destiny, the domain of punishment and misfortune. When the sage speaks, he fears that his words may stray from the wondrous truth. Though literary eloquence fills heaven and earth, when the worthy and sagely speak—

To a lord, their words bring grace to the state;
To a father, kindness to his child;
To a teacher, love to the multitude;
To brothers, fraternal conduct in action;
To a minister, loyalty to his sovereign;
To a ruler, filial piety to his parents;
To a friend, trust in their bond;
To a wife, chastity to her husband;
To a husband, harmony in the household;
To a younger sibling, reverence in ritual;
To a rustic, encouragement in farming;
To a Daoist, rectitude in the Dao;
To one of a foreign land, each guards their own realm;
To servants and maids, caution in their duties.

The Dark Lord of the Northern Cavern, the Solitary and Uttermost, the Five Numinous Ones, the Mysterious Elder—his surname is Hao, his style Fuming. Scion of the Mysterious August, descendant of the Grand Clarity, at the age of twelve in the midst of the Azure Heaven, his heart delighted in mountains and waters. After a thousand days he returned, and beneath the Mirror Mountain he encountered a field of lettuce. He gathered it to relieve the destitute, yet after three years his task remained unfinished, and he perished at the mountain’s foot. The Nine Heavens inscribed his yang virtue; the golden tablets recorded his jade name. His ethereal soul was conveyed to the Palace of Vermilion Clarity, where the Emperor dispatched the Golden-Winged Great Roc to spread its mighty wings over his corpse. Seven hundred years passed until the water kalpa altered the cosmic tide, and his remains drifted into boundless depths. When the waters receded, they came to rest upon the Northern Black Mound. Thirty years later, a great mountain fire raged, and he was refined in its flames before rising again, a five-colored cloud canopy above him. The Primordial Beginning bestowed upon him the *Lingbao Crimson Writ of the Five Qi of the Mysterious Heaven*, the true scripture of the Black Emperor of the North.

Some sold themselves to sustain the Dharma; some cast themselves before hungry tigers; some carved their flesh to feed the birds. Their utmost sincerity moved the Great Void; their hidden virtue harmonized with the Three Luminaries. The Most High’s *Ninefold Crimson Seals of the Five Thearchs’ Inner Perfected*.

Unmatched diligence, no peer in devotion; the forests and peaks, the Dharma-wheel. Kindly opening expedient means, great compassion pervades all. Dispelling greed and lust, calming wrath and affliction, eradicating perverse folly, extinguishing the three poisons—these four deeds are the forerunners of the Six Perfections.

Men and women each contend in their intentions; four horses pass like a crack in the wall—yet even this is slow. Compared to them, the fleeting question of a cloud is swift as lightning, yet neither matches the speed of thought. To master the heart is more difficult than taming tigers and leopards. Apes, monkeys, deer, and horses are all easily controlled. Only the supremely sagely can truly govern the heart.

Rectify the spirits, rectify the heart; rectify conduct, rectify the body. Heavenly spirits revere them; earthly spirits guard them. The discipline of cultivating the heart and entering the Dao unfolds in myriad branches. From beginning to end, steadfast in integrity, they guide in hidden transformation; in advance and retreat, harmonizing their light, they teach in secret practice. Eating but once at midday, they maintain purity in their person. Even gold must not be defiled—how much more the Supreme Dao!

The Three Wondrous Treasure Texts of the Supreme Nine Perfected Luminous Regulations.

Place a vessel of pure water, and two fen of true pearls. Write the Luminous Talisman of Penetrating Clarity and place it in the water, exposing it in the central courtyard for one night. Hold the water facing north, knock the teeth three times, and recite the incantation:

*"The radiance of heaven is veiled by vapors,
The five spirits are mingled with the true.
Cinnabar numina are all disordered,
Impure qi fills the sky.
Today, pure and auspicious,
Cease misfortune and reveal good fortune.
Three parts adorn and reflect,
Five mushrooms wash away dust.
The eight qi penetrate brightly,
Interweaving through my body.
Above, white; below, yellow—
Within and without, luminous and fresh."*

Wash the hands and face with the water; it may also be used for bathing. Pour the remaining water into an eastward-flowing stream. All impurities will dissolve, the myriad perfected will abide in the body, and even after three transgressions, one remains unstained—thus cultivating the Dao of the Three Heavens.

*Oral Instructions of the Azure Lad:*
In the realm of the living, purity is scarce and turbidity abundant; one should wear the tattered talisman. The qi of the Nine Heavens transforms into nine phoenixes, each guarding the body, soaring through the Three Realms, drawing the wondrous qi of the Three Clarities, and sweeping away the dust and clamor of the Nine Lands.

The *Supreme Azure Prime Upper Record* states:
*"Bathe with five fragrances at the three times."*

On the fifteenth day of the first, seventh, and tenth months, as well as on ordinary days at dawn, noon, and midnight:

*Qingmu* (cypress) leaves are divided into five segments, each fivefold in structure. The people of Tianzhu (India) say: the five fragrant herbs repel malign qi, stabilize the hun and po souls, subdue demonic entities, and summon numinous perfected beings. This herb grows abundantly east of the Canglang River, where the divine beings of the East each transform into *qingmu* incense.

When one burns *qingmu*, *xunlu* (frankincense), and *anxi* resin in the bedchamber, it dispels the foulness of the Five Turbidities and the demonic qi of the earth, which would otherwise rise straight up to the heavens for forty *li*. The smoke of this incense shatters the filth of turbid qi and parts the mists of evil demons. Heavenly beings and jade maidens, the Supreme Unity Emperor Lord, follow the fragrant vapors to rest upon one’s face and form.

Scholars of the highest learning ingest the radiance of the sun and moon, the flying roots of golden essence. The Way of the Yellow Qi: on the morning of *Lichun* (Beginning of Spring), boil *baizhi* (angelica), peach bark, and *qingmu*, then bathe facing east. On *jiazi* days, one should bathe.

*The Precious Divine Daily Record of the Queen Mother of the West* states:
On the first, fifteenth, and twenty-third days of each month, draw water from three rivers (or three wells, as some say). Measure the water in a *hu* vessel, then boil one *liang* each of *jishe* (clove), *qingmu*, *lingling* (lemongrass), *xunlu*, and *chenxiang* (aloeswood). Inscribe the *Tongming* talisman upon the water and use it for bathing. First, face east and knock the teeth twenty-four times, visualizing the Seven Stars above the nape, a canopy of purple mist filling the room, divine youths scattering incense to the left, and jade maidens holding towels to the right. Upon completion, recite the incantation:

*"The Three Luminaries shine brightly,
The Five Spirits become serene.
The heavens bear no floating haze,
The earth stirs no flying dust.
Bathe in the Eastern Well,
Receive and reverse your form.
Body fragrant, bones aromatic,
Ascend to the Jade Court.
Having received the Supreme Perfected,
Cast the talisman into the well."*

This is the supreme method of imperial bathing, transmitted from the Celestial King of Primordial Beginning to the Heavenly Emperor of Unity. Through cultivation, the Emperor Lord attained flowing purple radiance to crown his imperial form. The Supreme Prime Lord of the Southern Culmen refined it to emit an upper fragrance heard across the Three Clarities. The Celestial Emperor of the Grand Tenuity cultivated it, and the divine mushrooms of the Five Directions gathered in his chamber. The Golden Gate Lord of the Supreme Sages developed a royal glow upon his face. The Prime Minister Azure Lad refined it, and his fragrance suffused the Three Clarities. This secret Way resides within the Purple Chamber of the Southern Culmen.

Bathing in the Orchid Pool above,
Dragons bear the long-handled vase.
Golden youths scatter fragrant blossoms,
Jade maidens stream the Five Stars.
Crown and sash washed in jade nectar,
Refining and transcending the Five Immortals’ forms.
Body fragrant, myriad spirits descend,
Riding the light to ascend the lofty clarity.

Bathe at the Golden Gate,
Crown and sash aglow with divine radiance.
The Jade Void seals the talisman,
All immortals converge in return.
Heavenly officials and their retinues
Feast and wander the Three Clarities, ascending the Dark Peak.

The Supreme Unity Emperor Lord regards the Purple Chamber as the Primordial Father and Mysterious Mother, the Three Wombs as divine luminaries. The Eight Pure Ones adorn the Mysterious, with true contemplation as their foremost; the esoteric words and wondrous essentials are the *Inner Canon of the Nine Perfected*. The divine method takes pure thought as its deepest core, and the youthful adept takes thorough realization as attaining the numinous.
