The *Great Cavern* takes the exalted as its origin, the *Great Elixir* takes the Feminine One as its inner essence, the Five Elders take spontaneity as their morning bones, the Supreme Lord takes the Non-Beflowered as the Mysterious Clarity, the Yellow Venerable takes will and nature as the root of the Dao, the White Prime takes immaculate cultivation as entry into the real, perfected beings take qi-convergence as mutual refinement, and the essentials of immortality take essence-response as the completion of the Dao.

*Jingzi* (Essence Son), *Chengzi* (Sincerity Son), *Shenrongzi* (Spirit Glory Son), *Zhongzi* (Central Son), *Hezi* (Harmony Son), *Daonaihuazi* (Dao-Transforming Son):
Sincerity is the gateway of the spirit. It accomplishes what cannot be accomplished, guards what cannot be guarded. Ascending the Mysterious—there is being in non-being, non-being in non-non-being. Neither being nor non-being, it circulates through the Nine Extremes. Proceeding without cease, contemplating without weariness.

The five viscera within the body correspond to the Five Peaks. Learning is like the midday sun—before study, all is dark and obscure; this is the first stage of enlightenment. In learning, one must be precise and cannot be unclear, then one may fathom the wonders of the Three Clarities. Confine a thousand evils in the prison of the Eight Wastes, seal ten thousand demons at the ends of the Nine Distances. When the heart is upright, heaven and earth cannot oppose it. Constantly guard the Nine Hun souls to seek flying immortality.

The Great Unity abides peacefully in the Six Dwellings,
The Five Numinous Ones guard the Three Mouths.
The Three Officials refine and harmonize,
The five viscera are at peace and inquire no further.
Secure them with divine medicines,
Nourish the cloud-body.

What scholars cannot learn,
Where others cannot dwell—
the true and spontaneous One.
A tree of arm-spanning girth grows from a hair’s tip;
The smoke of ascending clouds arises from a spark’s flame.

*The Regulations of the Supreme Perfected*:
Evil accumulates and leads to death—
the suffering of death is lamentable.
Good accumulates and leads to long life—
the joy of life is cause for celebration.
Accomplish three thousand merits to ascend to heaven in broad daylight.
Accomplish three hundred good deeds to attain earthly immortality.
To learn the Way of ascending as an immortal, one must perform six thousand two hundred good deeds.
With surplus in cultivation,
Heaven sends a cloud chariot.
Those who magnify the Dao do not perish,
Attaining deathlessness by their own efforts.

The Way of Great Compassion
Takes saving others as its priority.
Without merit, there is no reward;
Without virtue, no promotion;
Without trust, no salvation;
Without practice, no immortality.
Those who establish merit and virtue
Do so for heaven and earth,
For the Three Luminaries,
For the emperor,
For the myriad people,
For ancestral generations,
For all beings,
And for themselves.

Exhale and inhale primordial harmony,
Sip and rinse with flowing rosy clouds.
The essence of the Five Flowers—
the question of the Immortal Duke.

The *Mysterious Record of Immortal Bones* inscribes names in the Golden Pavilion and Jade Register. Those who, in past lives, accumulated five hundred good deeds and fulfilled them all may attain the Three Ones.

On the Eight Auspicious Days,
They pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy,
Offering high vows to ascend the heavens,
Transcend the Jade Pure River,
And wander through the myriad heavens;
Middle vows to transform their forms,
Summon the Five Spirits,
And ascend through the Moon Gate;
Low vows that the Four Poles receive their oral commands,
The Western Florescence attend as guards,
Command golden lads,
Lead the Five Elders,
The Eight Sceneries share the same chariot,
The Upper Celebrations converge,
And the Five Vows unfold in full.

In paying homage to the celestial patterns,
There are eleven contemplations,
Fourteen merits,
And true persons who serve as bridges for the world.

The *Secret Scripture* in the Palace of Great Existence above the Nine Heavens—
Fierce dragons and venomous beasts guard the Jade Pass,
Jasper phoenixes spread their wings,
Girdled simurghs shade the mysteries,
Hosts of perfected ones feast in reverence,
Myriad sages pay homage in chariots,
Jade steps and canopies extend into the celestial court,
The Great Emperor humbles himself before the throne.

Golden perfection and jade radiance—
At dawn, sunset, midnight, and the quiet of night,
They pay reverence to the Heavenly Worthies of the Ten Directions, beginning with the East.

The *Scripture of the Numinous Treasure’s Spontaneous Dao* is inscribed in cinnabar and gold on the Terrace of Purple Tenuity. Daily, the perfected immortals and sages circumambulate it thrice, burning incense.

Those who receive and practice the *Supreme Mystery of the Cavernous Profound Scripture* follow the highest instructions. Thrice a month, they seclude themselves to pay homage to the Heavenly Worthy of Primordial Beginning, the Supreme Perfected Venerable, and the True Kings of the Nine Heavens. On those days, they bathe, enter the chamber, burn incense facing north, and kneel to say: *"I beseech the divine immortals to inscribe my name in the Jade Register."*

Bones grow marrow, flesh transforms into golden perfection.
The cinnabar chamber is infused with mystery, and purple mist arises within.
When finished, they rise and bow twice.
After seven years of cultivation, the true spirits manifest in form.
Golden bones and jade names are engraved in the Azure Palace.
After a thousand days of fasting,
Uninvolved in worldly affairs,
They hold fast to purity, incense, and precepts.
Unsullied by the dust of the world,
Serene in the six practices,
With hearts gentle and intentions profound,
Their names are inscribed in the Golden Canon,
Listed in the Nine Heavens.

Those who receive the *Thirty-Nine Chapters of the Great Cavern Scripture* from the Supreme Dao Lord of the Great Dao
Master the Eight Winds of Jade Revitalization and wander the path of the Imperial Unity.

On Mount Shu, a thousand-year-old tree spirit
Encountered three worthy men passing by who rested beneath its branches.
From within the hollow tree, a voice spoke: *"In past lives, my merits were incomplete, so I remain bound to this tree. I entreat you to visit my home and hold a three-day fast for me."*
The household then invited Daoist masters to burn incense, recite scriptures, and perform rites of repentance for three days.
Thereupon, the spirit ascended into the clouds, becoming a wandering immortal in the Radiant Empyrean, embodying the original conduct of the free-roaming immortals.
Their bodies fragrant and pure, now like gold and jade.

When the Three Primes unfold,
Their virtue crowns the heavens.
Virtue like the Great Void—
Formless and boundless, the origin of Primordial Beginning.
Virtue like the Great Dao—
Majestic and expansive, the treasure of divine luminosity.
Their virtue like heaven and earth,
Like the Three Luminaries, illuminating all heavens;
Like the four seasons, nurturing the myriad beings;
Like the Great Mystery, the capital of immortals;
Like Mount Tai, stabilizing spirits and anchoring numina;
Like the Great River, vast and unobstructed.

The Three Luminaries honor such noble conduct.
Each year holds six fasts.

On one’s natal day, the Gengshen day, and the Jiazi day, the Most High dispatches Perfected Ones, the sages of the ten directions, and immortals to descend upon the Three Realms below, while all ghosts and spirits likewise descend. The numina of heaven and earth tremble in reverence. Those who practice the Dao, recite scriptures, and in the six periods of day and night focus their minds upon the Perfected—such devotees shall have their lifespans extended by the Director of Destinies, be spared the Ten Sufferings and Eight Calamities, and ever dwell in blessed lands, while their seven generations of ancestors ascend to the Heavenly Halls.

In former times, the Most High transmitted the Six Fasts of the Three Annual Fasts to the Perfected One of the Stone Chamber, the Ten Methods of the Sixth Month to the Heavenly Elder Perfected One, and commanded the Perfected One of Emptiness and Nonbeing, Laozi, to transmit the Orthodox Unity teachings to the Three Heavens Master of the Correct One.

On the fifteenth day of the first month (Upper Prime), the fifteenth day of the seventh month (Middle Prime), and the fifteenth day of the tenth month (Lower Prime)—these three days of the year, along with the third day of the third month—when the Five Emperors of Earth, the Five Marchmounts, the officials of the Three Realms, and all the numina of the water palaces ascend to the Two Prime Offices of the Mysterious Capital in the Three Heavens, the Heavenly Worthy of the Boundless, the Thirty-Two Heavenly Emperors, the Flying Heavenly Kings, the Supreme Jade Void Perfected Great Spirits, the Lord of the Boundless Dao and Most High, the Venerable Ones, the Southern and Northern Poles, the Eastern and Western Unitary Flowers, the Ninefold Numinous True Mothers, the Jade Maidens of Grand Harmony, the Southern and Northern Dippers, and the constellations of the heavens—all assemble in solemn array. The officials of the Three Primes, left, right, and center, the Three Offices and Nine Bureaus, the One Hundred Ten Departments, the yin-yang officials of water, fire, wind, and the blade, and the examiners of merit—all tally the good deeds of heaven and earth, inscribing the virtuous in the Azure Register and the transgressors in the Black Register, each report submitted to the Three Offices. Those who follow the Three Primes’ rites of repentance shall have the earth spirits guard their gates, and the Three Offices shall protect and recommend them.

The Supreme Cavern-Real Three Nonbeing Fasts:
Upper Prime governs Heaven, Middle Prime governs Earth, Lower Prime governs Humanity.
The Three Primes unite in perfection, corresponding above to the Nine Mysteries.
Upper Prime lasts nine days, Middle Prime six days, Lower Prime three days.
On the day before the fast begins, bathe with five fragrances—from nine persons of the Upper Mystery to three of the Lower Limit.
On the day of the fast, inscribe the Golden Perfected and Jade Radiance tokens of the Nine Heavens and place them before the Five Emperors to summon the spirits and invoke the numinous.

The *Three Primes Three Grades Fast Method of the Great Perfected* records that the Five Venerable Elder Spirits and the Heavenly Emperor-Kings customarily gather on the Six Fast Days at the Mysterious Capital’s Primordial Yang Purple Tenuity Terrace in the Upper Heavens, where they tally the celestial reckonings and examine the movements of destiny. The Heavenly Emperors, the Great Ones of the heavens, the envoys of the sun, moon, and stars, the Three Offices’ examiners of destiny, and the great spirits of the Five Marchmounts and Four Watercourses traverse the world below, scrutinizing merits and transgressions. Those who cultivate the fasts shall have their merits recorded by the Three Offices and Five Emperors, their names inscribed in the heavens. Below, they may pay homage to the Most High, and their seven generations of ancestors shall all ascend to the Halls of Blessing.

On the seventh day of the first month, the Fast of All Heavens is observed. Inscribe names on yellow su tablets, erasing death and restoring life. The Great Sage of the Primordial Numinous Treasure of the Northwest Heavens, the assembly of perfected and venerable spirits, and the Venerable Elder of the Limitless Dao’s Imperial True Sovereign gather on the first day at the Numinous Treasure’s Mysterious Capital, the Purple Tenuity Terrace of the Northwest Mountain in the Upper Heavens. They command the Northern Dipper to descend with the Three Offices to assess ranks and expose deceit across the world below. Those who uphold the fast shall have their transgressions absolved by the Three Offices.

The Great Sage of the Northern Heavens and the Most High Lord Lao gather on the eighth day at the Numinous Treasure’s Mysterious Capital, the Yin Primordial Terrace of the Jade Mountain above. They urge the Northern Dipper’s Controller of Demon-Slaying to descend with the Eight Poles’ Registrars, traversing the world below. On this day, those who observe the fast shall have their transgressions erased by the Three Offices, their names recorded in the Three Heavens, inscribed in the Registers of Immortals. Heaven and earth’s spirits shall guard and protect them, and the myriad calamities shall not afflict them.

The Sage of the Northeast Heavens, the assembly of the Most High’s myriad transformations and myriad births, the Divine Sovereign of the Upper Mystery, and the Venerable Elder of the Primordial gather on the fourteenth day at the Mysterious Capital’s Jade Mountain, the Azure Tenuity Terrace of Penetrating Yang. They command the Great One’s envoys and the Northern Dengdu’s lords to traverse the world below, overseeing the affairs of humans and spirits. Those who cultivate the fast and establish virtue shall have their names inscribed in the Nine Heavens and matched to the immortal registers.

The Great Sage of the Eastern Heavens, the assembly of the Supreme Clarity’s Primordial Limitless Three Heavens’ Great Dao, the Most High Lord Lao, the Azure Numinous Perfected Sovereign of the Upper Heavens, the Great Emperor, the Nine Elders of the Immortal Metropolis, the Nine Qi Venerable, and the twelve hundred official lords, the Jade Sovereign beneath the Supreme Clarity, the Elder of the Eastern Limit, the Azure Radiance Great Spirit, the Prime Minister Sima, the Azure Youth of the Golden Watchtower’s Posterior Sage Emperor, the Nine Immortals of the Numinous Treasure, the Azure Harmony Jade Maidens, and the Jade Gentlemen of the Immortal Host gather on the fifteenth day at the Supreme Mystery’s Capital, the Azure Radiance Jade Terrace of the Jade Maidens. The Heavenly Emperor descends, along with the sun, moon, and stars, the spirits of the heavens above and below, the Five Marchmounts and Four Watercourses, and the attendant dragons. Those who cultivate the fast shall be protected and recommended by the Five Emperors’ divine guardians.

The Great Sage of the Southeast Heavens, the assembly of the Southern Upper Venerable Lords, the Cinnabar Sage of the Southern Culmen, the Perfected of the Southern Culmen, and the Jade Maidens of Grand Harmony gather on the eighteenth day at the Cinnabar Terrace of the Grotto Spirit on Jade Mountain. On this day, burning incense and practicing the Dao, the myriad wishes shall be fulfilled as the heart desires.

The Great Sage of the Southern Heavens, the assembly of the Southern Upper Crimson Emperor, the Cinnabar Numinous Venerable Lao, the Southern Culmen’s Deliverer from the World, and the Lord of Myriad Blessings gather on the twentieth day at the Primordial Yang Lodge of the Grotto Spirit on Jade Mountain. They command the Great One’s envoys and the Three Offices’ examiners to traverse the world below, observing and inspecting the affairs of heaven and humanity. On this day, reciting scriptures and burning incense, the Earth Office’s spirits shall guard and protect.

The Great Sage of the Southwest Heavens, the assembly of the Heavenly Humans, the Venerable Elder, the Southern Culmen’s Primordial Perfected Lord, and the Supreme Numinous of the Grotto Yang gather on the twenty-fourth day at the Vermilion Palace of the Jade Capital to review the Three Offices, the Nine Bureaus, the Five Marchmounts, Mount Tai’s twenty-four prisons. They command the Northern Asterism to descend with the Three Offices’ examiners, the Water Department’s exposers of deceit, traversing the world below.

The Great Sage of the Western Heavens, the Golden Hall’s Jade Immortal True Mother of the Western Florescence, the Posterior Watchtower’s Golden Watchtower Posterior Sage Prime Minister Emperor, and the Four Culmens’ Perfected gather on the twenty-eighth day at the Golden Watchtower’s Seven Treasures Palace of the Jade Capital. The Great One descends, the Armillary Sphere and Jade Balance observe together, all descending through the Celestial Pass Gate.

The Great Sage of the Lower Heavens, the assembly of the Lower Primordial’s Profound Abyss’ myriad immortals, the Five Emperors and Four Controllers’ Perfected gather on the twenty-ninth day at the Yellow Heaven’s Jade Pass, the Yellow Chamber within. The Great One and the Three Offices’ Nine Bureaus and Nine Departments’ exposers of deceit traverse the Five Marchmounts.

The Great Sage of the Upper Heavens, the assembly of the Most High of the Upper and Lower, Central, Four Directions, and Eight Quarters, the Venerable Lords of the Effortless Great Dao, the primordial qi of the Dao, boundless and without origin, formless and chaotic, empty and spontaneous—within the Dao, the luminous sovereigns of spirit and clarity, the myriad myriad billions upon billions, the countless hosts, the Venerable Lords of virtue and power, the celestial officials and great spirits of the immortals gather on the thirtieth day at the Seven Treasures’ Purple Tenuity Palace to pay homage to the myriad true emperors of heaven. They tally the great kalpas and the lesser kalpas of the hundred and six. On this day, they dispatch the Upper Great One to descend among them, the stars and constellations of the heavens, the sun and moon, the Armillary Sphere and Northern Dipper all descending with the Five Emperors, the Five Marchmounts and Four Watercourses, the Water Emperor’s examiners, and the earth’s spirits to traverse the world below. Those who cultivate the fast on this day shall have their names inscribed in the Registers of Upper Immortals.

The Supreme Mystery’s Upper Palace’s Northern Emperor on the day of Gengshen governs the rectification of the Three Corpses of Heaven, recording human transgressions and submitting them to the Imperial Lord. Those who cultivate the fast on this day shall have their names inscribed on the Azure Contract.

The Supreme Mystery’s Upper Palace’s Perfected and Venerable Spirits on the day of Jiazi dispatch the Great One’s Central Terrace’s great envoys to traverse the heavens and earth, inspecting the spirits. On this day, burning incense and submitting to the Three Heavens, they shall be appointed as Heaven’s Overseers and Earth’s Stewards, their names inscribed in the Jade Registers.

The Supreme Mystery’s Upper Palace’s High Perfected Great Spirits on the day of the Beginning of Spring gather the various venerable great sages at the Supreme Ultimate’s Upper Palace to tally the jade tablets and golden names, determining those worthy of immortality.

The Supreme Mystery’s Upper Palace’s Primordial Perfected of the Supreme Simplicity on the day of the Spring Equinox gather the various immortal officials at the Jasper Terrace of Kunlun to review and establish the Numinous Treasure’s true scriptures.

The Supreme Mystery’s Upper Palace’s Five Emperors on the day of the Beginning of Summer gather the immortals at the Purple Tenuity Palace.

The Supreme Mystery’s Upper Palace’s Three Officials of Heaven on the day of the Summer Solstice gather at the Office of Life’s Controller.

The Supreme Mystery’s Upper Palace’s Perfected of the Five Marchmounts on the day of the Beginning of Autumn ascend to the Yellow Elder Lord of the Central Yellow Chamber’s Cloud Court, gathering the immortal officials to review the world’s spirit charts and numinous medicines.

The Supreme Mystery’s Upper Palace’s Supreme Yang Terrace’s Perfected on the day of the Autumn Equinox ascend to the Supreme Clarity’s Numinous Watchtower, the Grand Tenuity’s Lodge, gathering the Numinous Treasure’s true spirits, the Most High’s Five Venerable Lords, and the Northern Culmen’s Perfected Duke.

The Supreme Mystery’s Upper Palace’s Perfected Assembly of Immortals on the day of the Beginning of Winter gather the immortal officials and jade maidens at the Terrace of Yang.

On the Winter Solstice, ascending to the Azure Radiance of the Eastern Florescence, they gather at the Eastern Sea’s Azure Youth’s Golden Opening, where the Prime Minister and the Perfected Great Spirits of the Ultimate review and establish the registers of immortals. Contemplate the spirit, record the qi, practice the methods, and ascend the names—these are the Eight Commands of the Most High for the fast.

Ascend to heaven without a cloud-ladder,
Step through flight without stellar qi—
Yet compare learning without fasting.

A day of pure fast adds ten decades to life;
Ten decades of pure fast add a cycle to destiny;
A thousand days of pure fast add a century to years.
Conceal virtue, hide radiance,
Summon spirits, seek response.

The Golden and Yellow Registers—
the solemn rites of the Numinous Treasure’s many fasts.
Six methods of fasting:
Golden Register, Yellow Rescript, Luminous Perfection,
Three Primes, Spontaneity, and Cultivation of the Body.

The repository of separation and union,
the gate of opening barriers—
these are the offices for delivering the living.

The palaces of the Six Heavens—
where names of the dead are cast aside,
where the repository of opening barriers
delivers the body of the adept.

If there is wrong, immediately reform and repent;
if there is right, steadfastly persist.
Inner and outer intermingle,
victory and defeat tilt against each other,
before and after connect.

*The Supreme High’s Chart of Predestined Fate*
Wash the heart, confess transgressions first,
dispel faults, send away errors.
Do not blame heaven and earth,
do not resent humans and spirits.
Reform virtue, cultivate the future—
in three years, carve and attain transcendence.

Accumulate goodness as ramparts,
the heavens’ net is like frost and snow.

The Three Sovereigns—
unless born of the Jade Clarity’s lineage,
all are conceived in the primal undifferentiated qi,
bound to the snatching of defilement.

*The Luminous Regulations of the Nine Perfected*
Unveil the Three Luminaries,
loosen the hair, knock the teeth.

Then, purify with a hundred days of fasting, receive the precious scriptures, and first confess one’s own transgressions. Master and disciple together endure the trials of the Wind-Knife’s Elder. The hun and po endure ten hardships and eight calamities, the body perishes in the Dark Springs.

The upper-grade person is serene and desireless, like water facing a mirror—unobstructed, unburdened, unattached, unseeking. The middle-grade person thinks little and desires little, trembling with vigilance. The lower-grade person reveres and trusts the Daoist teachings.

Vowing to the Three Luminaries, encompassing the ten thousand kalpas, their essence remains unwavering and unyielding. Lord Dao of Mount Long vowed to serve as master for the five paths of heaven and humanity. In due time, the five sacred peaks and all mountains shall be leveled, the earth like flowing glass.

The Twelve Supreme Vows,
*The Essential Exegesis of the Supreme Perfected Writ*:
The four movements harmonize, all vows are fulfilled.
Light illumines the heavens,
floating clouds gather like mist,
shading and veiling the profound mystery.
In concealment, they practice non-action;
in dispersion, they pervade all under heaven.

The Five Vows of the Thearch:
First vow: the body moves in unison with the Three Luminaries.
Second vow: the body dwells above the Great Void, within the jeweled chambers of the King’s Palace, feasting with the Jade Emperor by day and resting with the Mysterious Mother by night, quenching thirst with the jade nectar of the surging well and the red-flowered fungus, sating hunger with dragon embryos, jade fat, and the crimson fruits of the sacred tree.
Third vow: the body generates seventy-two radiant lights of myriad forms, with extraordinary hair and bones, entering and departing the imperial palace, drawing blessings in abundance, enjoying boundless longevity.
Fourth vow: to live and die with qi, to die and be reborn again, to be enfeoffed over the ten heavens and govern the host of immortals.
Fifth vow: to ensure that all beings, along with the sun, moon, and Three Luminaries, and those of the Dao, together with their seven dark and nine ancestral kin, ascend to the Southern Palace.

The Four Directions’ Five Vows converge in the Hall of Blessings.

On the first day of the first month, when the sun is aligned with the Celestial Thearch of the Great Tenuity, one should pray to the Heavenly Net and Earthly Web, saying:
*"As I wander alone through the nets of the ten directions and nine heavens above, dare any ensnare my body? As I roam through the webs of the ten directions and nine earths below, dare any entangle my form? As I ascend to the Supreme High, entering the feast in the Palace of Flowing Springs and the Curved River, let not my hun be detained."*

Reverently observe the charts and texts, perform the morning rites with solemnity.
Visualize the Perfected Lord of the Great One
within the Chamber of Mysterious Cinnabar.
Clad in swan’s down,
ascend to the Great Clarity.
Visualize the sun and moon upon the face,
entering the Grotto Chamber and Golden Flower Palace through the nostrils,
their radiance emerging from behind the neck,
forming a nine-colored halo that gently enters the Jade Pillow.
The sun enters from the left nostril, the moon from the right.

*The Precious Esoteric Instructions of the Supreme Ultimate*:
Visualize the descent of the Dao’s spirit, the jade countenance and golden visage.
Heart and appearance align—
this is called the Capital of the Great Mystery,
where the eyes behold the Jade Capital Mountain within the hall.

Bo Chengzi, Guang Chengzi, Qing Zhenzi, and Gu Xizi
contemplate the qi of the Dipper’s stars,
merging with the body into the lotus seed.
Suddenly, they perceive within the lotus a jade mountain spanning a thousand leagues,
palaces stretching ten thousand acres,
crimson trees laden with fruit beneath cloud-touched canopies,
purple blossoms sprouting from fungi,
azure brushstrokes on a yellow ground,
the Three Simplicities and Eight Wheels.
The Four Masters roam without realizing they are atop the lotus seed.

Once the five contemplations are established,
the form of the Dao appears.
Where the Dao abides, the ten thousand things are discerned;
where the Dao transforms, the ten thousand things converge.
To think of spirits is to govern spirits,
to think of the real is to attain the real,
to think of immortals is to attain immortality,
to think of the Dao is to govern the Dao,
to think of abundance is to govern abundance.
The essence of the sage is to think of the worthy and govern the worthy.
When one’s thoughts summon aid, it is granted.
If thoughts persist unbroken,
a scattered mind brings a thousand anxieties.
Twelve contemplations,
twelve rewards.

The Five Calamities—three calamities and nine tribulations—are guided by celestial officials and welcomed by earthly deities. Commanding the Six Jia spirits, they set the stars in motion. Summoning the Three Sovereigns, they dispatch ghosts and spirits, and life’s bones daily renew. With focused and silent contemplation, the Primordial Elder bestows the jade talisman in Nanyang; the August Emperor inscribes the purple name in the Cinnabar Numinosity. Engraved in the Western Terrace’s chambers, fixed in the Eastern Flower’s abode, they harmonize with the qi of the Three Simplicities. Gazing upward, one beholds the radiance of the morning lamp. The Eight Effulgences propel the body in ascent, circling through seventy-four directions. Grace flows through the nine marshes, and blessings surge through the mysterious and plain.

The *Nine Heavens’ Scripture of Spirit Generation* arises from the soaring, arcane qi of the Three Caverns. Threefold harmonies form its sound, coalescing into numinous script. It unites the hundred spirits, concealing their inner names through kalpas. Reciting the *Celestial Treasure* illumines the light of heaven and earth; reciting the *Numinous Treasure* awakens the souls of the Nine Dark Realms from eternal night; reciting the *Spiritual Treasure* governs the ten thousand spirits; reciting the *Grand Unity* delivers the body’s spirits; reciting the *Nine Heavens* generates life. When one recites it once, the sound ascends to the Nine Heavens, the Golden Towers and Jade Halls, the Twelvefold Gates, the Purple Portals and Jade Pavilions, the thirty-six thousand barriers. The Grand Unity confers talismans; the Primordial Lord grants life. Jade lads and maidens serve east and west, galloping in dragon chariots to ascend at dawn to the Nine Heavens’ spirit generation.

The *Five Thousand Characters of the Dao and Its Virtue*:
The superior adept, upon receiving its rhymes, becomes a Celestial King of the Most High;
the middling adept, upon reciting it, becomes a flying immortal;
the lesser adept, upon reciting it, becomes a Wheel-Turning Sage King.
The Heavenly Emperor’s numinous chariot welcomes their ethereal spirits.
Above, it extols the new bestowals of the Primordial Lord;
below, it celebrates the great compassion of the divine perfected teachings.
This path, when one supplicates the Five Chapters, the *Numinous Writ of the Great Emperor*, and recites the *Five Thousand Characters* ten thousand times, summons the descent of the Most High’s cloud-dragon in welcome. For those who have not yet departed, recite it thrice a month.

The *Supreme Ultimate’s Esoteric Annotations and Treasured Instructions*:
On the half-month, one’s fate-day, the eight solar terms, at noon and midnight, receive and recite the *Five Thousand Characters*. Entrusting one’s form to the Great Yin’s day, one avoids the trials of Mount Tai’s Five Offices and the hells’ punishments. Above, one is reborn before the Heavenly Emperor; below, one is reborn into the households of marquises and kings, endowed with perfect features and a spirit so radiant it outshines blossoms. In tranquil contemplation of the Mysterious Chamber, establish the Terrace of Blessings.

Entering the chamber to recite the scriptures, all don the sashes of the Five Emperors, while the Four Offices and their retinues come forth in welcome.

From the *Luminous Regulations of the Four Poles*:
When Yin Xi recites one scroll of scripture ten thousand times over a thousand days, his ears become keen of hearing, his eyes penetrating of sight. The heavens each present lotus thrones and high seats, celestial beings bear jeweled canopies to cover him, flying dragons roar, lions guard the gates. The divine kings of the heavens, possessed of the Five Penetrations, along with spirit-people, scatter flowers, burn incense, and make offerings.

The Most High Dao Lord expounded the *Great Wisdom Writ of Supreme Clarity*. The Golden Portal Emperor, seated in attendance, heard it and reported to the Azure Lad: "This prime ministerial rank may be conferred upon Daoist practitioners." Later, he informed Chi Xianzi of the Southern Marchmount, who fell ill in the Golden Flower Mountains. As the saying goes: "Heaven is lenient, but ghosts afflict with illness to disrupt one’s true nature." Though stricken, he chanted and recited, completing three thousand repetitions. The Great Golden Portal then made him the True Person of the Grand Hut. At the same time, all acclaimed his virtue, and his blessings advanced in threefold measure.

The True Persons of the Ten Directions
attended the *Numinous Writ* in the Jade Mountains, pacing the void through the Five Peaks, where all the heavens came forth in welcome, praising his excellence.

The Dao is not to be prized—what is to be prized is the power to act. The dragon transforms the seven yin souls, the thirst-demons within the body’s namesake.

The method for restraining the seven souls:
On the new moon, the full moon, and the last evening of the lunar month—once each.

From the *Purple Writ of the Numinous Book*:
In the Great Beginning’s primordial chaos, the Three Qi distinctly separated.

The Cavern-Chamber of Golden Splendor is called the Radiant Origin. The arts of restraining the hun-souls and controlling the po-souls, the methods for nurturing the spirit and cultivating life—these are recorded in the *Ink-Recorded Cinnabar Writs of the Most High*.

The Five Perfected stabilize and guard against external demons. The *True Scripture of the Grand Cavern*, the Jade Emperor of the Supreme Sovereign—none is accomplished without the One, none is perfected without the One. To unite with the One as One—this is the path of the highest of the high.

For those of the middle rank and above, one must visualize the Three Origins, give life to and stabilize the Three Offices. The Three Corpses will surely fall, and the Three Origins will again be wondrous. Diligently practice the Five Virtues, and myriad good deeds will accumulate daily.

That which does not live shall not live; that which prolongs death shall hasten death.

The One is where primordial qi arises. The One is the guiding principle of Heaven.

If you truly desire long life, the Three-in-One must be made clear. When hunger reaches the thought of the One, the One grants coarse food; when thirst reaches the thought of the One, the One grants broth. Though slow, it is not hurried—the One settles in its chamber.

If one can conceal and prepare, the One will not depart. Seek it without ceasing, and you will ascend to those Nine Chambers.

Heaven can guard the One and cover without lifting; Earth can guard the One and remain still in its place. The mountains can guard the One and not shun cold or heat. The darkness can guard the One and flow without returning. If a person can guard the One, they will surely attain transcendence and ascend as an immortal.

The Guardian-General of the Precepts, the Twenty-Four Great Spirits, serve to protect and defend.

Bocheng Qinsheng inquired of the Way of Yunfang and the secrets of the Three Perfections. The Jade Emperor and the White and Two Purities are the Lord Emperors of the body, the primal perfected ones among the hundred spirits.

Now, to assist the solitary and examine the upright, the Three Sovereigns settle within, the Great One preserves the embryo, and the Five Elders refine the essence. The One abides in the Cinnabar Field, where the Controller of Destiny guards life. The One dwells in the Crimson Palace, where purple qi bathes the form. The One is honored in the Grotto Chamber, where the Three Simplicities merge in radiance. The Cloud Palace of the Hall of Light, the Purple Gate and Jade Portal, the Yellow Watchtower and Golden Chamber, the Jade City and Vermilion Window—these are the inner abodes of the Imperial One, the treasure chambers of the Three Perfected.

Thus, the single scene of Yunfang blends spirit and human, ascending to Kunlun above and descending to the Pure Springs below. Cloud canopies rise in towering majesty, forests and bamboos flourish in verdant splendor. The Seven Numinous Spirits revolve, the Three Colors entwine, and layered towers of ten thousand tiers form mist in three years. The Jade Watchtower stands in serene emptiness, the Seven Gates lie in profound depths. Golden doors and jade cabinets hold the talismanic registers in five scrolls. The undifferentiated takes form—summoning yang and calling forth yin.

The Three-in-One is the numinous origin of the body, the root of life for the hundred spirits, the mountain source of fluids, the royal chamber of soul and essence. The stomach’s pool is square to receive things, the brain’s palace is empty and round to accommodate the perfected. Ten thousand hairs stand erect, a thousand pores generate breath. Virtue fills Heaven and Earth, rank equals the Great Mystery.

Above the space between the brows lies the Cinnabar Field Palace, where the Red Child dwells. The heart is the Middle Cinnabar Field Palace, where the Perfected One dwells. Three inches below the navel is the Lower Cinnabar Field Palace, where the Infant Brother dwells. These together form the Three Cinnabar Fields.

The head contains nine palaces: three inches inward from between the brows is the Upper Twin Cinnabar Fields; one inch inward is the Hall of Light Palace; three inches inward is the Grotto Chamber Palace; three inches inward is the Cinnabar Field Palace; one inch above the Four Halls is the Heavenly Court Palace; one inch above the Grotto Chamber is the Flowing Pearl Palace; five inches inward is the Jade Emperor. Above the Hall of Ultimate Perfection is the Mystic Pearl Palace, one inch above the Flowing Pearl is the Supreme August Palace.

Above the space between the brows, within it lie the Yellow Watchtower and Purple Gate, the Crimson Terrace and Azure Chamber. Together they stand guard. The Azure Chamber’s great spirit is named *Zhengxin* ("Upright Heart"), styled *Chufang* ("Primal Square"). Within the Cinnabar Field Palace, the Lord Emperor is ever present; within the guarded inch, the great spirit is ever present.

The Most High said: The reason the Perfected One values the One as the True One is simply this—it is the One alone. The One’s resonance with the Great Void stirs unity; the One’s transformations align with the Heavenly Dao in profound accord. The Upper One is the Heavenly Emperor of the body, the Middle One is the Cinnabar Sovereign of the Crimson Palace, the Lower One is the Primal King of the Yellow Court. The true essence of the One oversees and governs the fourteen qi within the body, corresponding above to the Twenty-Four Perfected of the Grand Tenuity.

When true qi circulates in harmony, the two substances take form. The mysterious spirit blends and divides, the Purple Chamber lies in deep obscurity. The Upper One is the ultimate of the Perfected Emperor, the Middle One is the perfection of the Perfected King, the Lower One is the subtlety of the Perfected King. The Heavenly Sovereign attains the Upper One and becomes the August Ultimate; the Earthly Sovereign attains the perfection of the Upper One and becomes the One; the Human Sovereign attains the subtlety of the Upper One and dwells among the myriad subtleties.

Juzi transmitted this.

Su Lin guarded the Dao of the Three Perfected and the Primal One. He informed Lin: "I have been summoned by the August Lord to serve as Grand Master of the Four Offices of the Central Yellow, governing the Northern Sea." Later, he left behind a single document, which read: "The Five Pecks and Three Ones are secrets of the Supreme Emperor. After twenty years of concentrated contemplation, the Three Ones appeared. I now transmit this scripture to you. If you can guard the Three Ones, your name will be inscribed on the Jade Tablets.

"Should you abide in the Grotto Chamber as a Minister of the Upper Clarity and be further enlightened regarding the Three Origins to become one of the Five August Lords, the Golden Portal August Lord of Later Saints shall ascend in radiant clouds, traversing the Ten Great Forests.

"During the reign of Emperor Yuan of Han, he told his disciple Zhou Jitong: 'Yesterday, I was summoned by the Mystic Province to serve as Perfected Minister of Destiny, Grand Master of the Supreme Ultimate, and Marquis of the Central Office. Tomorrow, a cloud chariot with feathered canopies, drawn by dragons and tigers, accompanied by thousands of attending officers, will come to receive me.' That very day, Lin ascended to heaven, rising slowly toward the northwest, enveloped in clouds and mist.

"Thus, in the era of the Three Sovereigns, those who studied the Dao all prized the guarding of the One. One must make the heart uncarved and the spirit congealed, the body single-minded in sincere devotion. Let no hundred thoughts arise, and let essence and intent not scatter. If for three months one inwardly gazes and fixes the mind, a single spirit will appear, and the radiance of spirit will transform and coil through the five viscera.

"After the dispersal of the uncarved and the true, and the latent rise of florid falsity, the One fails to summon response, and spirits do not immediately answer. The method of the Three Ones is the first chapter of the true scriptures of the Golden Portal August Lord of the Upper Clarity of the August Heaven, the ultimate of the most exalted Dao, the ford of divine immortals, the wondrous formula of the host of Perfected. In all the myriad affairs of advancing or retreating in one’s person, one should constantly contemplate the One.

"Mud the nine palaces to nourish the po souls;
Within the Central Origin, embrace the One Palace.
The two numinous storehouses of the Cinnabar Field,
Merge to give birth to the Spirit King.
The Three Passes govern the nine great [forces];
Inhaling and exhaling, the light of sun and moon.
The five stars nurture them,
While the six ministers first flow and submit.
In stillness, the ten thousand qi return;
Spirit at peace, the body too flourishes.
The Perfected of the Three Sections and Eight Effulgences,
Escort me into the Grand Palace.

Ten thousand scrolls of cinnabar script
Are not equal to abiding in the One.
In precious retreat, preserve essence and cultivate the celestial form,
That the myriad things may be nurtured.
The wise scholar transcends the transformations of thought.
In the era of the Upper Sovereign, people
Deeply knew the ultimate essence of heaven and earth,
Attaining the mind and intent of heaven and earth.
When not studying,
It is like gazing in the dark at night—
East, west, south, north,
One strays beyond one’s chamber.
Riding the wind and soaring through the void,
Driving dragons and galloping through emptiness,
One observes the body."

The Pure and Profound Daoist Sect,
In silent contemplation, enters the Three Pristine Palaces;
The subtlest Way of the Utmost Dao pervades.

Ten trials, nine humiliations—
Yet holding reverent humility is the first wisdom.
Guiding the Three Origins and Five Spirits is the second wisdom.
Circulating through the eight directions,
One pure, one turbid; one sinking, one floating—
This is the third wisdom.
After nine years of ceaseless turning,
Reaching twenty-four years at the middle,
Thirty-two years at the height—
Such is the fourth wisdom.
Ten thousand trials, boundless endurance—
This is the fifth wisdom.

Perceiving form, perceiving qi, perceiving spirit,
The primordial origin of thought and reflection,
Right perception and liberation.
Resplendent is the adamantine body,
Transcendent, the Supreme Immortal.
Knowing the real, one attains the real;
Diligently seeking, one obtains the real.
The marvelous union of spirit and origin,
In serene contemplation, ever flowing.
The sun’s radiance transforms and moves,
The Purple Court illumines the body.
The Dao awakens to the Supreme Perfected,
The Seven Numinous Talismans penetrate deeply;
The divine mechanism becomes keenly perceptive,
The Eight August Ones establish the scripture.
One’s name is presented in the Imperial Hall,
Feathered registers inscribed in the Great Origin.
The body reposes in the Verdant Chamber,
Soaring through the Jade Void.

External study may reach the origin,
Yet internal study naturally pervades all.
Guiding the reins to ascend the luminous rosy clouds,
Flowing essence shines upon the jade branches.
Gazing back, within the nothingness there is being,
Merging as one with the infant.

Treading warily as upon ice and blades, one ascends the Mystery.
Empty, empty—thus one naturally unites with the Dao’s true Unity,
Recorded in the Supreme Perfected’s Purple Writs.

Should you wish to ascend to Heaven,
First practice the Seven Numinous [Talismans].
Having scaled the Northern Culmen,
Enter the Purple Court—
There, inscribed upon the Northern Wall of the Supreme Ultimate,
Are these characters:
*"At Xianyang, Mao Ying received the Step of the Unyielding Scripture from his master."*
Tested by fire that seared his robe,
Though his mouth spoke not a word,
His countenance remained as the Celestial Hosts marching the Supreme Ultimate.
He ascended to the Upper Clarity,
And now, ninety-eight years hence,
Has been appointed Minister to the Thearch-Emperors—
Thus is the sincerity of discernment and acceptance made known.

*The Jade Characters on the Golden Tablet of the Grand Tenuity*
—Inner Transmission of the Lady of the Southern Marchmount,
The Purple Void Primordial Sovereign

The Three Realms and Six Heavens
Are the domains of ghostly spirits, demon-kings, and their officials.
Those who align with the Lesser Dao summon lesser spirits;
Those who align with the Middle Dao summon middle spirits;
Those who align with the Great Dao summon great spirits.

The Primordial is the origin of Heaven and Earth,
Exalted by the Three Realms,
Illumined by the Five Thearchs.
The Five Palaces bind qi,
The Six Repositories generate the true;
The Nine Treasuries brightly reveal the Supreme Perfected’s Nine Crimson-Speckled Talismans.
Fathom the marvelous awakening of Heaven’s essence,
Sever all attachments to proximate thoughts.
The Feminine One and the Five Elders—
A hundred petitions birth the realm beyond the absolute.

Scattering winds to harmonize jade flutes,
Flying mists racing with six reins.
Setting aside the myriad entanglements,
One roams freely between Heaven and Earth,
Beyond the eight limits of the clouds,
To dwell as a neighbor to the Dao.

Those who awaken first guide those who awaken later,
Turning the current back to the One Source.
Much toil yields little gain—
In the end, this strays from the Great Vehicle.

Fourfold attainment:
First, *ascendant attainment*—golden suzhou pearls and jade,
Seven-jeweled palaces,
Equal to the Jade Capital;
Second, *bodily attainment*—form and marks perfected,
Diamond-indestructible;
Third, *destined attainment*—lifespan’s length or brevity,
Entrusted wholly to the Three Treasures;
Fourth, *sincere attainment*—fortune and misfortune, good and evil,
Suffering and joy, self and other both forgotten,
Ascending beyond the Three Clarities.

The form of the Primordial Shape—
Those who are virtuous can glimpse it.
Wisdom practices the Six Perfections,
Transcending the Three Realms,
Delivering from the nine shades of suffering—
Thus it is called the Six [Virtues].

First, the power of diligence;
Second, the power of faith;
Third, the power of quiescence;
Fourth, the power of perseverance;
Fifth, the power of refining cold;
Sixth, the power of renouncing wine and lust.

The *Sutra of Dispelling Demons*—
Thus one dissolves the Three Nets.

Breathing nurtures the cloud-sprout.
Those of the first attainment—
A hundred words cannot cure them.
Those of the second attainment—
A thousand words cannot alter them.
Those of the third attainment—
Ten thousand words cannot reach them.
Those of the fourth attainment—
The ten directions cannot sway them.
Those of the fifth attainment—
A hundred methods cannot constrain them.
Those of the sixth attainment—
In utter silence, vast and boundless.
None but these six may compose true scripture.
All outside the Orthodox Dao are called deviant texts.

The Six Penetrations—
First, the eye’s penetration: *all-penetrating vision*,
Gazing upon the Three Honored Ones,
Undisturbed by the five colors,
Neither yin nor yang,
Neither small nor great,
Nothing unseen.

Second, the ear’s penetration: *all-penetrating hearing*,
Receiving the Three Treasures,
Unobstructed by the five tones,
Neither pure nor turbid,
Neither sharp nor dull,
Nothing unheard.

Third, the nose’s penetration: *all-penetrating emptiness*,
Neither old nor new,
Neither sinking nor floating,
All distinctions known.

Fourth, the mouth’s penetration: *all-penetrating void*,
Desiring to taste the sweet dew,
The wondrous Dharma surpassing cinnabar,
No craving for flesh or strong flavors,
Neither fear nor dread,
Neither hard nor soft,
No action unperceived.

Fifth, the body’s penetration: *all-penetrating subtlety*,
Neither broad nor narrow,
Neither inner nor outer,
All thoroughly fathomed.

Sixth, the mind’s penetration: *all-penetrating clarity*,
Irrigating the five spirits,
Scouring the ten desires,
Neither noble nor base,
Neither Dao nor worldly,
Nothing left unilluminated.

Unstained by defilement,
With the supreme medicine, one heals the madness of burning deviance.

The qi of the Six Awarenesses
Ever flows through the Six Wisdoms—
Heaven: *all-penetrating vision*,
Earth: *all-penetrating hearing*,
East: *all-penetrating emptiness*,
West: *all-penetrating void*,
South: *all-penetrating clarity*,
North: *all-penetrating turbidity*.

This adept bears the jade-name of the Supreme Ultimate,
Alone strides the Jade Capital,
Transcending the Three Realms—
How majestic the office of the Celestial Mountain’s Immortal Lord!

The markings of the Mysterious Metropolis are no empty boast.
*The Fundamental Vows and Precepts*:
Within the primordial lies the wondrous,
Refining the false into the true.
Heaven establishes yin and yang,
The Three Sovereigns.

The Heavenly Thearch Lord,
The Supreme Primordial Lord of the Southern Culmen,
The Heavenly Thearch Lord of the Grand Tenuity,
The Posterior Sage’s Ninefold Mysterious Lord of the Golden Watchtower—
Having purified through fasting for three months,
Profound contemplation stirs the Great Stillness,
Accumulated devotion awakens the Supreme Clarity.
Thereupon, the radiance of jade halts its splendor,
The ninefold *mystic* scriptures coil in sequence,
Hidden mushrooms weave their blossoms,
Night-born treasure-light arises,
*Excess dissipates, clarity descends*,
The primordial Dao advances with its companions,
Sipping the nectar of Great Harmony,
Grace flows through the jade tablets.

*The Supreme Simplicity of the Numinous*:
The first jade maidens were not true—
Only the fourth jade maiden,
Upon whose nose rests a grain of white jade,
Is the true Mysterious Jade.
The Numinous Sovereign discerns your intent—
The Supreme Ultimate has inscribed your name upon the jade tablets,
In the Green Script and Purple Void’s palace,
The Golden Book and Floral-Bound Pavilion.
Your name is carved into the cinnabar script of the Supreme Clarity’s brocade register,
Appointed as the Supreme Void’s Primordial Lady,
Controller of Destinies of the Supreme Clarity,
Further bestowed the title of Mountain’s Honorific,
Ennobled as the Lady of the Southern Marchmount.

How majestic the virtue of the Great Perfected!
How still the cause of non-arising!
A hundred rivalries smoke and rise,
Ten thousand currents branch and diverge—
Yet within the Mysterious, the virtue of awakening
Self-accomplishes the sage and Perfected.

The advent of the Great Cycle brings the Great Authority,
Following the times, one receives the mandate of the Three Heavens—
Those who serve as the world’s teachers all practice the Orthodox Dharma,
Receiving the mandate of the Six Heavens.
Those who serve as the world’s teachers all practice the Dragon Dharma,
Whether great or small, each bears a heavenly mandate.
Adapting to the world’s transformation, acting or concealing as the times demand,
Every thought resides in the heart.
Nine years of diligent cultivation make one a Perfected of the Great Simplicity,
Transforming form and altering substance in a thousand myriad instants.

To augment or complete the scriptures invites profound calamity.
The *Langshu* states:
*"The Way of No-Nothingness abides not even a day,
Its meaning reaches the utmost Mystery upon Mystery."*

The *Jade Capital’s Supreme Jade Sutra*
Is the ancestor of all scriptures.
The Supreme commands its transmission to the Lords, Kings, Earls, and Ministers of the Immortals.
This Great Dharma is transmitted to one person every forty thousand kalpas.

I, having received the scripture and attained Perfection,
Have commanded the Three Accumulations to bestow it upon four,
Together with you, making five.
The *True One’s Natural Scripture and Oral Instructions*:
As a token of transmission, inscribe one copy of the scripture,
Passing it to one, ten, a hundred, a thousand—
Yet the original text remains intact.

The *Fixed Resolve* states:
Among a million people,
One may obtain this text, possessing immortal scriptures and immortal registers—
Such is predestined fate.
After forty years of study, transmit this text,
Enter the famous mountains, wander the eight directions,
And none among heaven and earth’s spirits dare obstruct you.
The superior adept ascends as an immortal,
The lesser adept attains liberation through the corpse.

The *Three Sovereigns*:
The immortal youths attending the scripture,
The Lords of the Immortals inquire.
To receive the Dao without reverence or mindfulness of the master
Invites the Three Officials’ mockery.
To recklessly divulge it binds seven generations in the prisons of hell,
While the self suffers the trials of the Three Evils.

Kings and lords who uphold the scripture
Preserve their ancestral temples and secure their states.

The *Ninefold Subtle Supreme Perfection* transmits the *Scripture of Wisdom and Insight*:
The Grand Master of the Great Ultimate, the Lofty Immortal King of the Supreme Ultimate.
To transmit the scripture without faith is called transgressing the Dao of Heaven.
To transmit without proper lineage is to divulge Heaven’s treasures.
Patterned after Heaven and Earth—what does not arise? What does not come to fruition?
Patterned after the Yangtze, the Yellow River, the Huai, and the seas—what waters do not flow? What streams do not course?

Only when one bears the immortal countenance above,
Filial piety within,
And wisdom and clarity below
May one receive the scripture.
A single moment of sincerity—
Human and divine alike respond in kind.

From the Dragon Han era to the Crimson Brightness,
Through the long night of the Nine Dark Realms,
Those who attained liberation—
Their names are all inscribed in the Southern Mound Palace, the Nine Capitals, and the Upper Registers.
Eradicating the qi of the Nine Yin,
Their names are recorded in the Eastern Florescence.

Gazing toward the Eight Paths of the Mystic Radiance,
Seven revolutions of the Heaven-Weaving Scripture—
The Supreme Eightfold Simplicity Perfected.
Within a single heaven:
One becomes the Most High,
One becomes the Lord Sovereign,
One becomes Laozi,
One becomes the Heavenly Master.
Emerging from the Three Realms,
Externally aiding the Nine Heavens—
The Lords of the Immortals attain the Dao,
The Three Masters come to deliver,
As the Seven Jeweled Mountain is illumined by the sun.

With heart opened and mind enlightened,
Offer fragrant oil, paper, and brush
To the field of blessings.
O noble one of abundant virtue!

Offering gold and treasures to present the Writ of the Perfected.
One Master of the Three Caverns—
Surpassing the Yellow and Red Dao by eleven thousand.
Cinnabar radiance illumines the Cloud Court,
Purple mist glows in the Jade Grove.
Resplendent, the Seven Jeweled Brush,
Dazzling, it sways with numinous sound.
Gong and shang harmonize of themselves,
Pure fragrance scatters upon one’s lapels.

Through accumulated Dao, one becomes an immortal of Tortoise Mountain.
The Cinnabar Sovereign soars with the Dark Purple Writ—
Bubbling Jade, unpossessed treasure.
The name of the True Dao:
The Emperor’s Chart and Jade Register.
In the distant heavens of the Nine Empyreans,
White tablets and blue-green registers—
The Supreme Sage Lord receives them in the Nine Voids,
Binding the Flying Dark Sash with qi’s spontaneous script,
Recording the names of later students who attain immortality,
Inscribing them in the Hall of Vast Numinosity.
None but the Supreme Sages can comprehend or read them.
After seventy years,
They are inscribed at the northern source of Kunlun’s secret cavern,
Each character a zhang in size.

The Immortal Stair ascends above the Nine Capitals,
Where the Jade Register’s main ledger records the names of those who attain the Dao.
The student’s name is entered in the Azure Palace,
Yet without a gold tablet or jade script,
One cannot be appointed Immortal Attendant or Director of the Jade Bureau.
Those who are diligent and reverent—
All have their names memorialized to the Jade Emperor,
And the Three Primes and Eastern Florescence of the Most High then dispatch the transmission of their true scriptures.
None among the later sages and host of Perfected fail first to present a gold tablet to Eastern Florescence,
Or cast a jade missive to the Upper Clarity,
Before receiving the *Great Cavern Perfected Scripture*.
Unlearned disciples—
Their blue-green scrolls bear no name in the Gold Register,
Their jade ledgers no script of the Dark Writ.
They cannot unfold the divine scriptures,
Nor will jade maidens guard their bodies.

Those who study the Perfected receive the *Eight Simplicities Scripture of Dark Clarity*—
All have the Supreme Emperor,
Their names recorded in the Western Florescence Palace,
Where jade tablets and medicinal texts are kept in the Purple Palace.
As True Persons, five thousand years before their birth,
They already possessed the Dark Fixed Register,
And were destined to encounter this scripture.
The *Eight Simplicities* of gold marrow and jade bone,
The wondrous Dao of the Lofty Dark,
The secret scrolls of Jade Clarity—
All are conferred upon those of gold names and jade script,
The lofty immortals.

The Heavenly King’s Dark Mirror,
The Seven Sages’ inscribed scrolls,
The Western Tortoise’s fixed register,
The Eastern Florescence’s recorded names,
The Dark Chart and Emperor’s Tablet,
Names inscribed in the Azure Palace—
The Nine Heavenly Kings dispatch the Four Poles’ True Persons
To bestow the imperial writs of jasper script.
The Upper Prime of the Southern Culmen—
The treasured secret writs of jade seals—
Without gold tablets or jade marrow,
Without names recorded in the Emperor’s Chart,
One cannot behold the scrolls’ sequence.
Without a gold name in the Orchid Terrace,
Or cinnabar script in the Purple Chamber,
One cannot see its texts.

The Supreme August’s register of the people’s destiny fixes the True Jade Record.
The Three Heavens’ Orthodox Unity Masters wear it
To determine the names of those who attain immortality.
The Azure Lad daily declares:
The Heavenly Record manifests in the Azure Palace,
Qi and seasons are diagnosed in bodily form,
Green script shines in the Great Ultimate,
The heart’s spirit is rectified in the Purple Chamber.
One who has a name in the Gold Pavilion—
Their eyes possess sunlight,
Their teeth are green, their blood white.
Such a person is benevolent and delights in immortality,
Bright and keen, outstanding and transcendent.

If the Upper Clarity has a gold book and jade record,
Their back bears a mark like the River Chariot,
Their chest has recumbent bones.
If the Great Ultimate has cinnabar tablets and blue-green script,
Their hands bear the characters of "accumulated person" and "inverted great."
If the Square Cauldron has a dark simplicity and purple name,
Their eyes have four rings with purple light within.
If the Grand Clarity has a jade register and crimson name,
Their voice has jade resonance, their mouth square, their eyes round.
If the Grand Clarity has jasper tablets and gold script,
Their belly is white-willed, their mouth emits purple qi.
If the Southern Culmen has cinnabar script and purple records,
Their head generates five qi, ascending to the layered clouds.
If the Dipper contains a dark jade register,
Their heart is cinnabar, their apertures purple,
Yellow blossoms encircle their stomach,
Their mouth exhales fragrant qi, their teeth overflow with jade liquid.
From youth, they delight in gazing at the flowing clouds of sun and moon,
And rejoice in the luminous images of stars and constellations.

If the Dark Capital’s Cinnabar Terrace has white jade and gold script,
Their liver is green, their sinews purple,
Their kidneys azure with patterned veins.
Their breast brims with essence, their body is fragrant and supple.
If the Three Primes Palace has jade missives and blue-green script,
Their brain is purple, their tongue brocade,
Their will dark at the temples,
Their intestines green, their marrow vermilion,
Their forehead square, their brow round.
Their yin possesses hidden bones,
Their apertures three barriers;
Their eyes emit flowing light,
Green essence congeals into liquid.
Their palms bear the curves of fungi,
Their teeth three-edged,
They cherish water and embrace mountains,
Treasure their po and nurture their hun.
All who possess these marks are destined to become highest immortals.

Those next have a dark mountain and black will upon their nose—
Their belly must also have a dark mound to correspond to that mountain,
A red and black will.
Green bones...

Those who delight in the fragrance of the Five Perfumes and are eager to study the affairs of divine immortals—
They walk like cranes and move like dragons,
Their necks bear growths, and they avoid resting their ears upon pillows.
Beneath their morning-concealed lungs lies a blue *zhi*,
Their bodies bear networked patterns,
Their hearts are true, their gallbladders serene,
Their ears firm, their *qi* expansive.
The Dark Province also holds registers inscribed with golden names.

Next are the Three Palaces of Mount Tai,
Where the Dark Record and White Register mark the land of the living,
Not inscribing the realm of the dead.
The Great Yin’s records of life and death are kept in black ledgers, white scrolls, and cinnabar-bound bamboo slips.
When the true tally reaches six thousand slips,
Each person is inscribed in the land beyond death.

Master Jinglin spoke to Hua Cun:
"Now I see your essence—radiant as the dawn, luminous and resplendent,
Your round spirit shines with layered brilliance,
Phoenix bones pierce your brain,
Nine-colored jewel-lights,
Five viscera bound in purple,
Your heart bears bright script.
Thus, your form dwells among celestial mists,
Your spirit communes with the numinous realm."

*The Inner Transmission of the Purple Void Primordial Sovereign*
*Upper Clarity Scripture of the Dao-Treasures, Scroll One* (conclusion)

*Upper Clarity Scripture of the Dao-Treasures, Scroll Two*
**Heavenly Rank, Third Chapter**

No divine writ surpasses the Three and Five:
The sun, moon, and Northern Dipper as Three,
The five stars as Five.
The Great One
Is the celestial script, the Primordial Unity.
Heaven covers, earth bears,
All things arise between them.
Heaven and earth are the constancy of the Great Dao—
Heaven’s constancy is the One Heaven,
The Dao’s constancy is the One Dao.
*Qi* transforms into nine,
Thus there are the Nine Heavens,
Eighty-one heavens in all.

Heaven has Three Mysteries:
The sun, moon, and stars,
Above which are the Three Essences.
The Heaven of Purple Celestial Essence
Abides within the Great Primordium,
The *qi* of the Three Primes above the path of the Upper Radiance.
The Three Luminaries above
Form the celestial script.

Disasters have three ranks:
First fire, second water, third wind.
Nothing under heaven is eternal—how could anything be unyielding?
After the great transformation,
When four or five suns rise,
Rivers and streams dry, the great seas run empty.
When six suns rise,
All things perish,
Like rendered fat.
Heaven and earth shatter, yin and yang cease.
After nine generations, life begins anew.
A great wind comes from another realm, from between the sun, moon, heaven, and earth,
Bearing clouds to the Eleventh Heaven,
Above and below vast as two chariot wheels.
For tens of millions of years,
Heaven rains, and the waters rise to the Eleventh Heaven,
Surrounding it on all sides with great floods,
Held in place by encircling winds that prevent overflow.
The winds blow the waters for billions of years,
Generating thick foam that transforms into seven treasures:
First yellow gold, second white silver, third lapis lazuli,
Fourth crystal, fifth coral, sixth fine jade, seventh giant clam.
Chaotic winds scatter these seven treasures,
Up to the Eleventh Heaven,
Down to the Thirteenth Heaven,
Fashioning the Ninefold Heavens,
Where the heavenly people dwell.
Later, the winds blow the waters,
And the foam congeals into seven treasures,
Gathered in the heavens to form Mount Sumeru of jeweled treasure,
Three million three hundred thousand *li* high.
Again, the seven treasures—crystal and yellow gold—
Are gathered to build the sevenfold city walls of the Sun King.
Again, two treasures—white silver and lapis lazuli—
Are gathered to build the sevenfold city walls of the Moon King.
Again, one treasure—crystal—
Is raised forty thousand *li* high
To build the abodes of the gods beneath the heavens.
The great winds govern and propel them,
Like floating clouds,
Called stars.
The largest span four hundred eighty *li*,
The smallest forty *li*.
Again, seven hundred Mount Sumerus of jeweled treasure
Are gathered on four sides to form eightfold treasure mountains—
Yellow gold, white silver, and the like.
The winds transform the remaining waters into thick earth,
Whose foam hardens into adamantine mountains,
Six million seven hundred twenty thousand *li* high,
The palace of the Three Sovereigns.

The Great Sage and Venerable Spirit
Knew not of fifty-five heavens,
But spoke only of forty-nine layers of heaven.
The upper six heavens are lodged within the *qi* of the Dao,
For the Dao resides above the Three Heavens,
Beyond the Heavenly Web.
From the lowest, one attains the first heaven,
Named Yi Heaven, styled "Luminous Clarity."
The highest of the Three Heavens
Is named Supreme Primordial Ultimate Great Dao High Yi Heaven,
Styled "Primordial Upper Three Heavens."

The Jade Capital Terrace
Floats above the Supreme Great Heavenly Web,
Now present, now absent,
Now existent, now nonexistent.
The Great Heavenly Web—
Jade and forest wings surge through the mysterious,
Sun and moon gleam with numinous splendor.
Flying immortals ride emerald *qi*,
Mounting radiance and riding purple mist.
Lush and luxuriant, they emerge from the script,
In profusion—divine treasure immortals.

The Three Clarities’ Heavens
Lie beyond the Three Realms.
Immortals dwell in the Great Clarity,
Perfected Ones in the Upper Clarity,
Sages in the Jade Clarity,
Each with their own natural palaces.

The Three Heavens:
Great Crimson Heaven, styled Great Clarity,
Its cavernous emptiness *qi* connects to the lower rank;
Yu Yu Heaven, styled Upper Clarity,
Its purple emptiness *qi* connects to the middle rank;
Clear Tenuity Heaven, styled Jade Clarity,
Its jade emptiness *qi* connects to the upper rank.

Emerging from the sea of life and death,
Ascending the mountain of non-leakage,
Arriving at the shore of the Great Clarity,
Receiving the flow of the true Dharma,
Gazing into the four directions—profound and boundless—
Thus it is called Cavernous Mystery.
The ultimate within the gaze
Is difficult to proclaim.

Practicing the Way of the Jade Clarity,
One emerges with all the heavens’ immortals as an escort,
Attended by jade lads and jade maidens,
Bearing five-colored banners,
Riding purple clouds and driving twelve jade dragons,
Phoenix songs leading the way,
Mystic swords following behind,
The Six Masters opening the path,
Flying dragons flanking the chariot—
A rank equal to the highest immortals.

Practicing the Way of the Upper Clarity,
One emerges with the Five Constellations as an escort,
Attended by eight hundred jade lads and maidens each,
Bearing five-colored banners,
Riding a dragon chariot through flying mist,
Nine phoenixes wailing ahead,
Eight simurghs singing behind,
The White Origin opening the way,
The Supreme Ultimate’s victorious chariot—
Thus, among the perfected there are high and low,
And in ascending the mysterious, there are steps and ranks.

The Great Primordium links to the Jade Clarity,
The Three Luminaries illumine the high and bright.
The Eight Winds revolve the morning breeze,
Golden light crowns the celestial essence,
Jade splendor binds the Five Elders,
Purple mist drives the celestial plow.
Riding the *qi*, swaying through the mysterious chambers,
Yielding to the branches, emerging from the script.
Roaming freely in the Upper Clarity—
A hundred thousand kalpas are but a single day in the heavens.

*The True One’s Natural Formula*
Rising in body to the Great Clarity,
Transcending radiance and soaring beyond the purple dawn.

Ten thousand kalpas are but last night,
A thousand pillars like the morning court.
Precepts and wisdom magnify the Great Primal Chaos,
The mysterious steps rise on the whirlwind’s lift.

Three *qi* beget three—
Thus are the Nine Heavens named.
The root of the Nine Heavens
Holds three as supreme.
The heavens of the Nine Heavens,
With the Three Upper Heavens, form the Twelve *Qi*.

First, the Supreme Primordial Radiance, the Formless Heaven—
The Upper *Qi* of the Mysterious Clarity.
The Mysterious Brahma, Jade Void Heaven.
The Upper Void, Crimson Heaven.
The Great Brahma, Mysterious Origin Heaven.
Jade Emptiness, the Profound and Still Heaven.
Treasure Brahma, the Formless Mysterious Wonder Heaven.
Cloud Brahma, the Flowing Essence of the Middle Primordium Heaven.
The Upper Profound, the Boundless Heaven.
The Great Brahma, the Mysterious Essence Azure Heaven.
Purple Void, the Upper Primordium Heaven.
The Great Brahma, the Dao-Virtueless Heaven among the Nine Heavens.
Nine Spirits, the *Qi* Heaven.
The Nameless Utmost Extreme, the Brahma-Voice Heaven.
The Cicada-Silent Heaven.
Empty Brahma, the Central Heaven.
The Supreme Ultimate, the Boundless Purple Void Profound Heaven.
Verdant Brahma, the Natural Heaven.

The Four Heavenly Sounds—
The Thirty-Six Heavens share their names,
Born before the primordial *qi* of the Hollow Void,
Inscribed upon Kunlun’s mountain.
The Highest Ones chant their jade scriptures,
The Upper Ministers gather their wondrous chapters.
Above, they mark the Mysterious Chart;
Within, they hold pure the Six Offices and Thirty-Six Sounds;
Below, they govern the Nine Lands and Thirty-Six Earthly Sovereigns.

The numinous chapters flow unimpeded,
The jade tones gleam with spirit-freshness—
All are the wandering songs of the Heavenly Kings,
The treasured scriptures of the Hollow Mystery.
Six by six, their rhymes unite;
Four by four, they align with the perfected.
Nine by nine, the emperors divide—
Thus are the Thirty-Six Heavens named,
Above reaching the boundless and infinite,
Below plumbing the fathomless abyss of the Hollow Source.

None among the flying immortals and transcendent perfected
Who do not receive the jade tones
May wander and behold the boundless scriptures.
Those who obtain the scriptures,
Whose names are inscribed in jade books,
Whose characters are carved on purple tablets,
Whose records are bound in the Jade Dawn—
After thirty-six years of carving,
They attain the rank of Upper Immortal,
Ascending to the Heaven of Primordial Radiance above,
Plumbing the Nine Lands’ source below.
Like silver, like jade—
They gain a body of cold-hued essence.

The Six Demon Kings of Heaven:
First, the Crimson Void Heaven;
Second, the Supreme Clarity Capital Heaven;
Third, the Vast Heaven;
Fourth, the Great Mystery Heaven;
Fifth, the Great Mystery Azure Heaven;
Sixth, the Great Clarity Heaven.

The qi of the Primordial Highest Jade Emperor of the Primal Cavern’s Great Non-Being,
The qi of the Crimson Primal Non-Being’s Highest Jade Void,
The qi of the Dark Serene Mysterious Pervasion’s Highest Jade Void—
Though their years differ and their names vary, their root is one.

Without light, without form,
Without shape, without name,
Without color, without trace,
Without sound, without voice—
Accumulated yang forms heaven,
Accumulated stagnation forms earth.

The Three Qi are the honor of heaven and earth,
The Nine Qi are the root of heaven and earth.
The Three unite to perfect virtue,
The ultimate of heaven and earth.

The Five Phases array their positions,
The warp and weft of the Eight Poles—
Heaven and earth’s length and breadth.
The upper qi is the Beginning of Day, its color true azure;
The middle qi is the Origin, its color true white;
The lower qi is the Mysterious, its color true yellow.

The qi of Supreme Harmony, the Great Obscurity,
Lies above the Nine Heavens—termed the Obscure Qi,
Utterly remote and cut off,
Balancing the Nine Mysteries.
Only by reciting the *Great Cavern Jade Scripture* may one commune with it,
Whereupon the Jade Emperor mounts the Cinnabar Clouds to initiate the Dao,
The Great Obscurity dons green radiance and shines resplendent.
The halls of golden ramparts fill,
The courtyards of cloud-pearls receive the perfected.

Within the Three Primordials’ Palace,
The qi of Three Flowers arises,
Like the radiance of hibiscus,
Mysterious hues in the void.
Within the Origin’s Celestial Cycle,
There is a Golden Watchtower,
Wherein dwells the qi of the Upper Effulgence.
Its qi and color luxuriant,
Purple mists swirl,
Its brilliance illumines the ten directions,
Clouds shade the Golden Watchtower—
The gathering place of later sages.

Condensed qi forms purple radiance,
Cinnabar clouds mirror the azure sky,
Spread in the southwest’s turning.
The Three Mornings brighten the Seven Luminaries,
The constellations array the Grand Tenuity.

The Three Ones’ Primordial Lords
Each possess true qi,
Forming a thousand chariots and ten thousand riders,
Cloud carriages and feathered canopies.

The upright qi of the Twenty-Four Spirits—
Scattered, it becomes clouds and mist;
Gathered, it becomes form and shadow.
Issuing forth, it transforms into immortals;
Entering in, it becomes the True One.
Above, it binds the Three Primordials;
Below, it binds the myriad things.

The two qi part and unite,
Governing things in their seasons.
The Three Ways wax and wane,
Emergence and retreat follow fate—
The Nine Mysteries’ Dao Lords of Later Sages arrange the records.

The sun is the essence of yang, the eldest of virtue.
Virtue is that to which the myriad things return.
The sun rises in the east, and the myriad things also emerge in the east;
The sun flourishes in the south,
Sets in the west,
Hides in the north—
All things follow it.
The sun’s home is in the south, its position at noon.
In the fifth month, yin qi stirs within—
A minor waning.

The sun’s breadth spans two thousand thirty *li*,
Golden divisions,
Water essence’s halo within,
Flowing light shining without.

Within it lie walled cities and people, seven-jeweled bathing pools, where blue, yellow, and white lotuses bloom. The people stand twenty-four feet tall, clad in crimson robes, their flowering synchronized in decline and flourishing. Five winds govern the sun’s movement, thus ordering the sun, moon, and constellations in their celestial courses—all perfected by Brahmā.

Its framework: above the Golden Gate, the sun’s passage is the Open Portal. Within the Golden Gate lies the Pool of Refined Golden Essence, situated at the western pass, to the left of the division. Thus, on the day of *Lìchūn*, the solar spirit is further refined within the Golden Gate, its radiance shining beyond for forty-five days before ceasing. It proceeds in sequence to the Cavern-Yang Palace, the sun’s upper abode. On the day of *Lìxià*, it halts at the Cavern-Yang Palace, exhaling the essence of molten gold to irrigate the Eastern Well, bathing in the luminous splendor. Gathering the Eight Pure qi, it returns to the Palace of Vast Cold, arriving in thirty-five days—the moon’s upper abode beneath the Seven Stars’ floral canopy.

On the day of *Lìdōng*, the solar essence lies concealed within the Palace of Vast Cold. The sun’s yearly circuit completes its measure, crowned and girded in the four directions. The Two Luminaries part and unite; yin and yang wax and wane.

The sun and moon are the celestial and terrestrial ministers of emptiness.

From *Laozi’s Esoteric Canon of the Calendar*:
The sun’s surname is Zhāng, personal name Biǎo, courtesy name Chángshǐ.

From *The Three Sovereigns*:
The Sun-Moon King’s palaces and walled cities.

The eastern, western, southern, and northern spans measure two thousand and forty *li*. The walled city has seven concentric layers, each adorned with bamboo, trees, and groves. The city’s four gates enclose pools and forests where phoenixes, vermilion birds, and flying crows dwell—this is the chaotic wind’s domain and the Sun King’s abode.

At the city’s center stands a palace of yellow gold. On all four sides of the city walls rise golden towers and pavilions, their heights and depths spanning forty *li*. On the fiftieth heaven, beings descend to become the Sun Heavenly King, radiating great luminosity that illuminates the golden towers on all sides, generating five hundred beams of light to shine upon the four directions. The celestial beings of these heavens live for nine million years.

The Perfected of the Nine Heavens call the sun *Zhuóyào Luó*; the Perfected of the Three Heavens call it *Yuánguāng Wèi*; in the Heaven of Grand Simplicity, it is named *Miàojǐng*; the Supreme Perfected call it *Jiǔyào Shēng*. The Supreme Perfected constantly rides the luminous jade wheel, feasting within the sun. The immortals of Great Clarity call the sun *Dàmíng*; the Perfected of the Great Ultimate call it *Míngyuán*.

In the primordial era, within the Heaven of Purple Prime, there was ever a radiant glow, thin as mist—this was the origin of the nine suns, their light akin to that of a single moon. In the Heaven of Jade Worthies, the sun is called *Wēixuán*.

The radiance of the sun and moon is the effulgent bloom of their numinous brilliance. The Crimson Qi King is the divine spirit above the sun, named *Jiāngchē Liángzhī*. Those who know the name of the Crimson Qi King will not die but ascend to the Upper Clarity.

The Lord Lao calls the sun *Tàibǎo*; the Nine Radiance Eastern Perfected call it *Zǐyào Míng*, or sometimes *Yuánmèi*.

The sun’s essence is crimson, square in form yet round in radiance. Each month, it passes five times above the Golden Gate, where the essence of gold, stone radiance, and the water-mother’s flower are refined within the sun’s soul, casting forth eight rays of luminous essence.

The Cinnabar Crucible’s cinnabar qi nurtures celestial essence, firm yet receptive to the yielding. The yin bloom of scorching water, the sun’s primal radiance, is called *Dàmíng*. Nine yang forces coalesce, and twin vapors arise together. Concentrating the spirit and harmonizing the soul, the essence of harmonious qi gives birth to the Five Emperors within. They ride the light to govern form, their heads crowned with dragon-flower kerchiefs, clad in crimson sashes and azure robes. Simurghs and crows flow in mystery, their rosy glow suffusing the azure above.

The Azure Emperor within the sun, whose taboo name is *Yuáncháng Yuán* and courtesy name *Zhàolóng Tāo*, wears a robe of azure-jade brocade and a cape of verdant, feathered splendor.

The Vermilion Emperor within the sun, whose taboo name is *Dānlíng Zhì* and courtesy name *Lǜhóng Yìng*, wears a robe of crimson-jade brocade and a cape of vermilion, feathered splendor.

The White Emperor within the sun, whose taboo name is *Hàoyù Jiāng* and courtesy name *Huíjīn Xiá*, wears a robe of white-jade brocade and a cape of white, feathered splendor.

The Black Emperor within the sun, whose taboo name is *Chéngcáo Tíng* and courtesy name *Xuánlǜ Yán*, wears a robe of black-jade brocade and a cape of black, feathered splendor.

The Yellow Emperor within the sun, whose taboo name is *Shòuyì Fù* and courtesy name *Piāohuī Xiàng*, wears a robe of yellow-jade brocade and a cape of yellow, feathered splendor.

The sun’s inner spirit, the Lady of the Solar Soul, is named *Àixiāo Tái* and governs the Nine Perfected within.

The moon’s domain lies in the north, corresponding to the *zǐ* position; thus, in the eleventh month, the myriad things germinate beneath the earth. The moon’s breadth spans two thousand nine hundred *li*, while its radiant circumference measures seven thousand eight hundred and forty *li*. Within, white silver, lapis lazuli, and crystal reflect one another, divided into sixty parts, their scorching brilliance illuminating the interior.
