The city walls and populace are arrayed with seven-jeweled bathing pools and forests of eight *qiān* trees growing within.

The people of the moon stand sixteen feet tall, clad in garments of azure hue. From the first to the sixteenth day of the month, they gather white silver and lapis lazuli, refining them in the crucible of scorching light—thus, as the moon waxes, its luminosity grows bright and vast. From the seventeenth to the twenty-ninth day, beneath the *qiān* forests, they gather the blossoms of the three qi to brush the light of the sun and moon.

On the autumnal equinox, the moon lodges above the Eastern Well in the Hall of Vast Spirit, bathing in the Eastern Well’s pool to refine the lunar soul, brightening the eightfold radiance of clarity. It receives the yang essence from the sun’s brilliance and exhales yellow qi into the Jade Pool. All celestial beings gather the blossoms of the jade trees to brush the light of the sun and moon, while the moon’s yellow qi washes the countenances of the heavenly beings. The autumnal equinox is the day of the celestial assembly.

On the winter solstice, the moon rests in the upper lodge of Vast Cold, nurturing the lunar soul in the Vast Cold’s pool. It absorbs yellow qi into the jade womb and exhales yang essence into the frigid pool. All celestial beings gather the blossoms of the azure forests to brush the light of the sun and moon, while the moon’s yang essence washes the countenances of the heavenly beings.

On the vernal equinox, the moon lodges above the Golden Gate—this is the moon’s gate of numinous communion. Within the crucible of golden essence, it refines the pool of stone radiance and water-mother, adorning its luminous splendor. It irrigates the Golden Gate with yang essence and absorbs yellow qi into the Jade Spring. All celestial beings gather the blossoms of the *qiān* trees to brush the light of the sun and moon, while the sun’s yellow qi washes the countenances of the heavenly beings.

On the summer solstice, the moon rests in the Cavern-Yang Palace, the upper lodge of the day and the moon’s flowing fire court. It refines the eight rays, brightening the solar soul, irrigating the Cavern-Yang with yellow qi, and absorbing yang essence into the Fire Palace. The Eight Pure Perfected all gather the forests of azure emptiness to brush the light of the sun and moon, while the moon’s yang essence washes the countenances of the heavenly beings.

The moon’s surname is *Wén*, personal name *Shēn*, courtesy name *Zǐguāng*. From *The Three Sovereigns*: The Moon Heavenly King’s abode is a palace of lapis lazuli. On all four sides of the city walls rise golden towers and pavilions, six hundred and forty *li* in height. Beings from the fifteenth heaven descend to become the Moon Heavenly King, radiating great luminosity to illuminate the world without cease.

The *Eight Qiān*—trees of the moon, also called the King of Medicines—comprise eight trees in total.

The moon’s radiance is yellow, square in essence yet round in form, revolving and waxing, its circuit complete yet ever waning.

On the fifth, fifteenth, and twenty-fifth days of each lunar cycle, the moon bathes in the numinous radiance above the Eastern Well, adorning its essence and refining its luminous brilliance, so that its golden splendor shines anew. The Dark Canopy scatters the numinous majesty of the King of Spirits; the Three Purities open the circular path, and the golden blossom illumines the vermilion moon.

**Lady of the Bluegreen Emperor in the Moon**
Her taboo name is *Éyǐnzhū*, her style *Língyàn Yīng*. She wears a robe of azure-flowered jade brocade and a shawl of kingfisher-green embroidered with soaring dragons and phoenixes.

**Lady of the Red Emperor in the Moon**
Her taboo name is *Yìyìliáo*, her style *Wǎnyán Xū*. She wears a robe of cinnabar-and-jade brocade and a shawl of vermilion-flowered phoenix-patterned gauze.

**Lady of the White Emperor in the Moon**
Her taboo name is *Língsùlán*, her style *Yùlián Huá*. She wears a robe of fourfold dragon brocade woven with jade and a shawl of white feathered embroidery.

**Lady of the Black Emperor in the Moon**
Her taboo name is *Jiéliánqiáo*, her style *Tíngtíng Jīn*. She wears a robe of ninefold cloud brocade and a shawl of black feathered dragon-patterned gauze.

**Lady of the Yellow Emperor in the Moon**
Her taboo name is *Qīngyíng Jīn*, her style *Jiǒngdìng Róng*. She wears a robe of yellow cloud-and-mountain brocade and a shawl of green phoenix-feathered embroidery.

**The Nine Stars**
The Nine Stars are the numinous roots of the Nine Heavens, the luminous beams of the sun and moon, the abyssal palace of the ten thousand kinds. Heaven possesses nine *qi*, with the Nine Stars as their spiritual pivot; Earth possesses nine provinces, with the Nine Stars as their divine sovereign; humans possess nine orifices, with the Nine Stars as the mansion of destiny; the nine palaces of yin and yang have the Nine Stars as their gates; the Five Peaks and Four Seas have the Nine Stars as their abyssal palace. The Five Nines array in ranks, revolving through the Three Luminaries to harmonize the Four *Qi*. The Supreme Emperor employs them to commune with the perfected; immortals rely on them to attain transcendence; the Five Phases ride them to achieve their measures; the ten thousand kinds receive them to attain life. When heaven is clear and earth is still, the Nine Stars blaze with brilliance. When heaven is turbulent and earth obstructed, the Nine Stars darken and dim. The Jade Armillary summons the kalpa’s destined cycles; the Celestial Pass governs the *qi* of the Five Phases.

**The First Star: Celestial Pivot**
The spirit-soul of the Yang Brilliance Star, the Celestial Pivot is majestic yet does not blaze, luminous yet does not shine. It permeates the Great Void, spanning nine hundred and twenty *li*. Opposite the northwest gate of the Yang Brilliance Star, this star is called *Kuí Jīng Xuán*. The August Lady of the Supreme Perfected, surnamed *Míngtōng* and taboo-named *Shàngzhēn*, wears her hair in a soaring-cloud chignon. She is clad in a robe of purple, yellow, and azure brocade, girdled with a nine-belled sash, and exhales a radiance of blue-green *qi*.

**The Second Star: Celestial Rotation**
The spirit-soul of the Yin Essence Star, it shines yet does not blaze, permeating the Great Void with a span of five hundred and fifty *li*.

Opposite the western gate of the Yin Essence Star, this star is called *Xū Jīng*. The August Lady of the Supreme Mystery, surnamed *Xuánjìng* and taboo-named *Jīnguī*, wears her hair in a soaring-cloud chignon. She is clad in a flying brocade gauze skirt and a phoenix-patterned brocade mantle, girdled with a flying-spirit purple sash, and exhales a radiance of blue-green *qi*.

**The Third Star: Celestial Jade**
The spirit-essence of the Perfected Person Star, it is mighty yet does not manifest, radiant yet does not blaze. Opposite the southeastern gate of the Perfected Person Star, this star is called *Líng Fēi*. The Primordial August Lady, surnamed *Chángmíng* and taboo-named *Liúlàn*, wears a morning-infant treasure crown, a flying-cloud luminous brocade robe, and a six-jade flying-star sash.

**The Fourth Star: Celestial Balance**
The spirit-essence of the Profound Darkness Star. Opposite the eastern gate of the Profound Darkness Star, this star is called *Shàng Líng Shén Fēi*. The Resplendent August Lady, surnamed *Kāishēng* and taboo-named *Yīngguān*, wears a seven-tiered crown, a crimson gauze phoenix-patterned robe, and a golden-perfected jade-luster sash, exhaling the essence of red *qi*.

**The Fifth Star: Jade Pivot**
The spirit-essence of the Cinnabar Prime Star, vast yet not silent, surging yet not blazing.

Opposite the northeastern gate of the Cinnabar Prime Star, this star is called *Běi Shàng Jīn Gài*. The Central August Lady, surnamed *Yuánfāng* and taboo-named *Bójīng*, wears a purple-morning flying-flower crown, a nine-colored robe, and a divine-tiger jade-patterned sash.

**The Sixth Star: Celestial Gatekeeper**
The spirit-essence of the Northern Culmen Star, its numinous radiance latent yet illuminating. Opposite the lower gate of the Northern Culmen—the gate of the Northern Grotto—this star is called *Ān Shàng Chén Huá*. The Primordial August Lady, surnamed *Wángyuán* and taboo-named *Mínghuì*, wears a jade-morning crown, a flying-cyan feathered robe, and a flowing-gold fire-bell sash.

**The Seventh Star: Jade Brilliance**
The soul of the Celestial Pass Star, the Great Luminance. Its light revolves through the hollow void, turning the mechanism of the Celestial Pass. Above, it faces the southern gate of the Celestial Pass Star; below, it aligns with the Northern Culmen Star. This star is called *Yù Huá*. The Numinous August Lady wears a flying-flower cloud-tousled coiffure, a seven-hued night-luminous cloud-brocade skirt, and a nine-heaven awe-inspiring talisman.

**The Eighth Star: Grotto Radiance**
The soul-essence of the Auxiliary Star, the Yang Luminance. Its light revolves through all heavens. Above, it faces the southwestern gate of the Auxiliary Star, situated above the Celestial Pass, the *Liáng*, the yang ray of the Northern Culmen. This star is called *Dà Míng*. The Eternal August Lady wears a flying-cloud flower-tousled coiffure, a flying-gauze cloud robe, a nine-luminance sash, and exhales the light of cyan *qi*.

**The Ninth Star: Hidden Prime**
The luminous essence of the Adjuvant Star, the Hollow Numinous. Concealed beneath the canopy of latent breath, its hidden light shines within the hollow void. Above, it faces the southeastern gate of the Adjuvant Star. This star is called *Kōng Xuán Biàn Yún*. The Supreme August Lady wears a seven-tiered flying-heaven treasure crown, a cyan-patterned brocade robe, a nine-luminance night-candle sash, and exhales the essence of black *qi*.

**Yang Brightness Star**
The Celestial Grand Commandant, governing administration and rectifying transgressions. Above, it oversees the perfected of the Nine Heavens; in the middle, it supervises the flying immortals of the Five Peaks; below, it leads the later-disciples among the perfected—all of *liuli* water essence. Within it stands a jade tree bearing cyan fruit with golden-winged ravens perched upon its branches, spontaneously growing cyan-jade numinous mushrooms. One bite grants a lifespan of ninety thousand years. The star possesses nine gates, each with four *qi*, illuminating nine hundred million *li*. Within lies a cyan-walled jade tower, where the Dipper Perfected, titled the Nine Mornings Lord, wears a cyan-feather flying robe, holds the Dipper’s chart in hand, and sits within the jade tower.

**Yin Essence Star**
The Celestial Grand Steward, governing emoluments and ranks. Above, it oversees the celestial lodges; below, it leads the ten thousand spirits—all of *liuli* water essence. Within its jade tower grow black fruit, spontaneously bearing dark mushrooms and jade embryos. Consuming them grants a lifespan of fifty thousand years. The star possesses five gates, each with four lights, illuminating nine hundred million *li*. Within stands a five-hued jade tower, where the Northern Culmen Perfected, the Northern Supreme Morning Lord, wears a dark-essence jade crown, a dark-feather flying robe, holds a five-hued feathered staff, and sits within the jade tower.

**Perfected Person Star**
The Celestial Controller of Destinies, governing the affairs of gods and immortals. Above, it oversees the Nine Heavens; in the middle, it supervises the numinous immortals of the Five Peaks. Within its jade tower, yellow blossoms grow spontaneously, along with yellow essence and jade mushrooms. Consuming them grants a lifespan of thirty million years. The star possesses twelve gates, each with four lights, and above stands a yellow terrace jade tower. The Perfected, titled the Sun Immortal Florescence Morning Lord, holds the Dipper’s green register and records lives within the jade tower.

**Profound Darkness Star**
The Celestial Vanguard, governing the punishment of rebels. Above, it oversees the ghosts of the Nine Heavens; in the middle, it leads the Three Officials of the Northern Thearch; below, it monitors the myriad multitudes. Within it stands a vermilion tree bearing red fruit, spontaneously growing cinnabar mushrooms and *liuli*. Consuming them grants a lifespan of eight thousand years. The star possesses three gates, each with four lights, and above stands a vermilion terrace jade tower. The Dipper-Stepping Perfected, titled the Mystic Supreme Flying Canopy Morning Lord, wears a cinnabar-brocade flying robe, holds the life-numinous staff, and sits within the jade tower.

**Cinnabar Prime Star**
The Celestial Dipper Lord, governing the registers of destiny. Above, it oversees the Nine Heavens. Within it stands a vermilion tree bearing white fruit, spontaneously producing golden essence refined into an unguent. The star possesses seven gates, each with four lights, and above stands a plain terrace golden tower. The Perfected, titled the Golden Culmen Seven Mornings Lord, holds the green register of the nameless.

**Northern Culmen Star**

**Celestial Grand Constancy Star**
The Heavenly Grand Constancy governs ascension and advancement, overseeing the Perfected of the Nine Heavens above and commanding the Flying Immortals of the Five Peaks below. Within it stands a plum tree bearing white fruit, spontaneously producing dark mushroom jade essence; those who consume it attain a lifespan of fifty thousand years. The star possesses eight gates, each with a dark terrace and jade tower. The Dipper-Stepping Perfected, titled the Northern Aster Flying Blossom Lord, holds the Jade Scepter of the Northern Dipper.

**Celestial Pass Star**
The Heavenly Supreme Emperor’s star, governing the mechanisms of Heaven and Earth and the length of the four seasons. Within it stands a triple-flowered tree bearing five-colored fruit, spontaneously producing a nine-flavored mushroom unguent; those who ingest it emanate nine-colored radiance. Above stands a nine-tiered jade tower. The Dragon-Riding Perfected, titled the All-Numinous Nine Origins Northern Canopy Aster Lord, holds the Radiant Spirit Scepter and sits within the jade tower.

**Auxiliary Star**
The Heavenly Venerable Jade Emperor’s star, overseeing the Nine Heavens above and ruling the Nine Earths below. Within it stands a blue-flowered tree, spontaneously generating nine-toned script. A blue crow—a three-legged crow—produces lapis lazuli blossoms; one bite grants union with the Jade Emperor’s Perfection. It possesses eight gates, through which the eight qi interflow. Within, a purple-qi jade tower traverses the Three Realms. The Perfected, titled the Imperial Venerable Nine Mornings Lord, holds a fire bell.

**Rectifying Star**
The Great Emperor’s Perfected Star, governing boundless transformation. Within it stands a triple-flowered tree, spontaneously birthing the Jade Emperor of the Nine Heavens. Above perches a golden-beaked phoenix, holding a fire bell in its beak. Within shines the natural radiance of the Seven Luminaries. The star possesses nine gates, intersecting the Celestial Market, where a jade terrace and purple palace wander through the Three Yangs. The Perfected, titled the Imperial Perfected Origin Morning Lord, wears the Nine Heavens Dragon Robe, holds the Imperial Insignia, and sits within the purple palace.

The Nine Dippers form the true canopy of the Celestial Culmen, the flowering treasure of the Mystic Axis. Their mechanism turns the Eight Directions, revolving the Nine Degrees, grasping the Great Image, enfolding the Dipper in mist and wrapping the soul to generate the body. To the left, they harness green clouds; to the right, they rein in the crimson dawn, ascending to the Grand Simplicity.

**Seven Stars**
Forty-nine myriad li from Earth, their walls are forged of golden essence and lapis lazuli, their light kindled by the purple radiance of the Seven Luminaries. Within, the multitudes of Heavenly Beings and Perfected Ones roam and feast in these halls. In one day and night, they revolve once like the wheels of the sun and moon. Within also grow seven-jeweled vermilion groves. At the hour of settled meditation, when generative qi first stirs, the Seven Stars undergo refinement in the Palace of Broad Coldness, their luminous purple effulgence mingling with the radiance of the Seven Luminaries. At this moment, the Seven Luminaries blaze and scatter, their essence streaming across the heavens, their purple effulgence spilling forth to irrigate all heavens. Thereupon, the Perfected gather the purple-orchid effulgence and the light of the Seven Luminaries, which transform into seven youths: the first named Pivot Bright, the second Radiant Spirit, the third Northern Origin, the fourth Treasure Essence, the fifth Cinnabar Infant, the sixth Numinous Purity, and the seventh Purple Jade—these are the inner essences of the Seven Treasures, metamorphosed into the Perfected of the Seven Luminaries.

**Supreme Perfected Unity Lord**
In his left hand, he grasps the handle of the Northern Dipper; in his right, the firmness of the Northern Aster. The unmoving star of the Northern Culmen is called Aster Firmness.

**Five Stars**
The spiritual roots of the sun and moon, the five viscera of the Celestial Embryo, the Five Stars formed by the intertwining of celestial essence. When Heaven’s qi fails to nurture, the Three Conjunctions wane and wax.

*The Eight Simplicities Scripture*
**Jupiter**

The Round Mirror is the essence of Wood, the Dark Clarity binds the Yang’s strait.
Within the star are Nine Gates, each gate has a Green Emperor; in all, nine Green Emperors attend and guard the Central Green Sovereign Perfected Lord.
The True Yellow is the Supreme Perfected of the East, the Primordial Essence Celestial Venerable within the Green Emperor’s gate of the Spirit Portal. He is also called the Duke of Green Numinosity, or the Green Spirit, or the Green Essence, or the Lord of the Green Emperor.

**Mars**
The Round Mirror is the essence of Cinnabar, within the star are Three Gates, each gate has a Red Emperor; in all, three Red Emperors attend and guard the Southern Mountain Sovereign Perfected Lord.
The Vermilion Yellow is the Supreme Perfected of the South, the noble spirit of the Cinnabar Palace.
Within this star is the Red Lord, also called the Duke of Red Numinosity, or the Red Spirit, or the Red Essence, or the Lord of the Red Emperor.

**Venus**
The Round Mirror is the essence of Metal, its radiance illumines the Western Spirit.
Within the star are Seven Gates, each gate has a White Emperor; in all, seven White Emperors guard the Supreme August Lord of the West.
The White Sovereign Lord is the Supreme Perfected of the West, the august sovereign of the Grand Simplicity.
Within the gate is the White Emperor Lord, called the Duke of White Numinosity, or the White Spirit, or the White Essence, or the Lord of the White Emperor.

**Mercury**
The Round Mirror is the essence of Water, its penetrating luminance reflects the Northern Abyss.
Within the star are Five Gates, each gate has a Black Emperor; in all, five Black Emperors together guard the Supreme August Lord of the North.
The Dark Perfected August is the Supreme Perfected of the North, the august sovereign of the Grand Mystery. Within the gates are the Black Emperors, called the Duke of Black Numinosity, or the Black Spirit, or the Black Essence, or the Lord of the Black Emperor.

**Saturn**
The Round Mirror is the essence of Earth, it stabilizes and responds to the Yellow Dao.
Within the star are Four Gates, each gate has a Yellow Emperor; in all, four Yellow Emperors attend and guard the Yellow Perfected Lord of Unmoving Stability.
The Central Yellow Supreme August is the loftiest and most revered, the Yellow Emperors within the gates are called the Duke of Yellow Numinosity, or the Yellow Spirit, or the Yellow Essence, or the Lord of the Yellow Emperor.

**Three Luminaries**
They traverse the Dao in their courses, manifest in Heaven and illuminate the Eight Extremities. All stars reside in their places, while the Five Stars scrutinize their transgressions.

Those who cultivate virtue are guarded by the Star of Virtue; those who cultivate martial prowess are guarded by the Star of Valor; those who cultivate gentleness are guarded by the Star of Gentleness; those who cultivate strength are guarded by the Star of Strength; those who cultivate trustworthiness are guarded by the Star of Trust. Alternating by day within the mysteries of the Dark Realm, they abide in the limpid waves of the Celestial River.

The *Nine Heavens’ Chapter of Spirit Generation*—the Crimson Youth crosses the Bitter River. The numinous verses are intricate, the Seven Mysteries ascend the celestial terrace, and the Ten Cycles mount the Han.

The *Seven-Colored Precious Clouds* from the *Cloud Scripture of Life’s Passage*.

The qi of Kunlun Mountain manifests in five colors, as recorded in the *Laozi’s Hidden Scripture*.

**Auspicious Clouds**
Where they gather is called a Cloud Encampment. From the Jade Chamber of Supreme Purity arise the Seven Treasures’ clouds, their hues layered tenfold, their qi fanning in nine directions. Only the Perfected Youth Xuanni may ride these precious clouds to ascend into the Heaven of Jade Purity. The one who wards off evil is the spirit within the Great Tenuity; Xuanni is the spirit of Jade Purity.

When the Lords of the Three Origins set forth on their journey, the bright sun inclines its radiance, the Eight Winds surge through the waves, their joined splendor spanning ninety thousand leagues. High in the empyrean, the dawn dances, crimson clouds spread thickly, and seven-hued yellow clouds gleam.

**Purple Buds Emit Radiance**
Crimson clouds unfurl across the sky, the Three Luminaries shine on high, and all heavens glow with light.

**Nine-Colored Clouds**
Purple and azure clouds, five-hued purple clouds, the Three Pristine clouds, the cinnabar clouds of the Dark Numinous, and the green and blue clouds of the Three Verdant hues—all recorded in the *Yuan Record of Mount Gui*.

**Early Clouds**
Eight Pristine purple clouds, seven Pristine crimson clouds, six qi green clouds, and five Pristine blue clouds, bright and clear—from the *Perfect Scripture of the Great Cavern*.

**Four Assemblies of Auspicious Empyrean**
The Eight Paths blaze with brilliance, the Three Luminaries shine in unison, and the Nine Qi glow with clarity.

**Palace of Nurtured Essence**
Within it lies the Chamber of Supreme Florescence, where blue qi arises, called the Fragrant Smoke of Reversal, its scent carried three thousand leagues against the wind.

The Ten Floral Immortals gather where purple mist congeals into palaces. The Primordial Beginning sings within the azure jade void above the Great Floating Li Land, seated upon the azure clouds.

**The Lord Emperor of the Great Tenuity**
Born within luminous clouds, enwrapped in five-colored clouds, he is also named Jade Emptiness. His true essence solidifies and his fluid consolidates; myriad thoughts revolve through the Dark Clouds, and his contemplation soars through the empyrean to ascend the void. He commands the Dark Dawn across the Ten Heavens, rides the swift lightning to rein in dragons, and through accumulated thought achieves perfection. In due course, he transmits the essentials to the Blue Youth.

**The Five Clouds**
The azure cloud of the East is named Feixu;
The white cloud of the West is named Suxu;
The crimson cloud of the South is named Zhiming;
The black cloud of the North is named Xuanxiang;
The yellow cloud of the Center is named Zongsheng.

Those who know the names of the Five Clouds may summon flying plows. By meditating morning and evening, the Dark Empyrean will come to welcome them, bearing them aloft to ascend into the Grand Purity.

**Auspicious Empyrean’s Double Flight**
Vermilion orchids bloom, streaming cinnabar swirls upward, and jade clouds are infused with essence.

**Verdant Clouds Emit Nectar**
They spread across the great void, purple emptiness congeals into mist, lingering in the cinnabar chamber. The Three Luminaries illumine with penetrating brightness, and the Seven Luminaries stream with light.

**Purple Clouds Illuminate the Emperor’s Seat**
Five clouds illuminate the Nine Mysteries, the Eight Winds arise at the edge of the cosmos, and the profound clarity pervades the green pavilion.

**The Seven-Colored Precious Clouds**
The Elder of the Lower Emperor drinks the mist of the Seven Celestial Spirits and feasts upon the light of the Cavern Heavens.

**The Azure and White Dew**

The Sky Unbroken averts famine years. When Heaven and Earth achieve harmony, sweet dew descends. Drawing from the dark canal’s sweet dew transforms white hair and restores square pupils.

**The Great Cavern**
When yang qi reaches its transformation, snow turns to rain; when yin qi reaches its transformation, rain turns to snow.

**The Crown Prince**
In the northwest stands the Sky-Sustaining Fire—Pillar; wind descending from above brings cold. In the northeast stands the Sky-Sustaining Stone—Pillar; wind descending from above brings frost. In the southeast stands the Sky-Sustaining Fire—Pillar; wind descending from above brings warmth. In the southwest stands the Sky-Sustaining Charcoal—Pillar; ash-laden wind descending from above saps human vitality.

The wind’s banner flutters, whirling canopies dance, jade trees strike resonant tones, and jade-like grasses sound as flutes. When divine winds converge in the four directions, yin and yang achieve harmony, and timely rains pour forth.

When the people long for rain, the Immortal Duke possesses talismans in the village shrine; when Heaven and Earth darken, great rain falls.

**The Northern Realm Below Heaven**
Heaven rains the Eight-Flavored Waters, washing the human body free of filth.

**The Three Sovereigns**
Gentle rain and gentle wind harbor good spirits within. Violent rain and violent wind harbor evil spirits within. Yin qi becomes snow; yang qi becomes rain.

**Thunder Duke**
Surnamed Guo, styled Junwu.

**The Three Sovereigns**
Kan and Li form the north and south.

The thunderbolt’s might is thus achieved. Thunder and lightning are the essence of fire. The Southern Emperor spurs the lightning—"Swiftly expel my defilements, let no poisonous heat assail the cinnabar essence, let the numinous winds prevail."

The Eight Winds play upon the mist, streaming lightning amplifies its power, and the hundred yangs exhale their essence. The Five Elders flank the imperial chariot, the Eight Winds fan from behind, divine lightning leads the way, and jade radiance escorts the wheels. Stirring the hundred yangs gives birth to lightning; drumming the thousand yins releases its might.

**The Great Sage Sovereign**
*Fourth of the Earthly Grades*

Those of earthly talent accumulate yin and congeal dregs, bearing mountains upon their backs. The Most High dons the garb of office.

*The Sutra of Karmic Retribution*

Heaven and Earth: south at *wu*, north at *zi*; east at *mao*, west at *you*. The four void corners lie each ninety million myriad *li* apart. The Earth is ten thousand *li* thick, and beneath it lies the great void’s four corners, where natural golden pillars stand. There are further three thousand six hundred golden axles, each pillar five thousand *li* in girth, all interconnected. The divine winds serve as their strength, thus they can lower the Pleiades and advance or retreat.

*The Inner Transmission of the Perfected*

Earth possesses the Five Powers, the Five Constants of soil—mother of the myriad things.

**The Realm of Zhen’guan**
Its landform resembles an upturned crescent moon.

Beneath Mount Kunlun lie nine earths. Beneath each earth is a layer of water, and beneath each water a layer of wind—thus it continues for nine layers. The present-day tremors of the Earth are the swaying of wind and water. When a ruler achieves great virtue, if grievances and cruelties arise, Heaven and Earth quake in response, and spirits are moved by it.

The Earth is all of glassy lapis, white silver, purple gold, true pearls, and azure jade, interspersed and combined to form palaces of golden millet and the seven treasures.

**The Imperial Domain extends a thousand li**

**Paulownia Parasol Perfected**

Within my Golden Court Abbey, I unharness my steed at the Three Radiance Terrace.

**Supreme Ultimate Perfected**
Plunges nine myriad leagues deep, spanning nine thousand li in breadth. Those who later study and attain the Dao invariably bathe in the Eastern Well before ascending to the Azure Palace of Eastern Florescence. Three paths of yellow qi and solar essence converge.

**Jade Florescence Palace**
Contains a jade well; those who partake gain a lifespan equal to the Three Luminaries.

**Celestial Summit Mountain**
Composed of the Seven Treasures as stone, with aloeswood, storax, benzoin, and turmeric as its flora, lions and pixiu as its beasts, phoenixes and vermilion birds as its fowl. The mountain yields springs of five-hued flowing auroras, and its inhabitants are perfected immortals of wondrous conduct.

**Left of the Heavenly Model**

**Western Tortoise Mountain**
Also called Dragon Mountain, the subtle root of the Nine Heavens, the abyssal府 of myriad qi. Situated at the northwest corner of heaven, it spans four thousand li in circumference, its height bordering Jade Clarity. To the southeast, its towers link the auroras of Yang; above, it adjoins the gates of the Azure Palace’s divine emperors. To the northwest lies the wilderness of Broad Cold; above, it connects to the divine precincts of the Golden Watchtower’s immortals. Southward, it extends to the realm of Great Cinnabar and Pure Profit; its qi harmonizes with the radiance of Cavern Yang. Northward, it points toward the Celestial Net, intersecting the Plain Canopy, its qi traversing the expanse of Vast Spirit.

At its center, it directly pierces the Eight Simplicities Wind Mountain of Jade Capital. Its summit levels with heaven at thirty myriad li. Walls of yellow gold, gates of green jade, golden terraces and jade towers, twelve divine palaces. Above stand halls of spontaneous flowing essence and Purple Watchtowers of Golden Florescence, chambers of jasper and chalcedony. Flanking it are the Nine Caverns; spontaneously arise clouds of purple and white. Cliffs birth purple cassia; ridges flourish with jasper groves. Coral forms its branches; jade is planted as its roots. The *qian* trees bear fruit; red youths and white jade rings appear. The Three Florescence bloom in vermilion splendor; returning fragrance flows through the Great Mystery. Eight qi fan the breezes into ceaseless song; jade zithers resound in the void to form music. Dragons roar on cloud-wreathed peaks; phoenixes cry on soaring crags. Venomous beasts array in the thousands; serpents stretch a thousand fathoms. Divine palaces stand majestic; numinous immortals teem in multitudes. Such is the wondrous transformation of the Primordial Beginning, the sacred root of Heaven’s Origin. *Record of the Tortoise Mountain’s Origin*

Within the Eight Seas lies **Numinous Crow Mountain**, also called **Human Crow Mountain**, all adorned with palaces of the Seven Treasures, terraces of jasper, and chambers of jade.

**Cavern Chambers**
Are the inner palaces within famous mountains; the summits serve as outer palaces. They contain divine medicines of gold, silver, pearls, jade, and nephrite, myriad treasures flourishing in hundreds of thousands of varieties. Lions, divine dragons, simurghs, phoenixes, and qilin roam amidst jade trees and jasper groves. When the pure wind stirs them, it resounds like the *Nine Shao* melody. Aloeswood and storax, a hundred fragrant fumes, waft against the wind for over four thousand li.

**Queen Mother of the West**
Studied the Dao under the Primordial Beginning Great King. After three thousand years, her Dao was perfected, and she returned to Kunlun.

As they departed, they inscribed together upon Human Crow Mountain, characters each eight *zhang* in breadth.

**The Most High on Human Crow Mountain**
Neither celestial nor earthly, neither sinking nor floating,
Primal qi and fiery mist—where the divine truth wanders.
Jade wells, limpid and deep, irrigate without cease;
One hundred twenty palaces connect with the celestial treasuries.
Sun and moon dim and bright, ten thousand stalks of dark *zhi* mushrooms,
Crimson trees rise alone, their fruits all pearls.
White jade towers in jagged splendor, sweet springs gush from the corners,
Flowing leftward in their course.
Jade maidens ascend, purple clouds drifting,
Sweet dew falling in gentle showers.
Golden ground and jade chambers lie within.

*The True Scripture of the Great Cavern*
*The Azure Empyrean’s Empty Song*

The Tree of Nurturing Clarity bears leaves inscribed with purple script. The Golden Root Tree bears fruits of jade essence, its branches inscribed with the thirty-six nations’ tongues and the inner scriptures of all heavens.

*The Foreign Lands’ Dispersed Wonders*

Celestial Summit Mountain is encircled by sevenfold treasure-walled cities, upon which grow Seven Treasures’ Trees, their canopies overspreading the eight directions beyond the walls. Their roots and trunks are of vajra, their branches of patterned jade, their blossoms of bright moon, their leaves of night-glowing radiance, their fruits of giant clamshell, agate, and brain-incense, interspersed with silver, pearls, and jade. Fragrant Trees, Garland Trees, and Melody Trees stand at heights of four *li*, three *li*, two *li*, and one *li*.

*The Three Sovereigns*

In the Non-Directional Realm, trees curve and intertwine, their forms like interlaced dewdrops. Within the Golden Gate stands the Lofty Tree, its yellow qi and yang essence flowing in threefold alignment.

In the Eastern Well’s expanse lies the Hall of Vast Numinosity, where grows the Three-Flowered High-Ringed Tree, towering four thousand *zhang* with branches spanning two thousand *li*. Once in an *effort*, it bears plum-like fruits without pits; those who consume them ascend as flying immortals. Such is the Crimson Tree with cinnabar fruits, whose hues illumine the five viscera.

Where the four yellow waters converge, a single branch of phoenix-brain fruit is planted in a hole one *zhang* deep. After three years, it sprouts a crimson tree like a pine, five or six *chi* tall, its fruits pear-like and white as jade. Eating them grants ascent to the Supreme Subtlety; spittle cast to the ground transforms into azure jade.

*The Purple Writ of the Numinous Book*

Dig eight *chi* into the earth to plant a crimson tree seed, watering it with *huishui*—the elixir of cinnabar. Phoenix-brain is the name of its sap. After three years, a crimson tree resembling a plum grows.

*The Arrayed Records of the Three Heavenly Lords of Highest Clarity*

The cypress is the essence of the Eastern Well, the marshal of ten thousand waters, and the sovereign of a hundred herbs.

*The Mystery Within the Mysteries*

The locust tree is the essence of the Void Star. The privet is the essence of Lesser Yang, its eastern corner formed by the convergence of the four *geng* days and the threefold qi. The plum is the essence of the Encampment Mansion, harmonizing the qi of the east in the first month; the jade among trees, it blooms before all others. The mulberry is the essence of the Winnowing Basket.

The cornelian cherry is the essence of the Great Fire and Heart Star. It grows in mountain ravines and marshes, its square stems bearing leaves in opposing pairs, resembling the union of yin and yang.

The grain tree is the essence of the Horn Mansion.

The Seven Treasures’ blossoms and fruits compose the scriptures and texts of the Three Caverns of Supreme Clarity. Those who consume these blossoms and fruits become Radiant Golden Immortals.

The Water Essence Mountain lies north of a small sea that flows into the great ocean. There is also a layered mountain, four thousand *li* high, upon which water rests. Its base is golden sand, and five-colored lotuses, large as wheels, exude a juice like honey when pierced.

The blossoms of the Azure Forest are the flowers of the sun’s essence and the threefold *qi*.

*The Nine Vermilion Talismans of the Five Emperors and the Inner Perfected of the Supreme*

The blossoms of the Triply Converging Intertwined Dragons

*The Arrayed Records of the Three Heavenly Lords of Highest Clarity*

The sprouting of the hundred herbs

*The Scripture of the Supreme on Karmic Retribution in the Womb*

The Supreme Thearch plucks the medicines of the Azure Forest

*The Perfect Scripture of the Great Cavern*

Water springs avoid the solid and return to the void; in the north, the high flows downward. Five-colored waters emerge from Renwu Mountain, yielding the flowing liquid of returning souls.

Emerald waves soar from the azure sea as nine dragons rise abreast.

The waters of the Weaving Girl of the Eastern Pole extend westward to the Long Dusk of Yuanyuan.

Divine Mushroom Water governs the revolutions of heaven and earth.

The Heavenly River sways and trails across the sky.

*The Dispelling of Demons*

The jade essence of swirling waters, the sapphire droplets of the falling spring—
Rinsing and sipping at Dongmeng, dwelling in joy by the Canglang,
the Feminine One, the Venerable Lord.

The Mountain of the Great Thearch bears the Nine-Windowed Gate of the Mystic Gullet. Beyond lies the Abyss of Sweet Springs and Jade Nectar. In the north, the Mystic [realm] nourishes the heavens with five-colored *qi*. Below lies the Abyss of Longevity, and within dwells the home of the Supreme.

The Five Thearchs release golden dragons into the Pure and Cold Abyss. The Lord of the Numinous Treasure and Great Dao illumines the dragon’s patterns upon the Azure Abyss.

The Divine King of the Eastern Sea’s Water Thearchs—
Surname: Kai, personal name: Neiling—rides a scaled dragon, soaring upon cloud chariots.

The Divine King of the Western Sea’s Water Thearchs—
Surname: Dao, personal name: Dongqing—rides a flying chariot of plain mist.

The Divine King of the Northern Sea’s Water Thearchs—
Surname: Pen, personal name: Yuanyuan—rides a flying chariot of dark mist.

Beneath the Brocade-Woven Terrace lies the Sea of Myriad Fordings.

*The Jade Scripture of the Great Cavern*

The Eastern Sea—
Surname: He, title: Lord of Return.

The Southern Sea—
Surname: Liu, personal name: Xiaojun.

The Western Sea—
Surname: Li, personal name: Rilai.

The Northern Sea—
Surname: Wu, personal name: Qinqiang.

The River Earl—
Surname: Feng, personal name: Yi, courtesy name: Pingjun—rules over water.

The wise fear neither wind nor wave, neither hunger nor thirst.

The Azure-Gem Stream of the Heaven-Mirror Land—
Above the Land of Nothingness grows the fivefold mushrooms of the Mystic Gorge. Those who drink its waters share the lifespan of heaven and earth. Within dwell thirty thousand immortals who drink this water.

In the Center of the Primordial Heaven lies the Flowing Gush Pool, a thousand *li* wide, its waters fragrant and sweet. Within grow jade trees and ten-*zhang* lotuses of gold. Immortals dwell among the lotuses, and those who drink this water find their five viscera clarified and their faces wreathed in purple clouds.

North of the Mystic Province lies the Emperor’s River, where the Jade Nymph Immortal and the Golden Lotus Immortal Maidens often wander.

The Western Na Jade Land—
Its Golden Essence Jade Pool is where flying heavenly immortals bathe thrice yearly.

The Cold Pool of Yushan Land spans five hundred *li* and contains the flowing essence of jade mushrooms. The men and women of this land drink the pool’s water, their faces like jade.

The Seven Treasures Pool of the Pure Harmony Land—
Within dwell black crows, azure-white, red, yellow, and green birds, as well as kingfishers and emerald phoenixes. Their songs are wondrous, and all who hear them awaken the heart of the Dao.

Within the Golden Gate lies the pool of golden essence refinement. It contains stone-shadow golden marrow, jade cream, cinnabar mushrooms, yellow *qi*, and yang essence—three currents flowing in harmony.

The Night Radiance Liquid—
The hymns and poems of the assembled perfected.

Within the Hall of Vast Spirit—
Beneath flows the Azure Mushroom Jade Cream Spring, where the Spirit King of Yang Valley drinks.
The Ten Thousand Emperors of the Upper Immortals—
On the day of Autumn’s Beginning, they bathe in the Eastern Well Spring.

The Ten-Thousand-*Zhang* Valley—
Beneath Mount Luo Deng lies the prison of ghosts and spirits.

*The Golden Mystery Feathered Chapters*—
The Jade Nectar Spring governs the revolutions of Heaven and Earth.

The Five-Colored Flowing Spring arises upon an island—
Amidst the Azure Sea, west of Fusang’s waters, it borders Penglai, where the blossoms of immortals grow. Here dwell tens of thousands of transcendents.

Zu Island—
East of Fusang, within the Eastern Sea, holds the elixir of immortality. The immortal officials gather and consume it, their faces aglow with flowing radiance after a hundred years.

Long Island—
Also called Green Mound, it lies in the *chen-si* region of the Southern Sea, beyond the bounds of the celestial void.

Yan Island—
At the heart of the Southern Sea, where flames accumulate and touch the heavens.

Liu Island—
In the southern reaches of the Western Sea, where tens of thousands of transcendents reside. It yields the stone of Kunwu, which tempers iron into steel—its brilliance piercing and luminous, like crystal cutting jade as if it were earth.

Xuan Island—
Beyond the Land of the Heavenly Mirror, where the Chamber of the Supreme Mystery is governed by the True Lord, the Immortal Earl of the Great Mystery.

Seven-jeweled hues surge into the heavens—
Veiling sun and moon.

*The Sutra of Karmic Retribution*—
The Heaven of Supreme Beginning.

Amidst this, the Night of Auspicious Origin—
The river named the Ford of Transcendent Crossing.

Jade flutes sing upon the clouds—
Phoenixes cry through the ninefold depths.

Golden bridges and silver pillars,
Atop lapis lazuli terraces,
Seven-jeweled balustrades,
Shimmering and radiant,
Illumine the abyssal waters below.

*The Scripture of the Dao and Its Treasured Mysteries, Scroll Two* concludes.
*The Scripture of the Dao and Its Treasured Mysteries, Scroll Three*
**Chapter Five: On Life and Death**

**In the Womb for Nine Months**
Nine qi coalesce into form,
Spirit and body complete.

**The Tenth Month: Birth**
The Nine Heavens rejoice.
The Great Unity holds the talisman,
The Thearch confers destiny.
The Director of Fates fixes one’s allotted years,
The Five Thearchs oversee birth.

Humans receive the harmonious qi of yin and yang,
And the nature of the Five Phases.

*From the* Inner Chapters of the Mysterious and Wondrous:
The Nine Heavens’ Venerable One addressed the Jade Lads of the Three Heavens, saying:
“The Two Images embrace the true,
Above corresponding to the Nine Mysteries.
Flowing cinnabar undergoes nine transformations,
Qi congeals into essence.
The essence of the Nine Heavens
Becomes the immortal embryo of the human body.
Six wisdoms gestate within the womb,
Modeled upon the Five Numinous Powers—
Together, thirty-six thousand spirits.”

Humans are the dwelling-place of virtue and power—
Thus the divine and human alike are bound by precepts.

**The Fivefold Dao of Spirit and Form**
*From the* Original Birth of Laozi:
“Three Passes guard the Way.”

The Seven Mysterious Fluids course through the meridians,
Sun and moon illuminate the Six Voids.
Mouth and eyes govern their numinous vessels—
Such is the human Dao.

Clouds drift and rain descends,
The Five Causes reach completion.
The Five Causes are the Five Spirits.
The Three Paths are the Three Perfected,
The august deities of the Three Ones.

The Great One is named Wu You Shou,
Styled Gui Hui Chang.
Those who comprehend this attain long life and avert ten thousand calamities,
As jade maidens descend in welcome.

The spirit of the Upper Qi of the Three Primes
Is the Lord of Left Non-Being.
The hun and po are born in the Palace of the Nine Numinosities,
While the divine fluid circulates through the perfection of the Three Qi.
Its ruler is titled the White Prime Cavern Yang Lord,
Also called Vermilion Essence.

The Central Controller of Destiny,
Also known as the Lifespan-Regulating Venerable,
Or Spirit Ancestor, or Numinous Flower.
The Peach Lord of the Gate of Destiny
Is the primal resource of Heaven and Earth,
The numinous ancestor of yin and yang.
The Pass of Gold and Jade, the treasure of the chamber’s portal—
All are governed by the qi of the Peach Lord.

The Three and Five intermingle,
Transforming to give birth to the Five Spirits.
They receive the great numen of the Five Qi,
And the mysterious ancestor of destiny’s tally.

All beings that contain qi
Are born through the Primordial Granary.

*From the* Upper Record of the Primordial Granary:
The Six Dusts—
**Form-dust**: green, yellow, red, white, black, perceived by the eyes.
**Sound-dust**: gong, shang, jue, zhi, yu, perceived by the ears.
**Fragrance-dust**: rank, scorched, fragrant, fishy, putrid, perceived by the nose.
**Flavor-dust**: bitter, sweet, pungent, sour, salty, perceived by the mouth.
**Touch-dust**: soft, rough, light, heavy, firm, slippery, dry, damp, cold, warm, perceived by the body.
**Dharma-dust**: generates mental consciousness; when the mind turns toward dust, the five senses become distinct perceptions, hence the name "distinct dusts."

The Four Great Elements—
Earth, water, fire, wind,
Four principles combining with the four dusts,
Thus named the Four Great Elements.

The Six Houses—
The Wood Spirit of Jia Yin governs hair and bones,
The Metal Spirit of Jia Shen governs teeth and nails,
The Earth Spirit of Jia Xu governs flesh and muscle,
The Wind Spirit of Jia Chen governs breath and respiration,
The Fire Spirit of Jia Wu governs warmth and moisture,
The Water Spirit of Jia Zi governs moisture and luster.
The Six Harmonies together form the human body.

The Wood Spirit becomes the liver,
The Fire Spirit the heart,
The Earth Spirit the spleen,
The Metal Spirit the lungs,
The Water Spirit the kidneys,
The Wind Spirit the gallbladder.
Thus there are the five viscera and six bowels,
Nine palaces and twelve chambers,
One hundred eighty mechanisms,
Three hundred sixty joints,
Four limbs and five constituents,
Triple burner and six trunks—
All in imitation of Heaven and Earth.

*From the* Inner Chapters of the Mysterious and Wondrous:
The Six Roots—
Ear, eye, nose, mouth, body, intent.

*From the* Western Ascent:
The Five Roots—
Primordial wisdom, right contemplation, liberation.

The Five Substances—
Harmonized to form the provisional name "human."

Within the jadelike womb and purple chamber,
The Nine Elixirs ascend and transform amid the fetal sac,
Following the qi of the Nine Heavens.
The purple net binds the embryo—
By karmic destiny, the immortal is born.

*From the* Jade Book of the Grand Empyrean:
The Sun Mother,
Elder Mother of Jade Purity,
Supreme deity governing the fetal sac.

*From the* Jade Scripture of the Great Cavern:
The Primordial Purple-and-White Sovereign Lady
Entrusts the jadelike womb to the purple sac,
Enfolding emptiness and elegance within the jade chamber.

The Heavenly Venerable, Great Sage—
From the outset, the place of rebirth is the jadelike palace,
Luminous within and without,
Abiding in karmic retribution within the womb.

Twenty-eight layers of fruition—
The transformed body emerges naturally,
By the seventh month, form gradually changes,
By the tenth month, sound and voice are complete.

Cloud Mist Adept—
Scion of the Primordial Emperor’s void qi,
Middle son of the Great Emperor,
Embracing the jadelike womb within the jade chamber,
Weaving cloud essence at the golden gate,
Enclosing sun and moon within the purple sac,
Transforming vast dew to congeal the spirit.
On the first day of the third month in the ninth year of the Upper Emperor,
Dawn breaks at Heaven’s Radiance,
Born above the Nine Mysteries in the Heaven of Boundless Treasure,
Beholding the great sun at Cloud Cliff,
Radiating golden countenance from the jadelike pavilion,
Aligning with the imperial foundation in the celestial plan,
Emulating jade elegance from the natural,
Bathed in the radiance of the Nine Numinous,
Anointed with sweet and fragrant jade springs,
Nourished by seven-colored numinous mushrooms,
Fed with nine-times-refined flying frost.
Divine dragons flank his sides,
Jade phoenixes shade his crown,
Purple mist arises above,
Flowing light glows in the neighboring realms.
The Two Symbols temper his strength,
The Three Luminaries harmonize his authenticity.
The divine continent sings of his wonder,
Seven transformations alter his spirit,
Void winds hasten his form,
Returning fragrance disperses his dust.
High in the vast emptiness,
By the misty shores of the Cavernous Waves.

*From the* Jade Book of the Grand Empyrean:
The Dao’s root—Nine Heavens’ Primordial Father.

His form spans seventy million *zhang*.
In spring, he dons the Jade Rage, clad in the Nine Heavens’ phoenix robe of cloud-and-crow, ever riding the azure mist’s flying chariot, attended by twelve winged dragons.
In summer, he wears the Nine Suns’ robe of crimson phoenix and tiger-patterned armor; in autumn, he girds the Warm Dragon Abyss sword; in winter, he transforms into the radiance of solar essence, merging with the purple glow to blend the qi of the primal Chaos and the Two Symbols.

The Dao’s apex—Nine Heavens’ Mysterious Mother—
spans seventy million *zhang*, attended by twelve phoenixes and thirty-six immortals, who bear the essence of the moon and ride twelve-hued clouds.

The Jade Numinous Immortal Mother of the Supreme addressed the Azure Youth:
Before the Prime Minister of Crimson Light, we were born together at the gate of the King’s realm.

The Nine Palaces’ Perfected Ones, *The Original Conduct*:
Eight Sceneries unite in perfection, nine emperors share luminance.
Southward, floating profits; northward, the Cold Palace falls.
Auspicious clouds layer in profound mystery, four directions interflow.
Sacred peaks are no common abode—flying clouds are my dragons.

*The Jade Book*:
Friends are all Perfected Ones;
jade youths are his household.
Ascending into the Grand Clarity, he is the Supreme’s honored guest.
Alone he strides the Three Realms—
the five phases’ qi clash,
the Three Luminaries lose their measure,
yin and yang rage in conflict,
the eight nodes fall into discord,
and thus ten thousand maladies arise.

The ancients alone grasped Heaven and Earth’s intent;
the middle era grasped half;
the latter era grasps nothing.
Within the body’s thirty-nine portals—

*The Arrayed Records of the Three Heavenly Lords of Highest Clarity*:
Revolving through the Three Paths, traversing the Five Roads,
all share the road of death,
vague and dim in the nether gloom.
The Grand Clarity’s Perfected One, Yin Xi, had eyes of solar essence,
his head bore the circular radiance,
his five viscera bore script,
his face bore the seven stars,
above emulating celestial patterns,
below conforming to earthly principles—
thus states *The Inner Transmission of the Primordial Perfected One*.

Within the head are the Nine Palaces and Five Peaks’ immortal lords and brain spirits,
attended by a thousand chariots and ten thousand riders in azure robes,
each one inch and two *fen* in stature.

The Supreme’s Purple Azure Left Primordial Lord—
guards the head and face’s domain, barring all malevolent spirits.

The Brow Spirit, Yuan Guang, is the Great Numinous Lord.
Laozi observed the celestial patterns.
The central brow is the White Primordial’s canopy of blossoms,
the Supreme’s Pure Numinous Emperor,
also named Seven Numinous, also named Divine Script.
One guards the space between the brows.

*The Perfect Scripture of the Great Cavern*:
The Eye Spirits are Dao-keeping youths,
three inches in stature, clad in five colors, golden perfection and jade radiance.
The left eye’s youth is named Mystic Light,
the right eye’s youth is named Heroic Brightness.
The eyes are the Supreme’s sun and moon, the Pure Numinous.

The right eye’s youth, named Morning Infant,
oversees the Heavenly Pass, surveys the imperial court,
dwelling in the Three Dawns, riding the turning cycles.
The left eye’s youth, named Flying Spirit,
mystically boundless, gazes upon jade essence’s brilliance,
like celestial might unleashing streaming stars.

*The Scripture of Treasured Radiance*:
The nose is named Mountain Source,
also called Ghost Well, Ghost Pool, Root of Evil, Terrace of the Soul.

*The Perfect Scripture of the Great Cavern*:
The nose is the Three Primordials’ mountain range.

The Mouth Spirit is the Heavenly One Lord, named Cinnabar Vermilion,
serving as the Bright Hall’s official.
The mouth is the Vermilion Palace’s cinnabar abyss.

*The Pure Numinous*:
The Tongue Spirit is the Dao’s forked essence,
seven inches in length, clad in vermilion.
The teeth are the Stomach Palace’s mighty power.

*The Pure Numinous*:
The tongue is the Primordial Hero’s dragon axle,
the Supreme’s Minor Youth facing the Perfected Emperor,
settling beneath the tongue to channel the fluid’s source.

*The Scripture of Treasured Radiance*:
The Ear Spirits are the Delicate Maiden,
also named Jade Hall’s official,
the Nine Mysteries’ Perfected One, named Universal Controller,
dwelling in the right ear—spirit of wisdom,
eavesdropping across ten thousand leagues,
entering the boundless palace’s abode,
lush with immortal emperors,
their positions instructing the destined measure,
their mandates aligning with celestial tally.
The Sovereign One’s soul, named Supreme Return,
dwells in the left ear, governing all mechanisms,
three merging as one, equal in radiance.

The ears are the Emperor Lord’s gates of hearing.
Those who hear golden tones and jade sounds—true qi enters;
those who hear the sounds of stringed music—the Six Ding Jade Maidens come to guard.

The Supreme’s Revered Spirit returns to the Flourishing Assembly,
guarding my jade pillow.

*The Perfect Scripture of the Great Cavern*:
The Cinnabar Emperor moves the pearl,
the Vermilion Palace’s spirit,
filling the great hammer’s edge at the nape’s center.

The Yellow Plain’s Middle Primordial Lord, named Round Blossom Yellow Blade—
guards my chest and abdomen’s domain,
subduing demonic spirits, annihilating the Three Corpses’ forms.
One Perfected of Heaven.
The spirit is tranquil and serene.

Dwells in the chest’s center, governing all matters of life and inquiry.
Clad in brocade robes, soaring azure skirts,
for the adept they extend destiny, sealing the gate of death.
Containing radiance, they join the Nine Mysteries.
Below, they guard the back; radiance gathers in the Central Field.
Spirit Child Qi Ling,
also named Kunlun, also named Great Abyss.

Left: Wu Ying Duke’s Son,
styled He Fu Zi.
Also called Primordial Essence Lord, also called Divine Duke’s Son.
Guards my left armpit, the liver’s rear gate.

Right: Bai Yuan Cavern Yang Lord,
also named Vermilion Essence, also named Qi Cheng.
Guards my right flank, the lung’s rear gate.

*The Perfect Scripture of the Great Cavern*:
The Two Cheek Spirits,
styled Dao Cheng, four inches and one fen in length.
They grasp the essence of the Great Yang,
styled Po Shang.
Within the sun, the Controller of Destiny, named Jie Sheng,
dwells in the adept’s right hand’s four great [vessels], named Five Flowers.
Preserving the true, placing the numinous,
they tend the sun and moon, swallowing primordial essence.

The Sun’s Peach Lord, named Fang Ying,
dwells in the adept’s left hand,
wielding the Dipper stars, upholding Heaven’s Ridge,
commanding the Five Spirits, traversing forty degrees,
weaving the Celestial Court, circling thrice,
the Nine Caverns pure and bright.

The Foot Spirit, essence of the Great Yin—
the feet are the numinous gateway of the kidney’s origin.

Visualizing beneath each foot, twin white dragons emerge, stationed to my left and right. *The Central Scripture of the Nine Perfected*:

The Throat Spirit,
named Bai Liu Fang, styled Dao Tong.
*The Three Heavens’ Method of Nurturing the Five Radiances*:
Within the adept’s throat, it grasps the wondrous scroll.
In the womb’s primordial unity, the task is the Mysterious Child;
the Supreme One’s essence-soul, the Mysterious Returning Child,
guards the adept’s five viscera, ensuring deathlessness.

The Lung’s Youth, named Su Ming,
purifies the adept’s lung-gate within and without,
dispersing the wandering soul and scattered po to Huang Ning.

The heart like a gibbon, or like leaping flame—
*The Supreme Scripture of the Eight Simplicities*:
The heart as the Yang mechanism.
For the perfected entering mountains, this is essential.

The Supreme One’s Five Spirits,
once merged as one, transform into a great spirit dwelling in the heart,
styled the Celestial Essence-Fluid Lord.

The Vermilion Lord spreads true [qi]—
crimson clouds swirl and refine, five paths and four nodes,
emptily soaring, flowing with the true; revering the numinous spirits,
irrigating the eight encircling [realms], the Red Child bearing the radiance,
all spirits converge in submission.

The heart’s palace receives essence, the five palaces brightly open.
The Dao conjoins to form immortality; the four limbs lightly soar,
the Five Thearchs flank and reflect, ascending into Purple Tenuity.

*The Primordial Record of Mount Tortoise*:
Within the Crimson Palace of the heart’s cinnabar field,
the Central One, the Primordial Sovereign of the Cinnabar,
spiritually moves the pearl, styled Zi Nan Dan,
also named Sheng Shang Bo, also called Shi Yun Ju.

The gallbladder as the Purple Chamber Palace—
the spirit named Long De Ju.

*The Seven Perfected’s Yang Passage of Life-Years*:
Guarding the adept’s five viscera and great stomach,
vermilion blossoms and jade mushrooms naturally overflow and fill.

The Great Yang’s radiant essence—
jade cassia luminously connects, the six qi flow and spread,
illuminating the vermilion court; the qi-palace interpenetrates the true,
the six stomachs flourish with blossoms.

The Lord of Crimson Qi in the Blood—
the Controller of Destiny and the essence-soul spirits,
together guard the blood of the hundred passes.

Golden bones and jade names—
the purple script of Supreme Purity, when fully attained, summons the numinous;
the talisman for summoning the numinous is the talisman of
the Seven Origins’ Liberation.

The Third Perfected of the Bone Joints,
named Jian Li Jun, styled Yi Yu Mei.

The Supreme One knocks the teeth seven times—
for the path of the Ten Luminaries.

Five exhalations to sever the five sufferings of sentient beings.
*The Scripture of Ascending the Mysterious*:

Knocking the teeth, the great resounding of Heaven’s Drum—
summons celestial perfected ones, convenes the immortals of Wei.
Strike Heaven’s Bell on the left, beat Heaven’s Drum on the right,
warding off demonic calamities, a hundred blessings arrive.

*The Hidden Commentary on the Supreme Ultimate’s True Cuckoo*:

One inhalation, one exhalation—
three knocks for goodness.

Flicking the fingers summons the Ten Heavens.
*The Scripture of Ascending the Mysterious*

As one walks the mountains to gather herbs,
with each step, a resonant cough—like the sounding of a chime.

The Primordial Heavenly Worthy commands:
"Let the Two Lords of the Mysterious Unity open the Seven-Step Wondrous Radiance Jade Treasury within the Purple Net,
and reveal the *Golden Writs of Fixed Life*,
bestowing them upon the Supreme Void’s Primordial High Daoist Lords."

Reciting a chapter of the *Riverbank Perfected One*
summons the Most High’s Jade Capital;
all the Heavenly Immortals clasp their hands in praise.

Paying homage to the Azure Lad of Eastern Florescence—
three bows facing north to seek one’s desired divine transcendence,
performed on a *ding-mao* day.

The day the Longevity Bone is born,
the day the Dao of Immortality is accomplished—
such are the Master’s decreed teachings.

The Heavenly Worthy commands the Marshal of the Nine Heavens
to present the *Jade Writs of the Nine Heavens’ Life-Generation*.

The Four Supplements take their places,
the Five Elders oversee the perfected;
the Great One commands the Jade Emperor to intone the covenant,
standing tall facing south,
to deliver them to the Limitless Flying Heavenly Divine Kings.

The Heavenly Worthy confers the scriptures upon the Most High Daoist Lord—
the Guardian of the Way.
Lady Wang of the Supreme Perfected holds the Ten Mystic Spirit Ribbons below,
the Jade Lads of Scripture-Attendants stand to the left,
the Marshal of Supervision and Salvation to the right.
The True Kings of the Nine Heavens hold the Nine-Colored Standards at the center.
The Primordial Lords return the tally thrice;
the myriad spirits arrive as one.
The True Kings face east,
turning the standards thrice in praise.

The Heavenly Worthy rises;
all the Heavenly Great Sages, Perfected Ones, and Jade Maidens bow in unison.
*Golden Essence of the Simplified Writs*

The Heavenly Perfected descend,
the Dao’s qi shines resplendent.
Paying homage to the Three Origins,
attending the Jade Purity,
ascending its terrace,
beholding the divine forms.

The Heavenly Worthy gazes heavenward and smiles—
from his mouth issue two hues of qi, azure and yellow-red,
their radiance piercing the ten directions,
leaving no darkness, no concealment.
Golden scripts in purple characters,
jade texts in cinnabar writs,
glorious within the Three Qi.
The Three-Eight Luminous Spirits,
the Twenty-Four Perfected,
each accompanied by a thousand chariots and ten thousand riders,
hover above the Void’s Mystery,
guarding the numinous writs.
*The Twenty-Four Generations*

The Most High and Lofty Perfected One
shines with a golden countenance, smiling.
Roaming the cloud-lattices,
treading the void to pace the Mysterious Record,
traversing the dust through kalpas.

The Primordial Beginning’s Wisdom of Right Contemplation and Liberation.
The Most High Dao Lord sits upon a great lotus,
while all the heavenly perfected immortals and the great assembly,
each and every one, manifest myriad lotus blossoms—
on every petal, the lands of the ten directions appear,
and within each flower, their kingdoms, courts, and palaces are revealed.

The Dao is that by which heaven is aligned and earth is rectified:
the White Tiger dwells in the West, the Primordial Qi in the North.

The Azure Emperor of the East,
whose constant name is Jing Meng,
wears a robe of azure over a jasper-green brocade flying skirt,
girded with a sash of interwoven kingfisher plumes and numinous cords.
He rides a cloud-chariot of nine azure dragons,
attended by twelve Jade Maidens of the Azure Waist,
each bearing blossoms of the verdant forest,
along with nine-colored staff-banners,
as he roams the Eastern Marchmount.

The Vermilion Emperor of the South,
whose surname is Tu and whose name is Dong Dan,
wears a cloud-brocade robe and a skirt of cinnabar script,
adorned with the talisman of the Southern Culmen,
girded with the Eight Radiant Lights of the Vermilion Palace sword.
He rides a flying wheel of crimson mist,
attended by twelve Jade Maidens of the Great Cinnabar,
each bearing the solar essence’s threefold qi blossoms,
as he roams the Southern Marchmount.

The White Emperor of the West,
whose surname is Hun and whose name is Zhi Gui,
wears a crown of sevenfold luminous qi,
a robe of white brocade and a flying skirt of cloud-light embracing plain silk.
He rides a cloud-chariot of pristine white,
attended by twelve Jade Maidens of the Great Simplicity,
each mounted upon a white tiger,
as he roams the Western Marchmount.

The Black Emperor of the North,
whose surname is Xuan and whose name is Shuo Meng,
wears a robe of black brocade,
girded with the divine transforming sword of patterned body.
He rides a flying cloud-chariot,
attended by twelve Jade Maidens of the Great Mystery,
mounted upon flying tortoises,
as he roams the Northern Marchmount.

The Yellow Emperor of the Center,
whose surname is Ma and whose name is Zhong Shun,
wears a robe of yellow brocade and a flying skirt of mysterious yellow cloud-brocade.
He rides a cloud-chariot of golden hue,
attended by twelve Jade Maidens of the Yellow Simplicity,
each mounted upon a flying unicorn.

The August Jade Emperor above,
adorned with golden tiger and phoenix patterns,
girded with the divine tiger jade seal,
abides within the luminous jade cavern.
In his hands he holds the Dipper Star,
beneath the canopy of blossoming clouds,
standing upon the purple mist,
within the Purple Void.

*The Record of Mount Gui* states:

When the Perfected Lord manifested in the world,
phoenixes became household fowl,
and qilins and lions became domestic beasts.
As the Great Assembly neared, the True One emerged—
the grand convocation was held west of Chang’an and Luoyang,
by the banks of the Yellow River and the Marsh of Beneficent Moisture.

The heart is the sagely sovereign of humanity,
a spirit of Heaven and Earth,
sharing the same qi as the sun,
dwelling within the five viscera—
most revered of all.

The Primordial Heavenly King
was born amid the space of the Hollow Cavern,
after seven thousand kalpas,
when Heaven brightened and qi cleared,
and the twin radiances wove their meridians.
The Mysterious Void and Purple Canopy illumined his name,
while the lightning of the Six Qi bore his true form aloft.
Alone he held the tally of the Numinous Talisman,
his jade chariot and wheel of mystery,
his lordly brush and the essence of the Dark Dragon,
flowing and gleaming through the halls of the Lightning Void.
He journeyed east to the realm of Azure Waters and Luxuriant Forests,
rested above in the Nine-Bend Chambers of Blue Mist,
and ascended afar to the Golden Portal,
where he received his title as Lord of Jade Purity.

The Heavenly Son of the Great Ultimate
was once a minor official.
Through yielding and deference, he ascended to rule the world—
the Heavenly Son of the Central Ultimate.
The Ninth Heavenly King
descended to transform and be born as a Son of Heaven.
The world rejoiced greatly, none failed to submit to his rule,
and the Primal Chaos was unified—
a sovereign of supreme virtue.
The warp became emperors, the weft empresses;
the Nine August Perfected Lords,
keepers of the Upper Clarity’s sacred prohibitions,
preside over the Three Primordials of Jade Flower.

The Supreme Unity Lord of the Upper Primordial
governs the ten thousand immortals,
oversees the true qi of the Marchmounts,
removes the registers of death,
and inscribes the registers of life.

The White Primordial Lady
treasures the Dao of the five viscera,
wears a white brocade cloak adorned with dragon patterns,
and a crown of purple canopy and hibiscus.

The Yellow Primordial Lady of Lofty Radiance
possesses a body of golden essence,
and wears a crown of purple-flowered hibiscus.

The Purple Primordial Lady
dons a tiger-patterned cloak of purple brocade,
a skirt of purple dragon designs,
a hibiscus crown of the Purple Dawn,
and a canopy of twin purple-pearl stars.

The Lady of the Upper Primordial
is the mother of the Three Heavenly Perfected Saints,
commanding the names of the Jade Maidens of the Ten Directions.
She wears a green robe with a crimson frost-patterned gown,
bears a fiery jade of six or seven hues,
and wields a sword of flowing yellow essence.

From *The Inner Transmission of Lord Mao*:
The Lady of the Purple Tenuity,
surnamed Wang and named Qing’e,
is the twentieth daughter of the Queen Mother of the West.
Her Purple Tenuity Palace lies beyond the Northern Desert,
in the Feather Bright Wilds of Mount Xuanlong,
east-northeast of Kunlun.
The Lady of the Purple Tenuity spoke to the Queen Mother, saying:
*"Round in form yet square in radiance,
square in essence yet bearing softness.
Radiance conceals within form,
essence hides within image.
Radiance is crimson, image is yellow—
these are the treasures of sun and moon.
If one knows this Dao,
one may exhale and inhale the flowing mist.
At dawn, ingest the sun’s qi;
at midnight, gather the moon’s splendor and store it.
Withdraw it nine inches before your face,
letting its light and radiance illuminate your Mud-Pill Palace,
descending to the five viscera,
permeating the entire body."*

From *The Hidden Scripture of the Cavern of Perfection*:
The Lady Attendant of the Central Candidate.

The Master of the Great Cyclic Wind and Primordial Fusion, the Lady of the Purple Tenuity, is the preceptor of the *Great Cavern Perfection Scripture*. The Lady is also called "Little Youth," signifying that the ignorant and unlearned rely upon the Great Lord. Later, the Sage Lord, Grand Master Peng, established the Ministry of the Square Cauldron; the Lord of the Azure Youth ascended to protect the Palace of Great Cinnabar; the Primordial Lord of the Southern Culmen transmitted the Office of White Mountain; the Perfected Lord of Primordial Simplicity governed the Office of the Western City. The Perfected King of Totality, one master with four assistants. The assistants—left aide and right minister, front counselor and rear chancellor—along with the four or five diviners and observers, all serve the assisting master.

When divine beings govern, perfected ones serve as ministers; when perfected ones govern, immortals serve as ministers. In high antiquity, sage emperors and kings served as ministers. Those who employ the words of sages share virtue with Heaven and Earth and harmonize their hearts with the divine spirits.

The Heavenly Great General, surnamed Wang, named Yang, styled Ziling, wears a crimson unlined robe.

From *The Central Scripture of Laozi’s Successive Treasuries*:
The Left General, surnamed Tang, named Hong, styled Shiming, stands seventy-two *zhang* tall. His countenance is red, he wears a great crown, and in his left hand he holds a golden tally, commanding an army of thirty million.

From *The Five Thousand Characters of Lord Lao*:
The Central General.

The Central General, surnamed Zhou, named Wu, styled Wengang, stands eighty-one *zhang* tall. In his left hand he holds the jade tally of Yang, commanding an army of thirty million.

The Right General, surnamed Ge, named Yong, styled Wendu, stands seventy-two *zhang* tall. In his right hand he holds a jade halberd, commanding an army of thirty million.

The Azure Dragon General stands eighty-one *zhang* tall, wielding bow and arrows.

The Yellow Court General stands seventy-two *zhang* tall, grasping the *Kuigang*.

The White Tiger General stands thirty-six *zhang* tall, bearing a drawn crossbow.

The Fire Star General stands sixty-four *zhang* tall, sounding the battle horn.

The Dark Warrior General stands twenty-five *zhang* tall, striking bells and drums.

The Supreme Microcosmic Lord commands the Supreme Ultimate Immortal to soothe the Nine Flowers with resounding bells.

Those whose rank attains to the Immortal Ministers serve the Three Sovereigns.

The Scripture-Attending Immortal Gentlemen—Wang Sizhen, Kong Wenqi, and Liu Wenjing—are dispatched by the command of the Supreme Ultimate Perfected One.

From *The Scripture of the Supreme Perfected One’s Spontaneous Oneness*:

The Jade Lads of the Three Heavens Above Emptiness wear seven-changing brocade robes of azure and yellow, seated upon clouds of twelve hues with a hundred shifting radiance. In their hands they hold nine-jointed golden staves, their light entwining like the brilliance of sun and moon.

The Jade Morn Lads—three thousand attend and guard.

The Writ of Myriad Spirits Hidden—concealed by the Highest Jade Emperor in the Jade Purity Upper Palace’s Jasper Chamber.

Five hundred Golden Immortals and Jade Lads attend incense, bearing luminous treasures and scattering the Three Qi’s returning incense flowers.

The Jade Maiden Cui Zhu Qiong carries the light into the Golden Chamber.

From *The Twenty-Four Images of Life*:

The Jade Maiden E’rong Taidan—her hair bound in a cloud-like coil, clad in crimson robes and flying skirts.

From *The Immortals of the Five Peaks*:

The Upper Palace Golden Flower Jade Maidens—seven hundred attend the Immortal Mother, tasked with governing the flowing essence of the Purple Watchtower’s Golden Chamber and Jasper Hall. Thrice each month they ascend to Jade Purity, twice feasting on Kunlun.
