From *The Hidden Records of Laozi*:

The Jade Purity Emperor Lord commands the Dragon Flower Jade Maidens of the Northern Frontier’s Golden Terrace to sing the *Lofty Cavern Divine Poems*, dispelling demons and summoning the true, their melodies bestowing grace upon the Lofty Mystic Perfection.

The Southern Culmen Longevity Lord then commands the nine hundred Jade Maidens of the Vermilion Palace’s Yang Gate Cloud Tower to attend the True Scriptures.

The Emperor brushes the sun’s essence and purple radiance’s splendor over the divine scriptures.

The Perpetual Divine Maiden of the South, the Purple Nymph of Radiant Grace, and those with countenances of golden-green dragon-flower hues shall attend to the left of the *Billionfold Scriptures*.

From *The Golden Tablet of the Supreme Ultimate with Jade Characters*:

Three thousand worthy maidens, each twenty years of age, having received the scriptures, entered the famous mountains. After six years, they attained deliverance and now reside in the Zhongyang Palace, three hundred li south of the Western Marchmount, two hundred seventeen li from the Duyang Palace.

The Bright Star Jade Maiden governs the revolutions of Heaven and Earth.
The Supreme Harmony Jade Maiden commands the Directing Merit Officers to stand at the four directions, while the Orthodox Unity Merit Officers stand at the center. The Upper Division Officers gaze afar toward the heavens, the Middle Division Officers survey the eight directions, and the Urgent Qi Officers hasten the ten directions.

From *The Numerological Regulations of Dignified Conduct*:

During the six fasting months of the year, the Three Heavens command the Celestial Thearch Taiyi’s envoys, the sun, moon, and stellar lodgings, and the Three Officials to summon and examine the transgressions of all people under Heaven.

From the teachings of the Three Heavens:
The Great Worthies—ten aspirations yield ten attainments.
The Middle Worthies—ten aspirations yield five attainments.
Among the Heavenly Worthies, three possess wealth and nobility:
Nobility is greatest in the absence of guilt,
Joy is greatest in the absence of care,
Wealth is greatest in contentment.

From *Laozi’s Wondrous Truth*:

The soul is honored, the spirit is noble—first among humankind are those who receive this scripture.

In the Southern Mountains there is a Daoist of steadfast resolve.
Unceasing in goodness, his name resounds throughout the kingdom.
The Four Seas embrace his Dao,
Heaven and Earth cherish him,
The hundred spirits benefit from him.
Emperors and kings treat him as a friend,
Neighbors regard him as parents,
His merit shines before Heaven and Earth.

From *The Great Peace*:

In movement, one aligns with Heaven’s heart;
In stillness, one harmonizes with Earth’s intent.
The foremost of the hundred practices,
The finest of the myriad blessings.

If the Central Kingdom lacks good people,
Know that good people descend from Heaven,
And Daoists, too, are born of Heaven.

The Three Officials of Heaven, Earth, and Water record the good and evil of humankind.

From *The Questions of the Immortal Duke*:

The guests of the Supreme Lord are revered among the living.
To "bestow four and relinquish three":
The four bestowals are the four kinds of giving.
The three relinquishments are: relinquishing the self, relinquishing wealth, and surrendering fate to seek the esoteric instructions.

On days of luminous might and auspicious hours,
Make offerings to the Three Honored Ones.
Clarify the mysteries of the plain and the subtle,
Refine yin and yang—
This is the precept against licentiousness.

Golden tones and jade resonance
Awaken future generations.
Speak not at improper times,
Nor expound what is not orthodox.
Words, deeds, speech, and conduct unite with the Dao,
Transcending life and death—
Thus one becomes a teacher to gods and humans.

The accumulation of human kindness prolongs life,
Each thought unwavering.
Though blessings ascend to Heaven,
There may yet be decline.
Though calamities descend to hell,
There may yet be advancement.

The Vermilion Lad, Dragon Net Guardian of the Heavenly Cavern of Luminous Jade Realm—
At Scarlet Phoenix’s Bend, the maiden Natai was given her name at fourteen, captivating an entire kingdom.
The Supreme Purple Void Primordial Sovereign of the Southern Culmen, returning her chariot to the Cinnabar Gleam’s Bend, bestowed upon her a chapter of the *Numinous Treasure Scarlet Script*, the true writ of the southern quarter.

In the primordial era, beside the Azure Jade Stream and upon the Whirlwind Mound, beneath the withered mulberry of the Everlasting Grove, the radiance illumined the ten directions.
Natai beheld five-hued purple light curving to bathe the oratory hall. Climbing the wall to gaze afar, she saw to the east a mulberry grove ablaze with luminous blossoms for hundreds of *li*, yet barred by the Gate of the Scorching Sea at Bright Valley.
She cast herself into the void—
whereupon the Water Thearch’s divine kings bore her aloft on five-colored flying dragons.
In an instant, within the Mysterious Center, she transformed into a man, riding the dragon and urging it through the emptiness.

The Primordial Beginning conferred upon him the imperial title of the Immortal Metropolis.
When the great kalpa reached its extremity and the blue *qi* began its revolution, the Era of Illuminating Light opened at the Brahmā-Nārāyaṇa Terrace, the capital of the Flying Primordial Cloud-Root, the Ruins of the Ninefold Azure Radiance.
The Primordial Beginning then bestowed upon the Azure Numinous Primordial Elder Lord of the Treasure-Flourishing Grove the *Numinous Treasure Scarlet Script*, the true writ of the Nine *Qi* Azure Heavens.

*Fundamental Practices*
The Dhyāna-Pearl World.

There was a woman named A Qiuceng, whose heart brimmed with great compassion, her cinnabar sincerity amassing profound resonance.

In the first year of the Illuminating Light Era, the sacred and venerable deities of the ten directions, along with perfected adepts of wondrous conduct, convened together in the Azure Radiance Grove of the Three Luminaries Terrace within the Vermilion Cinnabar Southern Garden. Amidst floral splendor and celestial music, fifty million beings gathered, the true writs gleaming resplendent like the moon among stars.

At sixteen, Qiuceng bathed herself in fragrant waters. Facing south, she beheld the divine essence blazing like the sun, purple clouds encircling on all sides. She climbed the wall and cast her body forth, hoping her form would dissolve into dust, flying to the Way’s presence. She immolated herself in fire, and in an instant, transformed into a man.

The Primordial Beginning commanded the Venerable Deity of the Southern Culmen to confer upon Qiuceng the Ten Precepts. The Perfected of the Numinous Treasure bestowed upon him three hundred Jade Maidens of Great Florescence and three hundred Jade Lads of the Official Ranks, all adorned with every excellence.

*The Thirty-Two Marks*
His name was inscribed among the heavens. As a tenfold-turned disciple, he bestowed mountains upon the reclusive Daoists. Seven generations of his ancestors befriended the Five Thearchs. His merits were vast, his recompense profound. His boundless generosity flowed across the four seas, honoring masters and revering the Dao. Having recited the scriptures ten thousand times, the Supreme Lord’s dragon-drawn chariot descended to welcome him, ascending to heaven in broad daylight.

To yield is to defer—such is the Dao’s recompense. To yield virtue is to defer power. Among people, none are noble or base; those who hold the Dao are revered.

Breathing in harmonious equilibrium, observing precepts and scriptures—there are many paths to the Way, and small efforts may yet achieve greatness.

Let the heart be supple as reeds, that calamities may cease and blessings arise. With a heart of compassion toward the myriad things, one’s kindness pervades all beings.

The highest goodness is filial piety supreme. To yearn for undying guardianship and transform one’s parents—such was the most filial son of the Supreme Thearch of High Antiquity, whose virtue resounded across the four quarters.

*The Great Peace*
His name entered the realm of the Perfected.

*The Dispelling of Demons*

Proclaiming the Dao’s qi, converting the deluded and lost.
Stirring harmonious melodies, the flying cry echoes at the ford.

The Lord Emperor of the Grand Tenuity
dwells in silent chambers, gazing upon the cold, dark stream.
He plumbs the two images, exhaling and inhaling the soaring rosy clouds.
Contemplating the five luminances to illumine himself,
he moves the radiant glow of rosy hues—rich and lush—
flowing and gleaming through the jade hall and purple chambers.

Returning to truth, reverting to simplicity,
roaming the Great Plain,
observing the lingering customs of the Three Dynasties,
inwardly cherishing gold and jade.

The wanderer
now in mountains, now in waters,
now in the world, now at home,
now in court, now in the wilds.

*The Jade Writ of the Grand Empyrean*
Racing in the three karmas, bewildered by the six passions—
the Supreme Purity of the Perfected.
Deceiving heaven, deluding earth—
the wondrous truth.

Bearing mountains, shouldering stones,
dragging through the eight adversities,
stealing the lives of others in life,
facing calamitous retribution in death.

*The Ordinances of Illuminating Truth*
Inverting yin and yang, violating sun and moon.

*The Bright Years*
Reviling heaven and earth, humiliating the clouds and empyrean,
cursing the winds of the south.

*The Manifest Might*
Demonic paths diverge,
confounding the heart—
death leads to the three wretched destinies.
Entering the crimson-linked hells,
amidst water and fire,
for two thousand *yi* kalpas,
bereft of human form.

Rushing toward peril in water and fire,
disdaining past lives as delusion,
mocking the sacred scriptures as false and absurd.
The mysterious teachings decline,
heaven and humanity drown in suffering.

Disbelieving the great Dharma,
disrespecting the luminous deities,
defiling and scorning the numinous texts—
in death, ascending the sword trees,
where winds from eight directions blow,
swaying the trees low and high.
Feet descend upon the knife mountains,
born with the six afflictions,
revolving through the five torments,
sinking into the fields of sin.

Bestow upon me the medicine of grace
to cure the illness of ignorance,
with words of goodness expounded,
dispelling the darkness of delusion,
that the eye of wisdom may grow clear,
cool and bright,
illuminating the true form.

*The Root and Boundary*
The six passions, once stained...

Through the three wretched realms they revolve,
adrift and forgetful of return;
through the five paths of existence they drift,
long sunk in delusion, never awakening.

*The Settled Will*

A thousand pounds of gold,
a single scripture of immortality—
bestowed upon a barren mountain,
the next life shall surely yield a fortune of gold.
Greed is the great sickness,
not to be cured by moxa or mugwort.
Twenty-five years
of unspent blessings:
the Registrar of Destiny submits the record,
granting seven hundred years of great lifespan.

*The Precepts of the True Root*

Human passions are hard to restrain,
like a banner raised in the wind,
fluttering without cease—
only the sage can still them.
The immortal lads attending the scriptures
report the arrogant to the Three Heavens;
the Registrar of the True submits to the Most High.
Three memorials filed, and you shall lose the Way.

*The Questions of the Immortal Duke*

To judge and slander the Dao and its virtue,
to revile and shame the celestial true:
mouth says one thing, heart another—
the wellspring of a hundred evils.
Karmic stench pervades the heart,
shattering the ten virtues,
fostering the ten evils.
The four thoroughfares lie desolate,
the six penetrations are blocked.
The five spirits run wild,
fondness for wine corrupts conduct.
The three fears, the three calamities—
in death, one descends to the Dark Capital,
examined and bound in the ghostly prison,
revolving through kalpas uncounted.

*The Teachings of the *Laozi***

The five desires—
innumerable thoughts, innumerable beings:
the eye desires to see the five colors,
excess wearies the hun-soul;
the ear desires to hear the five sounds,
clamor torments the hun-soul;
the nose desires to smell the five fragrances,
fragrance overflows and essence flows away;
the mouth desires the five sweet flavors,
abundance muddies the spirit;
the body desires to indulge in the five pleasures,
sloth scatters the will, harms the spleen, and endangers conduct.
The five evils.

**The *Scripture of Numinous Writ for Deliverance of Destiny***

**The Seven Harms**
The August Sage Emperor said:
The first harm—
the spirit weeps in the Exhausted Mansion, its cries ascending on high.
The second harm—
one’s dark name is erased from the registers, extinguished in the Nine Springs.
The third harm—
the Five Mansion’s works collapse, the myriad spirits shudder in alarm.
True immortals soar in lofty flight,
the Red Child wails in sorrow.
Though a dark record exists,
the Jade Name is lost in vain.
The fourth harm—
the hun-soul departs, the po-soul flees,
the nine apertures fill with dust,
the Five Mansion falls to ruin.
The fifth harm—
the Azure Bureau inscribes one’s name,
the Golden Watchtower binds it in its annals.
One scorns the true and cheapens the precious,
reversing the Black Seven Mysteries.
The sixth harm—
the Five Spirits scatter and fly,
the numinous essence loses its radiance.
The seventh harm—
true qi grieves at the Gate of the Numinous,
the wandering spirit startles the Red Child.
Hun and po wander through the palatial abodes,
while true immortals ascend in lofty flight to Jade Clarity.

**The *Nine Heavens of Turning Heaven***

**The Ten Calamities**
One cultivates the practice,
yet fails to uphold the Dao with constancy.
The calamity of serving a master—
one does not remain devoted to the end of one’s days.
The Perfected One said:
Of ten failures, one failure—
the hun-soul wails in the Numinous Mansion,
its cries ascending to the Heavenly Pavilion,
where the Three Bureaus contend in judgment.

**Springtime Hunting**
Spreading nets and casting snares,
setting fires to burn the mountains—
in death, one bears the iron staff,
ten thousand pains converging,
driven to exhaustion through a hundred extremes.

**The *Clarification of the True***

Damming rivers and breaching channels,
spreading nets and dangling lines—
in death, one enters the Mountain of Knives and Forest of Swords,
though wisdom and right contemplation endure.
Life’s span cannot be fully explored,
nor can one harmonize with the heart of Heaven and Earth,
or the intent of yin and yang.
Thus, longevity remains elusive.

Life and destiny—
the most precious treasures of Heaven’s Dao.
Only by possessing virtue in secret
do the Six Directions of Heaven and Earth,
the Eight Distances, and the myriad things
all attain their proper place,
and thus gain an increase in years,
fulfilling one’s allotted heavenly span.
This is longevity.

Within the hollow void, beyond the boundless expanse,
above the utmost heights, below the lowest depths—
thus does one cultivate the Dao through stillness and silence to nurture the body,
through clarity and coolness to pacify the heart,
through sincerity and integrity to uphold one’s resolve.

Dwelling in profound seclusion, abiding in tranquility,
like the hidden coil of the dragon in the deep;
mired yet unsoiled,
like the two luminaries absent from the void;
transforming virtue to preserve the spirit,
like the sacred altars safeguarding their radiance;
establishing reverence for the divine,
like the ancestral temple maintaining its sanctity.

Unseen by others,
like the sacred fish within the vast net;
unknown to all,
like the sun’s rising beyond the east;
my boundlessness,
like the Dao’s limitless expanse.

Though Heaven and Earth are divine,
they cannot restrain it;
though the sun and moon are bright,
they cannot halt it.

**The *Great Peace***
The brain palace filled,
harmonizing the Six Fluids.

**The *Three Primordial Caverns’ Pearl of the Dao***
The palace of life’s court—
the Perfected dwells within the formless,
rests in the neighborless,
and attains the living source of the Mystic Pearl.

**The *Tortoise Mountain Record of Origins***
Longevity equal to the sun and moon.

He who gains the Heavenly Lord’s trust and heart—
a long-lived one, who serves with the celestial gods above.
No reckoning of fate or lifespan,
recorded in the Heavenly Treasury;
within the breast, pure whiteness—
will like flowing water, dwelling like a fortress,
thus attains long life.
Virtue moves Heaven and Earth.

**The *Laojun’s Strategems***
Mastering the Six Arts externally,
settling the Supreme Clarity within;
elixir fluids and mystic wonders,
ascending to the Purple Court.

**The *Ink Record of Cinnabar Tablets***
He who observes the celestial patterns—
names the Three Luminaries,
gazes upon the Three Paths of the world;
sun’s passage, moon’s return,
the Northern Dipper’s nine stars,
two concealed, seven manifest,
measuring the Mystic Ford.

**The *Treasure of the Mysterious***
Yin Xi gazed upward at the celestial patterns,
looked downward to examine earthly principles.
Examining earthly principles—
discerning the Three Colors:
soil, mountains, waters.
Surveying the Five Directions’ precious mystery.
Celestial immortals’ wondrous arts—
numberless beyond reckoning.

**The *Great Peace***
The Golden Watchtower’s Imperial Lord
spoke to the Azure Lad:
"Reveal to you the Way of Celestial Immortals."
Six Arts—
talismans, charts, scriptures, precepts, methods, calculations.
Six Harmonies as one wave,
a thousand pillars as one dream.
Three dawns like windows,
the vault of Heaven like a suspended beam.
Gazing up to pluck jasper blossoms,
stooping to sip from the gem-studded well.
A thousand years but a moment,
ten thousand ages like a flash of lightning;
years pass swift as a startled arrow.
Perfected officials sport at the Mystic Ford,
within the Purple Empyrean’s heart.

**The *Upper Prime Lady’s Song of the Mystic Step***
Once I entered the Dark-True Dao,
stepped lightly to ascend the Great Rosy Clouds.
Shouldering my satchel, I approached the Heavenly Gate,
inquiring of the Supreme Lord’s abode.
Suddenly I met the Purple Tenuity Garden,
where Perfected Ones stood thick as hemp.
Green radiance rose in limpid clarity,
cloud canopies reflecting crimson blossoms.
Orchid chambers veiled the forest towers,
jade chambers opened with gossamer veils.
Cinnabar terraces stood in empty construction,
latitudinal splendor birthing numinous flowers.
Soaring steps trod the ridgepole’s height,
cavernous illumination leaned on winding paths.
Jade embryos presented crimson mushrooms,
nine hues harmonizing of themselves.
Embracing and refining the immortal frame,
through ten thousand kalpas still a child’s teeth.
Who says lifespan has bounds?
Fusang is not yet a stump.

**Poem of the Supreme Cavern Spirit**
By chance the light chariot’s flight canopy,
swift reins floating through the Eight Clarities.
Aligning the carriage to control the Cinnabar Way,
glancing afar to feast in the Cloud Camp.
Dragon pennants gleaming with jade essence,
feathered robes in kingfisher and purple hues.
Surpassing the Six Drinking Terraces,
in profusion delighting in the Phoenix City.
Escorting the Divine Empyrean King,
soaring high to the Supreme Capital.
Gazing up to part the Three Pristine Chambers,
long mists scattering over the Eight Rivers.
The Perfect Dao transcends orchid towers,
the Great Radiance illumines Jade Clarity.
Flowing auroras follow my return,
flying to benefit the courtyard’s green axles.
Ascending high through the Four Gates’ opening,
jade splendor flourishing at the Golden Gate.
Divine radiance pervades Orchid Peak,
the Three Lights already resplendent.
Binding brightness to begin the primal qi,
the Eight Convergences level the hidden source.
Vast and distant at the kalpic dawn,
the Great Yang harmonizes with the morning court.
Numinous transformations in the Four Benefit Courts,
lush as the celestial patterns on high.
A thousand maidens arise without trace,
gathering the sun’s essence-spirit.
Returning the brush to rest in the Cinnabar Chamber,
silently contemplating the Supreme Mystery.
Congealing spirit to grasp the Nine Drinks,
linking watches to continue the long mists.
Three candles illumine the Great Radiance,
in absolute emptiness life stirs anew.
The Jade Emperor’s luminous robe,
rustling to penetrate the Nine Heavens.
Concealing gold in the ultimate verses,
treasuring my Jade Clarity’s chapters.
Azure clouds encircle the Cinnabar Chamber,
scriptural characters gleaming with purple radiance.
Raising my feet over the myriad ford-waves,
with mystic steps ascending the Jade Portal.
Eight winds drum the high peaks,
how towering the cloud forests!
Tall and straight, dragon and phoenix sing,
their commands harmonizing with the Mystic Talisman.
Grasping the tally to summon the Supreme Subtlety.

**The *Sutra of Demonic Destruction***
First bestowing this scripture’s poem—
crimson radiance floating in the dark dawn,
purple ploughs riding the cloud’s journey.
Gazing up to surpass the Golden Watchtower’s interior,
looking down to behold the Western Flower City.
Eastern auroras unfurl jade radiance,
divine light blazing with the Seven Numinous.
Obscuring reflections in the Three Candles,
fragrant mists scattering through the Jade Court.
Hand in hand with the Weaving Maid’s dance,
twin lapels dropping kingfisher green.
Leftward, the patterned feather banners,
flowered canopies following clouds’ tilt.
Feasting and resting beyond the Ninth Heaven,
right and wrong do not concern me.

**The *Hidden Book of the Great Cinnabar***
Fusang’s emerald empty peaks,
crimson numinous blossoms faintly bright.
Azure terraces above the auroral void,
four vistas reflecting lofty clarity.
Flying light controlling the purple wheel,
Three Pristine reins guiding the cinnabar carriage.
Reclining in the Supreme Emperor’s palace,
wailing in the Grandmother’s court.
Bathing and rinsing in the azure rapids,
lifting the jade wine jars.
At dawn’s curve riding the wind’s fan,
shaking the auroras to descend in tilt.
How cold and clear the winding chamber!
Nurturing perfection, awaiting the sun’s completion.

**The *Supreme Primordial Perfected’s Transmission of the Great Cavern’s Mystic Scripture to Xu Xiang***
Eight paths converge in non-origin,
riding the motion to observe the clamorous net.
Empty light gazing upon the jasper carriage,
the Mystic Potter’s crafting of the phoenix song.
Left hand grasping the Jade Flower’s benefit,
flying steps treading the Seven Primes’ threshold.
Three luminaries resplendent with purple radiance,
four directions all one’s own spirit.
Mystic waves shake the azure billows,
great fords drum the myriad streams.
Within clouds revolving the jasper wheel—
why hasten in the dust’s midst?

**Chanting the Jasper Hall**
Six clouds arise at the window.
The Supreme Sovereign’s Master silently chants the Jasper Carriage—
playing with the Three Passes’ luxuriance,
dark chapters unfolding their rhymes.
Sounds resonating with Grand Harmony,
ten thousand songs ending the feast.
Divine light of Eight Radiance,
Seven Qi intermingling to arise.
The Noble Scion harmonizes transformations,
the Imperial Unity congeals form.
Wondrous chanting of divine grace,
numinous tones scattering jade,
cavernous light merging with the Mysterious.

**The *Verses of the Pure and Plain***
Chanting and intoning the Imperial Unity’s honor,
a hundred passages naturally attuned.

**The *Mount Jade Capital Scripture***
Cloud dragons.

When the Dao of Cavernous Perfection is achieved, then it is attained.

**The Venerable Lord of Immortals**
Inquiry to the Supreme Sovereign Jade Emperor:
Chanting the hidden scriptures of Jade Purity,
the jade tones resound in distant clarity,
the resonant verses of Pure Subtlety vibrating—

The supreme radiance emits morning splendor,
golden skies dense with purple purity.
Jade purity illumines the jasper fan,
intoned before the Void-Spirit Perfected.
Hand in hand with the blossoms of the Azure Grove,
revolving the canopy o’er the Great Primordial Court.
Reclining in banquet within the emerald chamber,
soaring steps traverse the resplendent Jade Capital.
Lifting the Crimson Radiance King,
long mists scatter the void encampments.
The Four Kings dwell within which body?
Transformations divide—how could form be singular?

**The *Golden Mystery of Cavernous Radiance***
Poem of the Lady Attendant of the Central Watch:
The Supreme Perfected chant in the jasper chamber,
the lofty immortals sing in the gemmed hall.
Nine phoenixes intone the crimson pipes,
void rhythms inscribe the feathered chapters.

**The *Hymns of the Host of Perfected***
Facing the moon, chanting and sighing—
Nine Sages, Nine Mysteries.

The Dao Lord arranges the records,
the Supreme Sovereign Master joins in chanting the Mysterious Portal of Upper Clarity.
In the purple dawn of Supreme Purity,
abundant virtue brings Great Peace—
naturally summoning qilin and phoenixes.
Pure, cold, and immaculate,
naturally summoning mushroom spirits and jade maidens.
Harmonious and auspicious omens,
naturally summoning good fortune.

**The *Scripture of Laozi’s Precepts***
The Primordial Beginning’s *Cavernous Mystery, Numinous Treasure, Vermilion Script, Jade Chapters, True Writ*—
born before the Primordial Beginning, within the Void Cavern,
the numinous chart already resplendent,
the ten thousand emperors pay homage to the Perfected.
Heaven bestows the Twelve Mysterious Omens,
Earth emits the Twenty-Four Responses.
Above, celebrating the numinous mysteries of the Nine Heavens,
extolling the luminous treasures of the Three Heavens.

The Twelve Omens:
At that time, Heaven and Earth were the root of the ten thousand qi,
the Two Images divided the frame,
thirty-six thousand suns and moons
shone as one, illuminating all heavens,
no darkness left unpenetrated.
The supreme sages, great spirits, and wondrously practiced Perfected
feasted in the Jade Court,
roamed the Great Void,
extolled and recited the numinous writ—
Heaven spontaneously produced celestial music,
hundreds, thousands, myriad kinds,
all arising as one,
stirring the cloud palaces of the Cavernous,
the divine transcendent stags of the upper realms.
Numinous winds chant a hundred hymns,
the empty seats of the ten directions.
Gong and shang harmonize in accord,
all becoming cavernous chapters.

The Celestial Turning Mechanism halts its pivot,
the stellar lodges cease their motion.
Heaven knows no day nor night,
the four seasons dawn as one.
Purple clouds exhale their radiance,
streaming and scattering through all heavens.
Spring and autumn, winter and summer,
the four qi blend in gentle harmony.
The Five Marchmounts rest in tranquility below,
the Seven Treasures’ divine marvels disperse across the earth.
Wondrous forests of the Seven Treasures,
jade canopies cover the Ten Heavens.

The Twenty-Four Responses:
At that time, the primordial Heavenly Origin was in chaos,
no light yet shone,
the morning cock heralded the dawn,
the four scenes grew bright and clear.
Heaven’s mystery and Earth’s expanse unfolded,
giving birth to the Five Phases.
Thirty-six thousand suns and moons,
above and below shone as one,
illuminating without end.
The Azure Crow bore a writ,
announcing the Five Thearchs’ just divisions.
Three Tigers spewed forth gold,
securing and pacifying the Five Directions;
Numinous Dragons presented the Grand Talisman,
reporting to the Water Thearch.
Jade Phoenixes carried the imperial seals,
Crimson Crows soared and danced.
Flooddragons leapt and bounded,
stirring the vast abyss.
The River’s waters stilled their flow,
fish scales gathered in assembly.
Sweet dew arose of itself,
mushroom blossoms poured forth in abundance.
Lions and fierce beasts
drew near to humans as neighbors.
The aged reverted to youth,
their countenances splendid and majestic.
Earth’s treasuries released their stores,
gold and jade revealed their forms.
The world sang in chorus,
rejoicing in the Great Peace—
the earth bore lotus blossoms,
the Five Marchmounts shone with clarity.

*The Cavernous Talisman Scripture*
The Most High Lord of the Dao, in the Fragrant Grove Garden...

The myriad heavens spread their mats,
as clouds and mists surged thickly,
the four seasons merged in darkness,
three days and nights passed—
the profound yin remained unbroken.
Heaven and earth ceased to be,
before the vast desolation,
the Heavenly Venerable spoke:
“The Jade Script shines resplendent,
veiling the light of heaven.
For the sake of the four assemblies,
I reveal the wondrous auspices of the heavens.”

Those who uphold the scripture’s essence
may hear fragrant incense or the strains of zither and lute,
may hear chanting in the void,
or see a halo bright as the sun,
and the marvels of perfected beings and flying immortals from the ten directions—
all arising of themselves.

When wisdom is obstructed,
the gods of heaven and earth
no longer manifest.

The *Jade Writ of the Imperial Chapters*
must be placed upon the crown of the head and held in the heart,
then the Supreme Perfected Immortals will come to guard, never departing.

The Purple Tenuity gleams with seven towering trees,
jade blossoms and rosy clouds gather,
the sages assemble in the Jasper Palace,
the Queen Mother of the West commands the Azure Song.

*The Cavernous Numinous Chapters*
Within the Great Radiance,
white qi is woven into terraces,
ninefold clouds form the halls.
Purple mists layer the gates,
where divine splendor gathers—
the dwelling of the Primordial Sovereign of the Great Void.

The *Luminous Ancestral Heaven* drifts in the western skies,
above Dragon Marsh Mountain.
Of old, the *Scripture of the Three Sovereigns* existed there,
yet among a million men and women,
not one obtained it—
only those born with prior destiny received this writ.

The South Pole Lord of Longevity,
styled Yi Du,
concealed this scripture within the Nine-Bend Grotto Chamber of the Jasper Terrace and Cinnabar Cloud Palace,
sealed with the peaks of Yulin
and the chapters of the Lofty Profound Cavern.

In the western chamber of Mount Emei in Shu Commandery,
of old, the *Scripture of the Three Sovereigns* resided.
Among a million men and women,
in the Yellow Chamber,
it presides over the merits of the Flying Perfected of Sun and Moon.

*The Inner Sounds of the Myriad Heavens*
Those who receive the great cavernous oral instructions
preserve the five spirits within the Purple Chamber,
their voices resounding in the chambers of the Five Elders,
their virtue ascending above the Three Clarities.

The *Jade Writ of the Numinous Script*
and the *Jade Writ of the Great Empyrean*.

The Perfected Sovereign regularly ascends on the ninth day of the ninth month, the fifth day of the tenth month, the third day of the third month, the eighth day of the fourth month, and the seventh day of the seventh month—these five days mark the times of the Ten Assemblies. He mounts to the Supreme Ultimate’s Jasper Terrace, the lofty Jade Chamber within the Golden Hall, where he contemplates the Five Vows in the Secluded Palace, yearning for the mysterious decree to descend into emptiness and non-being. Unsealing it with jade tablets, the golden tones resound through the Great Void, summoning the Five Emperors to guard the numinous, while myriad blessings converge in the Solar Chamber.

The Triple-Flowered Citadel
A chamber name of the Jade Clarity, situated within the Jade City, where the Primordial Sovereign of Yang Peace resides.

The Hall of Vast Numinosity
Where the Three Primordial Lords of the Jade Empyrean dwell.

The Celestial Venerable of Primordial Beginning
Abides in quietude within the Cloud Palace’s Yellow Chamber, amidst the Seven Treasures’ splendor.

Yin Xi followed Laozi into heaven, ascending the Ninefold Gates of the Sun, entering the Seven-Colored Cloud Chambers of Flowing Radiance, where he exchanged rites with the noble assembly of immortals.
*Biographies of the Supreme Perfected*

The Lord of Longevity of the Southern Culmen
Ascended the Dark Ravine’s gorge, receiving the *Scripture of Golden Elixir and the Refinement of Cloud-Rooted Malleable Vajra*, the *Methods of Flying Smoke, Rising Frost, and Settling Snow*, and the *Dao of Summoning Clouds and Absorbing Essence*.

The Jade Chambers of Kunlun’s Piled Stones
Where immortals reside.

Presides over the kalpas of heaven and earth.

*Jade Writ of the Great Empyrean*

Watery mists entwine the sun and moon.
*Charts of the Twenty-Four Lives*

The Queen Mother of the White Jade
Enters the Azure Forest Palace within the Jade Tower of Mount Hao, where chambers of vermilion and purple are strung with pearls and treasures, attended by jade lads and maidens bearing instruments and guards.
*True Scripture of the Great Cavern*
Concealed within the Ninefold Mystery Jade Treasury of the Supreme Great Possession Heaven.

Hidden within the Purple Chamber of the Six Directions of the Supreme.

Within the Purple-Cinnabar Chamber

*The Outer Charts of Release*
The Pure and Tranquil—Fivefold Harmony.
By Heaven’s clarity, it is made clear;
by Earth’s stillness, it is made still;
by the light of sun and moon, it is illumined;
by the motion of stars, it is aligned;
by the nature of the myriad things, it is nurtured and stilled.

*The Numinous Sounds*—Tenfold Harmony.

*The Northern Prime Heavenly Numinous Mirror Writ*
*The Supreme Eight Simplicities*

The Daoist Abode’s Hall of Discipline:
above the scripture terrace, before the fasting hall,
all hang golden mirrors and stone chimes,
struck with bronze and stone to stir the chamber spirits.
*From the Supreme Perfected Regulations*

Within the Heaven of the Bamboo-Fall August Gourd,
the North Emperor’s Cold Numinous Window
gives birth to the essence of the ten thousand demons.
*From the Inner Writs of the Myriad Heavens*

Within the Heaven of Primordial Ascent through the Hollow Cavern,
the Southern Culmen of the Dark Quiescence
presides over those who attain the Dao.

*The Verdant Radiance True Scripture*
bestowed by the Ninefold Mystery Venerable,
transmitted to the Most August Former Master.
The Supreme Great Dao Lord sealed it within the Jade Writ.

*The Supreme Ultimate Record of Radiant True Scripture*
The Grand Simplicity abides above the Dark Mystery.
The Nine Palaces array their Golden Gates in the Heaven of Grand Simplicity.

The Jade Gate and Orchid Chamber—
names of the portals within the Supreme Clarity Palace.

The Supreme possesses the Four Luminous Gates of the Jasper-Feathered Portal,
the southern gate of the Supreme Clarity Jade Emperor.

The Eastern Florescence Square Reservoir Azure Lad Palace
has six gates, each enclosing a circuit of three thousand leagues.
The Eastern Azure Florescence Gate,
whose gatekeeper is Qiu Boyuan, oversees the registers of those who study immortality.
The Southern Divine Florescence Jade Gate,
whose gatekeeper is Wang Zusi, governs perfected ones and flying immortals.
The Western Jade Grotto Gate,
whose gatekeeper is Yang Shaoye, presides over true immortals.
The Southeastern Heavenly Eastern Heaven Pass Gate,
whose gatekeeper is Wu Che, governs past lives.
The Northeastern Cold Water Gate,
whose gatekeeper is Chong Lindu, oversees the departed spirits.
The Six Gates govern the Heavenly Mound Mountain.

The Palace of the Pure Golden Watchtower
lies north of the Three Luminaries, five myriad leagues distant.
To the east of the Supreme’s abode,
nine thousand leagues west of the Dark Feather Wilderness’s Mound Mountain,
it stands west of Jade Clarity, conjoined with the Heavenly Watchtower,
and has four outer gates.
The Eastern Jade Radiance Golden Fusion Gate,
where two kings—Wang Chen and Wang—wield nine-jointed banners, each guarding one half.
The Supreme Jade Clarity Void Sovereign’s guests of the Great Perfected
enter and exit through the Southern Grotto Treasure Jasper Cloud Gate,
presiding over perfected ones and flying immortals,
who roam the Eight Poles, traverse the Five Marchmounts,
and pass through the Western Dark Capital’s Jade Treasure Gate,
overseeing those who study immortality and receive registers, and the recording of perfected ones.
The Northern Dark Yin Culmen Cloud Gate,
governing the demotion of perfected ones,
encloses a circuit of seven thousand leagues.
*From the Purple Writ of the Golden Root*

The Nine Heavens’ Chariots Aligned,
the Eight Emperors’ Wheels Stilled—
they scour the jade portals for all ghosts,
while the Yin Armor arrays itself at the Dark Gate.
*From the Cavernous True Writ of Golden Mystery*

Within the Heaven of August Prime,
the Gate of Sun and Moon
channels the light of the Nine Darks,
opening the repository of the Long Night.
*From the Inner Writs*

Within the Heaven of Level Nurturance,
the Azure Florescence Gate.

Within the realm that governs the jade maidens of the host of perfected ones,

The Pass of Great Possession,

The Heaven of the Seven Luminaries’ Southern Culmen Gate of Fondness for Life,

*From the Yellow Registers’ Slips and Writs*

The Most High Lord of the Great Dao
addressed the Northern Culmen Perfected Lord, saying:
"In former times, I withdrew to the Northern Heavens,
my feet treading the Floriate Canopy,
my hands parting the Nine Origins.
In the cloud palaces of Leisurely Radiance,
I sported in the Northern Mystery,
roamed carefree through the Northern Dark’s halls,
and raced my chariot through the Cavernous Lofty Gate.
I gazed upon the revolving jade armillary to summon the turning of fate,
urged the kalpas’ convergence with dancing wheels,
mocked the withering decay of the myriad things,
and looked down upon heaven and earth, abiding forever.
Thus did I perceive the marvels of the stellar net,
and awaken to the supreme numen of the Dipper’s bowl."
*From the Most High’s Flying Feathers Writs*

Nine Heavens’ Dragon Scriptures.

At the Nine Heavens’ Three Passes Gate, inscriptions were carved.
Within the Flowing Fire Courtyard,
beneath the Cavernous Yang Palace,
its expanse stretched eighty myriad leagues.
The Upper Clarity Perfected Ones
crossed the Luminous Golden Pool,
ascended the radiant floating courtyard,
and encountered the Golden Essence Lord of the Eastern King of Primordial Script of Jade Clarity.

From the *Arrayed Records of the Three Heavens*:
The Southern Culmen Lord of Longevity
passed through the Golden Pool,
advanced to pay homage in the royal courtyard,
and beheld the Most High Jade Emperor of the Primordial Heavenly King,
the Lofty Jade Sovereign of the Three Heavens,
and the Jade Lads of the Three Heavens.
Together they dwelt in the chambers of clouded chambers,
with purple clouds as their roof,
azure mists as their walls,
yellow gold as their halls,
and white jade as their forms.
When the Celestial Thearch attended the Perfected,
the Golden Lads wafted incense,
blending a hundred harmonies to suffuse the Purple Courtyard.
They exhaled solar essence to dispel defilement,
and scattered lunar radiance to scatter dust.

From the *Essential Exegesis of the Most High’s True Writs*:
The Wondrous Court of Great Possession.

From the *Scripture of Salvation*:
The Supreme Jade Clarity Golden Perfected intoned:
"Twin lights issue from the void,
true forms and the seven qi intermingle,
feet tread the lapis lazuli courtyard."

From the *Jade Clarity’s Demonic Dispeller*:
The alchemical degrees of refinement.

From the *Jade Scripture of the Great Cavern*:
The Primordial Heavenly Honored One spread five-colored yellow gold to form an altar,
with white silver as its foundation,
and the seven treasures to invoke the numinous.
He transmitted the Cavernous Mystery’s Golden Writs,
the Purple Culmen’s Secret Glyphs,
and the Vermilion Chapters of Jade Script,
bestowing them upon the Most High Boundless Dao Lord.

From the *Twenty-Four Images of Life*:
The Primordial Venerable One
ascended the Purple Void’s Upper Jade Clarity Altar,
receiving the Nine Heavens’ Treasure Registers,
the Supreme August Treasure Scriptures,
the Jade Talismans’ Secret Chapters,
and the Jade Emperor’s Registers.

"Vacuous White—this is my dwelling.
Vacuous, the movement of heaven and earth;
White, the abode of the divine luminants."

From the *Laozi’s Wondrous Perfected*:
The lodging house of the host of immortals.

From the *Scripture of Great Peace*:

The Celestial Governance’s Mysterious Dwelling stands at the center of the earth,
seven beams high and six bays wide, twelve *zhang* in length.
At its center, two bays above, rises a one-story Lofty Mysterious Terrace.
Within the terrace, a great incense burner is placed, five *zhang* in height,
perpetually kindled with fragrant smoke.
Five *zhang* to the north, the Hall of Immortals is erected.
On its east and west sides, one bay each forms the Feast Chambers of the Immortals.
At the central bay of the great hall, three bays and five beams extend east and west.
The eastern side is the Yang Immortals’ Chamber;
the western side, the Yin Immortals’ Chamber.
Twelve *zhang* south of the Lofty Vacuous Supreme Mysterious Terrace,
near the southern bay, a five-bay, three-beam gate hall is built.
Before the great hall of the Mysterious Terrace,
on its east and west sides, wings of five bays and five beams each are constructed:
the eastern named Azure Ascent Chamber,
the western named Myriad Blessings.
One *zhang* north of the Lofty Vacuous Terrace,
a small chamber to the southwest serves as the Brightly Illumined Libationer’s Lodge.
At the western end of the great hall’s lower level, one bay faces east,
its door opening eastward, its western wall set with an incense burner for offerings.

The Celestial Master’s teachings and transformations are ever conducted facing east.

From the *Precepts of the Supreme Perfected*

The Venerable Lord of Primordial Beginning resides in the Numinous Heavenly Jasper Palace of Supreme Purity. (*Guishan Yuanlu*)

The Venerable Lord of the Nine Heavens resides in the Open Purity Palace.

The Primordial Father of the Nine Heavens dwells in the Jade Treasure Palace above the Nine Heavens.

The Mysterious Mother of the Nine Heavens abides in the Jade Treasure Cavern-Perfected Palace above the Nine Heavens.

The Vacuous August Lord, whose form and shadow follow the four seasons, resides in the Cinnabar Jasper Palace, Transformation-Birth Palace, Vermilion Bird Palace, and Phoenix-Song Palace.

The Lord of Primordial Celestial Alignment dwells in the Radiant Splendor Palace.

The White Emperor Lord abides in the Prior Communication Palace.

The Black Emperor Lord resides in the Northern Yellow Palace.

The Yellow Emperor Lord dwells in the August Loftiness Palace.

**Rankings of Musicians and Entertainers, Sixth Section**

The Great Music of Heavenly Harmony interweaves ten thousand melodies. The Perfected Consorts sing in unison, while celestial musicians number in the hundreds of thousands. The *"Jade Capital"* hymn resounds as the Four Heavenly Kings and their hosts attend Lord Lao, bearing incense and flowers to his right. The celestial entertainers perform together, their mournful reed pipes startling the heavens.

Music stirs the qi of the six directions and eight extremities—east and west, south and north, the cyclical signs *jia*, *yi*, *bing*, *ding*, and the twenty-five qi, each with its proper correspondence. Thus it moves all things, harmonizes yin and yang, stabilizes the four seasons, and balances the five phases. Strings are tuned by the nine-nines sequence of their silk, only then can they unite yin and yang.

**On the Days of the Earthly Branches:**
- **Zi day:** The maiden Xuan Shuang plays the *sheng*.
- **Chou day:** The maiden Huang Zhen plays the *xiao*.
- **Yin day:** The maiden You Ling plucks the *qin* and *se*.
- **Mao day:** The maiden [name missing] strikes the *zhu*.
- **Chen day:** The maiden Huang You plays the *qin*.
- **Si day:** The maiden Ying Dan sounds the bells and chimes.
- **Wu day:** The maiden Sima Xing plays the *xiao*.
- **Wei day:** The maiden Gongsun Wu plays the flute.
- **Shen day:** The maiden Zhen Jin performs the ninefold harmonies.
- **You day:** The maiden [name missing] sings the sixfold variations.
- **Xu day:** The maiden Chang Yun mimics the cries of a hundred beasts.
- **Hai day:** The maiden Gongche Jian composes the world’s newest melodies.

When music is to be performed, the master first ascends to the left palace of heaven to retrieve the instruments, returning with them amid the clouds. Before the music reaches even ten *li*, its resonance is already heard throughout the realm.

The Golden Perfected, the Divine Transcendents, and the assembled sages strum the cloud zithers, perform the *Heavenly Harmony*, dance with lions, and ride white unicorns. They coax white cranes to circle and crimson phoenixes to soar, while the eight tones ring clear, the nine hues gleam radiant, and pipes, drums, bells, and chimes weave a thousand wonders through ten thousand entertainments.

**From the *Supreme Purple Writ of the Jade Register*:**
The Celestial Entertainers of the Various Heavens—
For Mao Ying, the Queen Mother of the West commands her attendant Shi Gongzi to strike the bronze of Kunting, her attendant Wan Jueqing to pluck the strings of Wuling’s zither, her attendant Fan Chengyan to sound the dark-yin chime, her attendant Sheng Shuangcheng to play the *yunhe* reed organ, her attendant Xu Feiqiong to beat the *zhenling* drum, and her attendant Yu Shanghua to perform the eightfold rhythms of the *balang*.

**From the *Inner Transmission of the Three Mao Lords, Perfected of the Great Primordial*:**
The Purple Consort of the Western Flower and the Queen Mother of the West each command their attendants Zhao Yunzi and Li Qingyu to play the flowing-gold stone.

**From the *Highest Clarity*:**
The Lord Emperor of the Grand Tenuity commands the Perfected Envoy of the Grand Tenuity, Cheng Ling, to sound the nine heavens’ resonant [missing character] gold and mystery.

In the fast of the Grand Capital, jade chimes strike and jasper bells ring. The Azure Lads of the Square Cauldron...

The Jade Maiden of Eastern Florescence, Yanjing Zhu, is commanded to strike the bell of Western Fullness.

**From the *Inner Transmission of the Purple Void Primordial Sovereign*:**
The Sagely Lord plucks the cloud-hook zither,
stirring the hundred bones to fall,
jade claws strum the nine voids,
piercing the nine heavens’ axle—
the great cavernous divine continent’s hymn,
the soul-congealing melody,
mysterious verses of numinous elegance,
heavenly tones of subtle resonance.

**From the *Purple Script*:**
The Heavenly Venerable commands the Golden Numinous Sovereign of Western Florescence, the Flying Mystery Woman, Perfected of Radiant Augustness, to play the zither of the five destinies and sound the reed organ of the divine continent.

**From the *Spiritual Meaning of the Cavernous Void*:**
The Lord Emperor of the Grand Tenuity commands the Grand Tenuity’s Perfected Envoy, Wei Lingdai, to brandish the banner of the Upper Realm, its flowing-gold fire bells gleaming,
the five numina arrayed in splendor,
the six virtues resplendent,
the eight tones harmonized as one,
the ten thousand measures sounding in unison,
cloud zithers pure and resonant,
heavenly maidens weaving the celestial zither.

**From the *Golden Mystery*:**
The Jade Consort of Western Florescence commands her attendant Wang Xian to strike the eightfold *balang* zither.
Jade Lads pluck the proud melody—
Northern Florescence unfurls in snow.
The Lord Emperor plays the cloud-proud dragon of radiant light,
a hundred harmonies unite in jade resonance through the Great Void,
the kingly tone stirs the boundless.
The eight winds intermingle with the true at heaven’s center,
the five blossoms of immortals spread across the four corners.
The divine semblance awakens at the gate of jade and fine jasper,
the wondrous melody arises from the precincts of the Great Cavern.

**From the *Subjugation of Demons*:**
The Perfected of the Supreme Ultimate.

**From the *Biography of the Purple Void Primordial Lady*:**
She commands the Cold Jade Maiden Song Lianjuan to pluck the ninefold *qi*-bound zither.

**From the *Luminous Jade Canon*:**
Why do the five pipes sound so mournful?
The divine phoenix soars through the jade grove,
the herb-immortals display their feathered regalia.

**From the *Central Treasury of Laozi’s Calendar*:**
On the dark-moon and new-moon days of the eight solar terms, Heavenly One strikes the drum to assemble and summon all spirits—those unrecorded shall perish.

**From the *Purple Chamber of Supreme Clarity*:**
The Nine Heavens’ Grand Perfected intones:
The void drum resounds with echoing bells,
the nine skies plow floating clouds.

**From the *Cavern of Perfection*:**
When the Most High Jade Emperor Dao Lord receives the Hidden Talisman of the Lofty Clarity’s Boundless Dao,
jade drums shake with thunder,
ninefold radiance turns day to dusk.

**From the *Records of the Grand Tenuity Emperor Lord*:**
He dispatches Wei Ling to beat the azure drum’s dark flourish,
striking gold to shatter jade, tapping jade to count the notes—
dragons roar, tigers howl,
phoenixes dance, phoenixes sing,
cavern-light and golden mystery intermingle.

**From the *Inner Biography of the Purple Void Primordial Lady*:**
The Pure Void Perfected commands the Flying Mystery Jade Maiden Xianyu Lingjin to caress the ninefold gold-and-jade rhythm.

**From the *Scripture of Jade Pendants and Golden Diadems*:**
Notes of *gong* and *shang* harmonize in emptiness,
high and low coalesce into sound.
The Western Consort beats time,
heavenly maidens array their zithers.
Eight tones clamor in tumult,
transcendent echoes cloud the firmament.
The Twin Sovereigns quicken the rhythm,
phoenixes dance and phoenixes soar.

**From the *Three Sovereigns*:**
The Heavenly True Emperor commands the Mysterious Maiden to sing:
“Immortal sages roam the dark chart,
flying *brahmā* voices arise in resonant *uru*.”

**From the *Records of Immortals*:**
The immortal blows the ninefold numinous flute—
its sound carries thirty *li*,
the central flute has forty-nine holes,
the bamboo measures three to two *chi*.
When the nine flutes sing in unison,
a hundred beasts join the dance,
thousands of phoenixes come to harmonize,
the flute’s voice bestows great wisdom.

**From the *Arrayed Annals of the Three Heavenly Lords of Supreme Mystery*:**
The Western Florescence Purple Consort and the Queen Mother of the West each command their attendants—
Zuobao on the left, Han Longbin playing the phoenix-and-luan flute.

**From the *Records of the Three Heavenly Lords of Supreme Mystery*:**
The Divine King of Fusang’s Yang Valley commands the Cloud Grove Mistress Jia Quwei to blow the phoenix-defying flute.

**From the *Cavern of Perfection*:**
The Heavenly Worthy commands the Radiant Emperor to play the ninefold phoenix flute.
When the Most High Jade Emperor Dao Lord receives the Hidden Talisman from the Lofty Clarity’s Boundless Dao Lord,
fivefold rosy clouds entwine in splendor,
dragon-scripted flutes resound,
patterned tigers perform on the zither.

**From the *Songs of the Perfected*:**
The Southern Culmen Perfected’s poem:
“Resonant pipes on the dark peak ridge,
golden flutes channel the eight *qi*.
Why not blend the numinous wine,
and with bright gaze delight the nine lineages?”

**From the *Cavern of Perfection*:**
Dragons roar in ten thousand harmonies,
tigers howl, luan and phoenixes sing in unison—
the dragon’s radiance bears ninefold purple script,
the phoenix’s red writ.

**From the *Scripture of the Cavern’s Embrace*:**
The Grand Tenuity Heavenly Emperor Lord feasts in the jade chamber,
singing the Purple Void’s numinous verses,
drifting ethereal tones through the Great Mystery.

**From the *Cavern of Perfection*:**
The Primordial Heavenly King bestows upon the Southern Culmen Director of Destinies—
when the Seventy-Four Transformations of Supreme Clarity unfold within the cloud chambers,
the Three Origins’ True Jade and Supreme Origin’s Peerless Emperor Lord sings the *Inner Chapter of the True Transformation of the Supreme Origin’s Cavern Gate*:
“Three essences flow through the five rivers,
clouds traverse the ninefold mountain ranges.
Crimson numina open the azure chamber,
golden radiance blazes in the eastern rosy clouds.
Three luminaries illumine the Great Void,
jade gates coil through the winding cosmos.
Dispersing spirits beyond the nine degrees,
together in this ten-thousand-kalpa court.”

The Yellow Elder Emperor Lord of the Middle Origin sings the *Inner Chapter of the True Transformation of the Middle Origin’s Cavern*:
“Vast the Three Perfected array,
dividing currents of the ninefold cloud-*qi*.
Jade chambers bristle with rosy clouds,
golden realms shroud in deep mist.
Jade terraces soar in the upper mystery,
flowing essence gleams beneath the purple canopy.
Uniting the true in the Three Elixir Palaces,
dispersing spirits beyond the ninefold bounds.”

The White Origin Emperor Lord of the Lower Origin sings the *True Chapter of the Numinous Transformation of the Lower Origin’s Cavern*:
“Towering the rosy cloud gates,
golden portals coil through ninefold layers.
Cinnabar radiance gleams in the jade heavens,
flying auroras thicken on the dark beams.
Dispersing *qi* through the nine numinous portals,
branching into the myriad emperor’s offices.
The cavern transforms the cinnabar numinous grotto—
eightfold scenes may take flight through the void.
Silent, rosy clouds arise,
thus giving rise to the ten-thousand immortals’ lineage.”

**From the *Arrayed Annals of the Three Heavenly Lords of Supreme Mystery*:**
The Western Florescence Purple Consort and the Queen Mother of the West each command their four attendants—Xin Baihe, Zheng Bifang, Yan Wanlai, and Tian Shuanglian—to sing four melodies of the lofty immortals’ longing for the cavern’s numinous wanderings:
“Jade chambers blaze with eastern rosy clouds,
purple brushes float in the crimson dawn.
Flowery terraces may brighten the gaze,
feasting together in the flying heavens’ origin.
Jade terraces stand in the upper auroras,
golden splendor girds the numinous carriage.
Seven gates blaze with flowing rosy clouds,
jade chambers birth dragon-clouds.
Leftward, the Three Essences’ reins turn,
rightward, the myriad currents’ ford is struck.
Hands grasp the eightfold essence-*qi*,
the body drifts in the void’s midst.
Left hand holds the jade-flowered canopy,
flying scenes ascend the seven origins.
Layered auroras blaze with purple radiance,
all four directions are divine.
The dark heart within the Three Origins—
a single moment parts the years.”

**From the *Purple Phoenix’s Red Writ*:**
The Most High commands the Jade Clarity’s Upper Palace attendants Ji Yunmen and Tian Sifei to join in singing the *Precious Cavern’s Flying Auroras’ Utmost Mystery*:
“Reining the dark auroras above,
dragon pennants grace the golden city.
Flying mists coil through the winding cosmos,
purple phoenixes gleam in the jade capital.
Flying fragrance wafts through drifting smoke,
lush and dense, scattering across the eight wilds.
Riding the rosy jade chamber’s radiance,
grasping the tally in the jade-lit hall.
Above, summoning the Western Florescence Maiden to wail and command the ninefold dragon-script’s golden auroras.”

**From the *Songs of the Grand Ultimate Perfected*:**
“Cinnabar brightness blazes in Supreme Clarity,
eight winds disperse the rosy clouds.
Above, gathering the sun’s essence,
below, drinking the yellow moon’s splendor.
The numinous vista in the empty heavens—
the great path knows no crookedness.”

**From the *Songs of the Square Cauldron Blue Lad*:**
“Rosy clouds fan the divine radiance,
nine *qi* have no fixed form.
Dark reins fly beyond the auroras,
eight scenes ride the lofty clarity.
Hands grasp the Jade Emperor’s sleeves,
bearing me to be born in the dawn’s midst.
Brightly gazing upon the seven luminaries’ chambers—
dark, dark, and yet profound.
Arise, O scion of the Wei clan,
your name bound in gold script with flowering seals.”

**From the *Songs of the Fusang Divine King*:**
“Dawn opens the Supreme Emperor’s hall,
nine dragons rise together in reins.”

**From the *Songs of the Pure Void Perfected*:**
“Driving the carriage to rein in pure emptiness,
lingering in the fourfold flowery pavilions.
Jade wheels and dawn’s rosy clouds,
tiger lungs pursue the dispersing smoke.
Wisdom shakes the cinnabar banner,
bright torches illumine the eightfold brilliance.
Grasping the scene like a forest’s branches,
plucking the nine strings in the dark’s midst.
Bequeathing me the accumulated kalpas,
releasing this thousand-year sigh.”

**From the *Inner Biography of the Purple Void Primordial Lady*:**

The Queen Mother commands her attendants, Ku Pin and Li Longsun, to sing two songs of the *Mystic Cloud Melody*:

**"Though the Supreme Image hangs in clouds,
I grasp the gate of Heaven and Earth.
Parting the cloud-essence of Eight Effulgences,
I swiftly traverse the Six Realms.
Nurturing spirit within the Three Primes,
Absorbing essence beneath the Six Palaces.
Then mounting the myriad-dragon pillar,
I descend with phoenix gaze upon the Nine Wilds.
The Dark Garden halts the Northern Terrace,
Five Citadels gleam in towering splendor.
Unlocking the boundless ford,
I drift upon the Weaving Maid’s River.
Above, I ascend the Crimson Court,
Below, I wander the Sun’s Cavern Vale.
Gazing beyond the Northern Culmen,
I point toward the Ninefold Auroras of the Void.
In tranquil contemplation, moved by central harmony,
This is the song of the Mystic Void."**

*From the* Inner Biography of Lord Mao:

The Jade Maidens, graceful and flowing in dance,
Light and joyous, their forms swaying.

*End of* Upper Clarity Scripture of the Daoist Treasures, Scroll Three
*Upper Clarity Scripture of the Daoist Treasures, Scroll Four*

**Chapter Seven: Chariots and Mounts**

**Nine-Dragon Chariot of Jade Capital:**
When establishing the fast and performing the Dao-rites, the Four Heavenly Thearchs all mount flying dragons and green chariots, Eight-Effulgence Jade Carriages, accompanied by Perfected Ones and Jade Maidens. They grasp floral banners, with phoenix songs leading ahead, celestial zithers following behind, white cranes and lions roaring in harmony. Incense is burned, flowers scattered, as they behold and hearken to the Jade Sounds.

*From the* Great Sincerity of the Numinous Treasure:

The Primordial Beginning turns his Jade Chariot,
Yellow banners summon wind and clouds,
Sweeping clean the Fivefold Dao-Fields.
All the Great Saints of the Heavens,
Perfected Ones of Wondrous Conduct,
All ride the Ninefold Azure Radiance,
Streaming-Light Flying Cloud Jade Carriages.

*From the* Red Writ:

The Supreme Lord of the Great Dao
First mounts the One-Effulgence Chariot,
Harnessing Eight Pure Purple Clouds,
Escorting the Subtle Emperor of the Hidden Prime,
Together they journey eastward,
To the Jade Terrace of Heaven,
Where the Jade Clarity Purple Dao Void Sovereign,
Receives the Ninefold Radiance of the Great Dawn’s Hidden Talisman.

Next, he mounts the Two-Effulgence Chariot,
Harnessing Seven Pure Crimson Clouds,
Escorting the Subtle Emperor of the Crimson Prime,
Together they journey southward,
To the Peach Forest Dragon Net of Heaven,
Where the Jade Clarity Sun-Wing Void Sovereign,
Receives the Contemplation-Spirit Prime Hidden Talisman.

Next, he mounts the Three-Effulgence Chariot,
Harnessing Six Pure Red Clouds,
Escorting the White Emperor of the Purple Tenuity,
Together they journey northwest,
To the Azure Expanse Empty Song of Heaven,
Where the Jade Clarity Prospering Yang Origin Void Sovereign,
Receives the Total Dawn Nine Poles Hidden Talisman.

Next, he mounts the Four-Effulgence Chariot,
Harnessing Five Pure Azure Clouds,
Escorting the Black Emperor of the Mystic Prime,
Together they journey northward,
To the Jade Clarity Sevenfold Stillness Life-Guiding Highest Void Sovereign,
Receiving the Profound Radiance Revolving Root Hidden Talisman.

Next, he mounts the Five-Effulgence Chariot,
Harnessing Four Pure Yellow Clouds,
Escorting the Primeval Emperor of the Origin Prime,
Together they journey northeast,
To the Floating Blade Canopy Flowery Net of Heaven,
Where the Jade Clarity Great Brightness Void Sovereign,
Receives the Mystic Effulgence Dawn Tooth Hidden Talisman.

Next, he mounts the Six-Effulgence Chariot,
Harnessing Three Green Clouds,
Escorting the Central Emperor of the Numinous Prime,
Together they journey southeast,
To the Primordial Silence of Heaven,
Where the Jade Clarity Origin Void Supreme Empyrean Sovereign,
Receives the Conjoined Radiance Dawn Mandate Hidden Talisman.

Next, he mounts the Seven-Effulgence Chariot,
Harnessing Two Pure Purple Clouds,
Escorting the Proclaiming Emperor of the Lower Realm,
Together they journey southwest,
To the Harmonious Nurturing Heaven,
Where the Jade Clarity Sevenfold Contemplation Non-Birth Void Sovereign,
Receives the Lofty Radiance Dawn Mystic Hidden Talisman.

Next, he mounts the Eight-Effulgence Chariot,
Harnessing One Pure Numinous Cloud,
Escorting the True Emperor of the Cavern Prime,
Together they journey northwest,
To the Jade Clarity Eightfold Contemplation Highest Void Sovereign,
Receiving the Supreme Dragon Mist Talisman.

Finally, he mounts the Cavern-Effulgence Jade Chariot,
Harnessing the Great Auroral Purple Mist of the Mystic Effulgence,
Escorting the Ninefold Subtle Inner Emperors
And the Ninefold Heavenly Perfected Immortals of the Supreme Emperor,
All ascend together to the Mijianla Terrace,
The Empyrean-Cutting Desolate Mound,
The Flying Origin Cloud Root Capital,
The Jade Clarity Upper Heaven,
The Jade Clarity Purple Radiance Supreme Jade Thearch,
The Illustrious Supreme Lord of the Great Dao,
To receive the Hidden Talisman of the Highest Clarity Supreme Non-Ultimate Sovereign of the Dao.

*From the* True Scripture of the Great Cavern:

The Great Divine White Jade Queen Mother of Attained Dao
Rides the Nine-Canopied Floral Chariot,
Cloud-Dragons flanking her,
Immortal Lads arrayed before,
Jade Maidens lined behind,
Scattering flowers to her left,
Waving incense to her right.

*From the* Hidden Writ of the Dragon Script of Upper Clarity:

The Azure Lad of the Eastern Sea’s Square Cauldron,
After purifying himself in the Vermilion Chamber’s Yellow Quarters for three years,
Mounts the Threefold Numinous Streaming-Light Azure Cloud Chariot.

*From the* Numinous Writ:

The Supreme Lord of the Great Dao.

On the first day of the ninth month of the First Thearch’s inaugural year, the Celestial Worthy of Primordial Beginning journeyed westward to the Jade Realm’s Dragon-Cleft Mountain, arriving in a chariot of azure-green radiance, as all heavens rejoiced.

*From the* Golden Register of Simplified Writings:

The divine and sagely Thearchs, Celestial Worthies, and august Emperors of the myriad heavens, along with the perfected transcendents and lofty immortals, each observed the fast and upheld the Dharma, venerating the Supreme Void Thearch. On the day of the fast, all ascended in flying-dragon chariots of the Eightfold Radiant Clouds to the grand assembly at the Supreme Mystic Capital.

The Ninefold Numinous Perfected of Jade Capital intoned:
*"Dragon skirts sweep the skies above,
Tiger banners command the crimson hosts."*

*From the* Scripture of Jade Capital Mountain:

The mottled-dragon chariot, the luminous chariot of the Eight Ways,
The dark-radiance green chariot, golden-perfected and jade-luminous.
The cinnabar-red chariot of rosy clouds, the Thearch of the Supreme Tenuity—
He commanded the Upper Perfected of the Supreme Tenuity to aid Wei Ling in marshaling armor and aligning blades. Then, ascending the Eight-Jade Brush, resplendent as the dark radiance’s glow, the hosts of the Great Rosy Clouds led forth, proclaiming:
*"Let the Seven Dawns merge in brightness, the Five Thearchs expel the Great Yin of solar essence. The Eight Simplicities set forth the chariot; the Dark Might severs the weapons. Feathered canopies halt in the void; ten thousand riders incline as one. Poisonous dragons flank the carriage; flying mists coil about the canopy."*

*From the* Golden Mystery:

Reciting the *Supreme Rosy Chapters*:
*"Thrice opened, it shall surely brighten;
Clouds descend, lingering in the mist.
The void dispatches the flying-radiance carriage."*

*From the* Rosy Cloud Jade Writ:

The Night-Luminous Jade Maiden,
Clad in the emerald silk of Cloud Forest,
Rides this numinous conveyance to awaken the Real,
Driving the deer-brush across the Celestial River.

*From the* Hymns of the Multitude of Perfected:

Suddenly encountering the Fusang King—
The Nine Perfected of the Immortal Capital,
Testing the reins of the purple carriage,
How fresh their cloudlike countenances!

The Eightfold Radiance Chariot lingers;
The Jade Chariot of the Azure Lad—
Riding the jade-carved canopy,
Harnessing the qi of round pearls,
Ascending the mountain of cloud-waves,
Entering the chamber of Eastern Florescence.

*From the* Jade Scripture of the Great Cavern:

The Ten-Thousand-Flower Master ascends northward upon the radiance of the Three Simplicities and the feather-bright carriage, resting in the Hall of Ten Thousand Flowers atop the High Prime Peak.

The Lord Emperor King, True Uncle of the Prohibitions,
At times rides the sun-and-moon chariot,
Ascending the layered desert mountains.

The Immortals—
Feet suspended above the Five Peaks,
Hands grasping the bright rosy clouds.

The Three Primes’ Numinous Ones—
Purple and white clouds paired,
Lingering in the void of the Rosy Court.

The streaming-cloud cinnabar chariot,
The Three Simplicities’ flying carriage enters my Eight Gates,
Revealing the Dharma-wheel of life and death.

The green carriage—
Enters my Gate of the Dark Mystery.
The Perfected of the Dark Unity intones.

*From the* Hidden Writ of the Great Cinnabar:

Lingering amidst the Eight Mists,
Riding the radiance of the dark whip—
Dragons soar through the Nine Heavens.

The Feather-Bright Ones.

The Celestial Chariots of the Highest Clarity.

From the *Jade Scripture of the Great Cavern*:

The Supreme Ultimate Primordial Sovereign
Rides the soaring-feather chariot,
Feasting in the palaces of Highest Clarity.

Assigns three hundred Jade Maidens of Great Florescence to the Western Numinous Consort,
With twenty-four phoenix chariots,
To journey to the Golden Gates,
Receive the scriptures,
And ascend to the Jade Clarity’s Upper Palace.

Having recited the *True Scripture of the Great Cavern* thirty-nine chapters
Ten thousand times,
The Central Yellow Elder Lord petitions the Supreme,
Who commands the cinnabar-red chariot with the green canopy,
And the Nine Numinous Envoys and the Great One’s Life-Director to welcome you.

On the eight solar festivals ride the white simurgh chariots,
Harnessed to black-winged phoenixes,
To feast in Eternal Yang,
Gazing in inverted reflection upon the eight divine peaks.

With flying serpents as wheels.

The white-cloud chariot.

And all at once, the multitude ascends the void,
Riding flying-dragon treasure canopies.

Moon-embellished canopies.

The transmission of jade mushrooms and the warding of hidden splendor.

Journeys west to Dragonpeak Mountain at the Jade Gate,
Where the Primordial Heavenly Honored One arrives,

From the *Golden Register Simplified Writings*:
Mystic clouds and purple canopies,
Purple script with golden handles.

*On Ingesting and Nourishing*, Chapter Eight:
Cloud-purchasing feathered transcendents,
Cultivating mist and ingesting qi.

The Numinous Pass unites the Three Origins,
Essence transforms to bind the Five Spirits,
Nine refinements of the jade womb-palace.
Congealing qi to attain immortality,
Ingesting and nourishing with care for the Nine Numinous.
In tranquil contemplation, descending the Jade Chariot,
The Eight Level and Four Gates ascend to the Most High.

Ingesting divine elixirs and five-stone refinements to enliven the spirit,
Treasure the Five Offices to become a Perfected of the Nine Palaces.
Lush, the five cloud mushrooms,
Mystic radiance emits jade light,
Congealed essence pervades the numinous palace.
Wandering the palaces of sun and moon,
Five-colored principles govern the lofty Perfected.
Flowing brilliance illumines the ten directions,
Breathing without weariness.
Soaring heavenward with golden countenance,
Guiding and drawing to nurture the spirit-qi,
Mystic nourishment fills the six viscera.

From the *Twenty-Four Images of Life*:
Practicing the Nine Dawns’ illumination of the Grotto Chamber and Mud-Pill Palace,
To restrain the hun and po souls and subdue the myriad demons.
The qi of immortals and numina descends upon the bedchamber,
So-called: drawing the Three Lights and Nine Stars to illuminate the hundred spirits.
The Supreme Unity Emperor Lord,
Heavenly ghosts transform in unison.

The qi of profound emptiness and Grand Harmony,
Exhaling and inhaling the flowing mist of rosy clouds.
Embryonic breathing stills the hundred passages,
In boundless vastness, mastering the Three Efficacies.

From the *Scripture of Jade Capital Mountain*:
The child within the womb,
Exhales yin and inhales yang,
Using inner qi to nourish its nature.

From the *Great Peace*:
Qi is the vessel of spirit and luminosity,
The origin of purity and turbidity.
Feeding on the qi of the Mystic Root,
The spirit’s eightfold acuity,
The body bears solar radiance,
The face bears jade essence,
The eyes generate bright light,
The teeth contain purple qi.
The Dao’s essence lies in golden nectar,
Its affairs wondrous in water-jade,
So-called: exhaling and inhaling the Grand Harmony of spontaneity,
Riding the numinous qi of the Nine Essences.
Ingesting qi for ten thousand years,
Ever possessing youthful countenance.

From the *Five Talismans*:
The Primordial Five Qi.

To ascend the numinous treasure of Jade Mountain in the Mystic Capital’s Upper Palace, where the first radiance of yang light scatters the Primordial Beginning’s brilliance, streaming to irrigate all heavens—its qi dense and luxuriant, its glow warm and fragrant, essence like moon-pearls, light like purple mountains—this descends to nourish the roots of the scholar’s five teeth. The Perfected of Great Wisdom in the Upper Palace feed upon this radiance, completing their union with heaven.

From the *Jade Sleeve of Numinous Treasure*:
**Method of Ingesting the Teeth’s Qi**
At the eight solar nodes, enter the chamber in purity and alignment, visualizing the forms of the Five Elders. Practicing this for eight years, immortal officials and jade maidens will attend you; your body will emanate luminosity, illuminating the ten directions. The Five Thearchs will bow in reverence, and the administrators of the Three Realms will welcome you.

**Five Immortals**
Jade mushrooms in the Mystic Gulf’s depths.

From the *Twenty-Four Images of Vital Generation*:
Constantly contemplate the great sun within the spleen, and within the sun a golden tower, where a book lies sealed with a golden seal, three characters in breadth and length. When the sun’s majesty reveals it, read it aloud—your heart will open, your eyes will brighten, and you will become a transcendent.

From the *Laozi’s Observation of Heaven*:
Focus on the Yellow Field within the stomach—pure white as congealed fat, suffused with yellow qi. When it reaches the mouth, swallow it to attain satiety. This Yellow Field is the Great Granary. All spirits gather there to feast, where a yellow lightning cauldron steams rice, and jade maidens and youths serve as attendants, announcing: “The Yellow Thearch’s child has prepared the traveling kitchen.”

**Guiding Qi Nine Ascents and Nine Descents**
After twelve days, the body lightens; after eighteen days, minor attainment is reached; after thirty-six days, the Dao is greatly accomplished; after eighty days, the head and face radiate light; after one hundred twenty days, one becomes a Perfected.

**Entering the Chamber to Burn Incense**
Face due south, close the breath, and knock the teeth twenty-four times. Visualize as prescribed: *Li* above the head, *Kan* below the navel, *Kun* in the left hand, *Xun* in the right hand, *Qian* beneath the left foot, *Gen* beneath the right foot, *Dui* below the left flank, *Zhen* below the right flank. The eight trigrams manifest their forms, forms contain qi, qi contains spirit. The spirit-person shines with luminosity, arrayed in the eight directions, exhaling generative qi. In spring, *Zhen* governs and engenders fire; in summer, *Li* governs and engenders earth; in autumn, *Dui* governs and engenders water; in winter, *Kan* governs and engenders wood. During the four seasons, *Qian*, *Kun*, *Gen*, and *Xun* govern metal, rotating with the months: *Xun* in the third month, *Kun* in the sixth, *Qian* in the ninth, *Gen* in the twelfth.

**Method of Swallowing the Eight Qi**
In the months of *yin* and *mao* (spring), inhale *Zhen* qi three times, then spray high qi nine times; next sip *Xun* qi four times, then *Kun* qi twice; next spray *Qian* qi six times, then sip *Gen* qi eight times, *Dui* qi seven times, and *Kan* qi once. Conclude by knocking the teeth thirty-six times, rubbing the four limbs and five body parts. Practice this during the three or six periods of purification, bowing to the Supreme Eight Simplicities.

**Morning and Evening**
Recite: *jiazi*, *yichou*, *bingyin*, *dingmao*, *wuchen*, halting at *chen*. Strike the golden beam with jade clappers, circulate the Flowery Pond to recite the Wine Spring, scoop dew from the Boat-Shaving Pool, rinse the mouth’s perimeter, then swallow once after three repetitions—three swallows in total. Perform the *Six Jia* of the Lower Cinnabar as before, totaling thirty swallows to ingest their essential brilliance. The so-called golden beam is the tongue; the jade clappers are the teeth; the Wine Spring, Cinnabar Pond, and Dew Scoop are the saliva in the mouth.

From the *Method of Ingesting Qi*:
At dawn, consume the qi of the five clouds; at dusk, chant the three dawn-lights.

**The Cavernous Numinous Chapters**
The Great Dao wondrously formless,
Its numinous transformations manifest the Three Spirits.
At dawn, draw in the essence of the Five Stars;
At midday, spray the nectar of the sun’s core;
At dusk, ingest the yellow radiance of the moon;
In sleep, refine the Five Immortals beyond the body.

**The Twenty-Four Images of Vital Generation**
*Ingesting the Sun’s Essence*
To ensure longevity, the child must consume the sun’s essence.
On the first, third, fifth, seventh, ninth, and fifteenth days of the lunar month, from sunrise to midday, ingest it thus:
First visualize the sun at the center of the heart, the sun crowned with a dark canopy, beneath which stands a small boy, perfectly crimson, his crimson qi suffusing nine layers within and without the body. Envision the qi filling the head, ascending from the head to rise into the heavens, circling the sun ninefold.

Recite the incantation:
*"Sun Sovereign, Primordial Yang,
Return to the Crimson Chamber.
Unite with my virtue,
Together nourishing the small boy."*

Then visualize the surging essence descending into the nose, swallowing it twenty-seven times. The heart becomes filled with three figures: to the left, the Great One, the Father; to the right, the Dark Radiance, the Mother; at the center, the Crimson Child, the small boy. Seated upon a golden bed and jade couch, they hold jade ladles and jade cups. Within the cup appear jade blossoms, divine wine, and celestial ganoderma—visualize consuming them to attain longevity.

*Ingesting the Moon’s Essence*
This too grants longevity.
On the fifteenth night of the lunar month at midnight, face the moon and bow twice. Recite the incantation:
*"Moon Sovereign, Radiant Child,
Return to the Cinnabar Field.
Unite with my virtue,
Together nourishing the small boy."*

Visualize the moon’s white, pure, yellow essence descending into the nose and mouth, swallowing it twenty-one times. The moon’s essence anchors to the root of the kidneys, ensuring longevity.

*Ingesting the Stars’ Essence*
This ascends to the Grand Clarity.
At sunrise, dusk, midday, or midnight, visualize the Great Yellow Star of the North Pole. Recite the incantation:
*"August Heaven, Eternal Supreme Dao Lord,
Your humble descendant petitions for longevity."*

Envision the star’s essence descending, lingering between the brows, flowing into the nose and mouth. Swallow it fifteen times until the qi fills the heart and gallbladder. Within the spleen, the Dao Mother cradles the Crimson Child—thus is longevity attained.

The flying boat is named *Frost*,
Simmering and refining the clouds and waters.

Jasper and vermilion gold gleam bright,
Nine crucibles blaze in the heavens’ height.
Ascend the body to the Nine Heavens,
Leap beyond the Mystic Isles to roam the Nine Palaces’ domains—
Yet the True Person’s gate remains unseen.

*The Eight Essences*
Nine grades of immortal elixirs:
1. *Great Harmony’s Spontaneous Dragon Embryo Mead*
2. *Jade-Bestowed Jade-Fluid Paste*
3. *Flying Boat’s Purple Radiance Flowing Essence*
4. *Taste of Radiant Cloud Azure’s Bloom*
5. *Nine Springs’ Rainbow Radiance Divine Elixir*
6. *Pure Gold Fluid’s Flower*
7. *Nine-Turned Frost-and-Snow Elixir*
8. *Nine-Cauldron Cloud Bloom*
9. *Cloud Radiance Water Stone*

*Flowing Flight, Dragon Embryo, Flying Elixir*—these are the superior medicines.
*Unlit Radiance Spring, Grand Clarity*—the middle grade.
*Nine Turns, Nine Cauldrons, Cloud Radiance*—the lower grade.

*The Supreme Eightfold Purple Nectar Divine Elixir*
Also called *Four Medicines’ Purple Blossom*,
Or *Faint-Fire Purple Jade Bloom*,
Or *Five-Pearl Radiant Elixir*,
Or *Crimson Dawn’s Morning Bloom*,
Or *Three-Flower Supreme Divine Elixir*,
Or *Supreme Flying Rigidity*,
Or *Nine Spirits’ Supreme Elixir*—eight grades in all.

The Nine Elixirs are nine paths, like nine methods.
Consuming them grants ten thousand generations of longevity.

Eight paths of Central Yellow:

To ascend to heaven as an immortal.
Bestowed by the Thearch Lord,
Hidden in the Jasper Terrace.
Without the true record, the method remains unattained.

*Langgan’s Luxuriant Bloom*
Sevenfold yang sun’s infant nine-jade fluid,
Eight jades’ essence,
Four-petaled purple nectar,
Five-jade crimson bloom,

Fly the void, traverse the hollow cavern,
The Yang Palace’s flowing fire court—
Within burns radiant flame,
Eight refinements’ spontaneous mysterious elixir.
Yellow qi’s yang essence,
Three paths follow their course.

*Thirty-Six Waters of Divine Elixir*
The guardian of golden fluid.

*The Ink Record of Elixir Simplicities*
*Sarira* is the golden fluid’s congealed essence,
The returning elixir’s transformation,
The true unity’s spontaneous qi.

*A Dose of Nine-Turn Returning Elixir*
One divine formula,
Bestowed by Lord Mao upon his two disciples.

*The Immortal Mother’s Golden Elixir*
Also named *Queen Mother of the West’s Age-Halting Qi Elixir*.
Blend three *sheng* of congealed white honey,
Three *jin* of elixir essence with bright white bloom,
Two *jin* of mica flakes in a bronze vessel.
Simmer with mulberry wood on gentle fire,
Freeze for three days,
Then steam for thirty days,
Exposing it to daylight’s full fire.
Boil the bronze vessel for three days and nights,
Dry in the sun,
Pray and pound thirty thousand times,
Sift finely into powder,
Form into pellets with white honey the size of small beans.
Take twenty pellets at dawn—
Longevity without death,
Complexion like a maiden’s.

*The Great Grotto True Scripture*
*Jade Elixir, Golden Nectar*—
Flying and soaring medicines.

The Supreme Dao Lord asked the Supreme Venerable Lord,
Who revealed to the child Lingzhen the *Crimson-Expanding Heavenly Immortal’s Method*,
The *Hundred Mushrooms of the Jade Court’s Upper Clarity Essence Medicines*, saying:
Six pavilions’ blooming blossoms,

Purple youths,
