Supreme rainbow plums,
Celestial Han’s great herbs,
Southern palace’s giant pearls,
Western land’s supporting elders,
Three beams’ dragon blossoms—
Sought by the numinous consorts.
Those who consume these will age after heaven,
These are what the Jade Clarity consumes,
What the Supreme treasures,
Enabling ascent to soar the radiant heavens,
Dividing dawn’s myriad paths,
Guarding and stabilizing yellow essence,
Morning infusion into the nine brains,
Hearing the mysterious tones to disperse the turbid,
Listening to the wind’s qi to expel the foul.

The next are the *Upper Clarity’s Secluded Mushrooms*,
The Supreme’s nine hours with eight lights,

Born from the Western Mound.

Crimson river’s crimson jade.
Northward drawing from the Grand Ultimate’s well,
Plucking the patterned pearl’s veins,
Cloud court’s divine peaches,
Kun garden’s level sparrows,
Night essence’s white herbs,
Azure ford’s green reeds,
True officials’ lush altars,
Mysterious capital’s three canopies.

Rightward embracing the jade maiden’s qi.
Above summoning the divine radiance,
Below drinking the mysterious rapids.
Gazing upward to pluck the orchid garden’s jasper essence,
Stooping to gather the mystic mound’s purple crabapples.

White Water’s numinous clams,
Eight Heavens’ crimson leeks;
Once born in ten thousand years,
Nine ranks of flowing light.
Those who obtain and consume them
transcend mortality and depart.
What the Heavenly Emperor ingests,
the Supreme’s most precious treasure—
beyond what the Grand Ultimate has heard,
beyond what the Median Perfected can attain.

Next in rank: the Grand Ultimate’s grade,
the Four Perfected’s constant treasures.
Thus named:
Nine Stones’ smelted smoke,
Elixir Fluid’s jade sap.
Dog’s Head’s flowing pearls,
Jasper Bloom’s stone essence.
Cinnabar Furnace’s golden liquid,
Purple Bloom’s crimson flowers.
Grand Purity’s ninefold transmutation,
Five Clouds’ nectar.

soaring as one yellow.

Azure Waves’ green coins.
Shang Mound’s surplus grain,
Flying Fields of Accumulated Stones.

Grand Qin’s mysterious firmness.
Enduring Light’s flowing radiance,
Cloud Youths soaring heavenward.
These are what the Heavenly Immortals ingest—
beyond what the earthbound wanderer has heard,
beyond what the mountain recluse has seen.

One must further know the Nine Transformations and Ten Changes,
the Eight Hidden Earthly Guards—
only then can one roam the Mysterious Void,
retrace the steps of the Celestial River,
ride clouds and mount dragons,
ascend and soar without bound.

Next: the Thirty-Six Mushrooms,
flying furnaces smelting smoke.
Solar Waters and Lunar Flowers,
the Five Lords’ marrow.
They fill and generate the five viscera,
refine and renew the body.
Cloud Fragments of the Radiant Soul,
golden powder and jade mulberry—
prolonging years and enhancing life,
one may attain ten thousand years.

Next: Mysterious Water’s cloud-flower nectar,
the Five Yellows’ dense numen,
Median Essence’s thousand-stone □-meal,
the many treasures of Azure Greens and Vermilion Flowers,
White Chariot’s flying nodes,
Flowing Steed’s purple-wood yellow.
A single dose grants one a lifespan of a thousand eras,
years advancing with the medicine,
life shifting with the drug.

Next: the lesser medicines—
pine and cypress’ yin fat,
mountain ginger, hidden spirit, calamus,
asparagus, sesame, yellow essence,
chrysanthemum, wolfberry, cliff honey,
hidden fungus, peach bark, marsh drain,
solomon’s seal, coptis, cimicifuga,
rehmannia, red plank and vermilion yellow,
spirit-flying cassia and water cinnamon—
the essences of myriad things,
their kinds too numerous to list in full.
Ingesting them, one may attain seven hundred years at best,
or three to four hundred at least.
The body radiates luster,
reverting to a youthful countenance.
Commanding a thousand spirits,
one becomes an Earthly Immortal,
walking the Five Peaks,
roaming the famed rivers.

*The Divine Medicines for Dispelling Demons*

Su Lin, styled Zixuan, was a native of Qushui in Puyang. He studied under the immortal Master Qiu of Mount Hua for five years, gaining the ability to enter and exit water and fire, his complexion like that of a maiden. The Master declared: "You are a true person."

*True Unity of the Three Primes*

The Lady of South Marchmount, surnamed Wei, styled Xian’an, was a native of Rencheng. On a midnight of clarity in the final month of winter, she heard amidst the profound darkness the resounding of bells and drums, the melodies of reed pipes and flutes—eight tones clamoring in harmony. Gazing outward into the empty void, she saw descending from the eastern heavens: the Supreme Ultimate Perfected One, Anduming; the Great Divinity of Eastern Florescence, the Azure Lad of Fangzhu; and the Perfected One of Jade Radiance of the Bihé Yang Valley of Fusang, the Perfected of Pure Emptiness, the Lesser You Immortal King Wang Zideng. The Lady prostrated herself in reverence and was bestowed two elixirs: the first, *Hidden Transcendence and Self-Concealing Spirit Powder*; the second, *Stone Essence and Golden Light Transfiguration Spirit Pellets*. After seven days of ingestion, past midnight, the Supreme Celestial Immortals dispatched a soaring chariot to receive her. The Lady employed the *Mirror Method* to entrust her form to a sword and pillow, and from that moment, she vanished.

*Inner Transmission of the Purple Void Primordial Lady*
*Celestial Immortal Medicines*

Should the Great Granary’s hoarded grain be piled high—
*Crimson Silken Vermilion Child* is cinnabar.
From the *Numinous Writ of Purple Text*:

*Sun-Soul of Cinnabar Mountain* is realgar;
*Moon-Essence of the Dark Terrace* is orpiment;
*White Silk Flying Dragon* is white quartz;
*Green-Waisted Maiden Within* is malachite;
*Purple Mound Literary Marquis* is amethyst;
*Flying Blossom of Jasper Wall* is graphite;
*Mysterious Pearl of the Northern Thearch* is nitre;
*Yellow Lad of the Nine Numinous* is sulfur;
*Golden Ram of the Five Essences* is actinolite;
*Flying Blossom of Rain-Florescence* is mica;
*White Tiger’s Shed Fangs* is gold-tooth stone;
*Flowing Cinnabar White Cream* is ceruse;
*Reversed-Marching Divine Bone* is halite.

Those who ascend in learning ingest the Dao of sun and moon, meditate upon the Lesser Yang Perfected of Cinnabar Numinosity, and fill a lapis lazuli vessel with *Jade Spring Azure Fungus Cream* to anoint their destined form. They further take a golden crucible to refine and congeal the cream, bathing their bodies in the yellow qi of yang essence. *Mysterious Water Jade Liquid*—also called *Flying Dragon Cloud Marrow* or *Refined Quintuple-Stone Flower Cream*—when consumed for fifteen years, bestows a jade radiance upon the body, longevity coeval with heaven and earth, and command over ghosts and spirits. After three years, one’s hair may write by night. This formula surpasses the ingestion of eight-fold refined minerals, excelling even the *Jade Nectar of Cassia Water and Mica*.

From the *Great Cavern*:
*Mysterious Ripple of Dark Herbage* is the marrow of black sesame, also called *Mysterious Clarity*.
From the *Feminine Unity and Five Elders*:
*Purple Forest Marrow*.
From the *Lord Mao*:
*Fill-Soul and Secure-Spirit*.

The *Seventy-Four Directions Flying Spirit Pellets*—when consumed, one may ride the void and walk the emptiness.

From the *Purple Radiance of Scorching Flame*:
The *Grand Unity’s Fourfold Guardian Pellets* confer longevity of ten thousand years.

From the *Central Scripture of the Nine Perfected*:
Lady Wei’s ears and eyes grew clear and bright at eighty-three. In the moon’s light, she inscribed Daoist talismans for disciples. Through meditative absorption, she entered her chamber, fasting for a hundred days or even decades.

From the *Inner Transmission of the Purple Void Primordial Sovereign*:
Earthbound Perfected Ones first expel the Three Corpse-Worms, which bear three names and sever three lives. If the Three Ghosts remain, they pierce the Six Palaces and agitate the Five Spirits.

From the *Unified Method of the Primordial True One*:
The *Supreme Eight Jade Flying Essence Elixir*—the Perfected One Mao Ying, styled Shu and Shen, hailed from Nanguan in Xianyang. His master was the North-Facing Northern River Ghost Valley Master, who dwelt in reclusion on Mount Hua. At eighteen, Ying fled his home for Mount Heng. His great-grandfather, Mao Meng, had once ascended to heaven in broad daylight upon clouds and dragons amid Mount Hua. The village’s ballad sang:
*"The divine immortal attained by Mao at first perfection,
Rode the dragon upward to enter the Grand Clarity.
Now he sports on the Dark Continent and Crimson City,
Passing through generations to come—here in me, Ying."*
The Thearch’s master lauded him in the twelfth month.

Ying remained on the mountain for six years, whereupon he dreamed of the Supreme Mystery Jade Maiden presenting him with a jade writ and leading him, saying: "The Western Citadel King Lord possesses the true Dao." Thereupon he bowed his head in reverence and journeyed to the Numinous Citadel to meet the King Lord. In the seventeenth year, the King Lord charged him with overseeing the divine registers of robes and scriptures. After three years of cultivation, he was commanded to ride forth to White Jade Mill Mountain, where the Queen Mothers of the Azure Palace resided. The King Lord further bestowed upon Ying a dose of the Ninefold Cyclically Transformed Elixir and a single immortal formula. The Heavenly Thearch then appointed him as Upper Minister of the Eastern Marchmount and Director of Life and Death at Huolin, overseeing the registers of life and death in Wu and Yue. Thereupon he instructed his two younger brothers to ingest the Azure Tooth. Later, he told Ji Weiqing: "You ought to ingest the Divine Formula of the Four Fans Powder, which the Wind Sovereign received from the Yellow Emperor—I once received it from the Most High Master, and now transmit it to you." He also addressed Si Heqing, saying: "You ought to ingest the Queen Mother’s Four Lads’ Elixir Powder to replenish the marrow and fortify the brain." Both formulas were wondrous. After eighteen years of ingesting the medicines, his two younger brothers’ complexions became like those of maidens. *The Inner Transmission of Lord Mao*.

May the Mysterious Mother share with me the natural Seven Treasures Jade Syrup and the Golden Elixir of Purple Concealed Zhi. To the right, gather the Five Summons Night Radiance, Phoenix Brain, Tiger Foam, Cloud Lang, and Jade Frost—with but a single taste of these wondrous flavors, one brushes against the Great Void.

*The Feminine One*

The Sage Lord led the Azure Youth to sit and served the flowing rosy nectar, red trees with white seeds, and crimson woods with azure fruits.

*The Purple Text of Numinous Writ*

The August Person was dispatched by the Lord of Fusang, governing the immortal officials of Mount Emei. His body stood nine feet tall, his fur covering his form, and he dwelled beneath the northern cliff. Within, his house was made of azure jade, his bed of yellow jade, draped with curtains of patterned silk, and burning the incense of a thousand harmonies. His attendants were all jade maidens among the immortals, and three seated treasures were all Great Clarity Immortal Kings. They set out jujubes brimming in measures and rinsed their mouths with the numinous nectar of the Vermilion Palace’s Jade Well.

*The Five Talismans*

The Dark Water Cloud Blossom Nectar, also called the Cloud-Stored Vermilion Nectar. Drinking five *ge* daily, one’s face becomes youthful and one’s body fragrant.

*The Central Scripture of the Nine Perfected*

To study the Dao, one must wander the palaces of the sun and moon, meet the kings of the sun and moon, and drink the essence of the sun and moon, the golden-bound nectar.

*Wisdom*

The Perfected One of the Great Ultimate consumed the thousand-stone Azure Essence Rice, the divine formula of the highest immortals. Eating this rice renders one immune to all harm. After ten years, the spirit of the Azure Essence coalesces to summon wind and rain, and a single dose extends one’s lifespan by a thousand years.

*The Inner Transmission of Perfected Lord Wang of Pure Emptiness*

The five divine zhi of Mount Juqu:

The first is the Dragon Immortal Zhi, resembling intertwined dragons with leaves as scales and roots like coiled dragons. Those who consume it are appointed as Perfected Ones of the Great Ultimate.

The second is the Ginseng Zhi, crimson in color with a radiant vermilion glow, its branches and leaves chiming like metal and stone when struck. Those who consume it are appointed as Grand Masters of the Great Ultimate.

The third is the Swallow Embryo Zhi, purple in hue, shaped like a sunflower with leaves bearing the likeness of flying swallows, its luminosity penetrating and clear. Eating one stalk appoints one as the Dragon-Tiger Immortal Lord of Great Clarity and Rectifying Unity Gentleman of the Court.

The fourth is the Night Cavern Zhi, green in color with white fruits like plums, standing three to four feet tall, its leaves resembling cypress. At night, its fruits illuminate an entire chamber like moonlight. Each stalk bears nine fruits, which fall to the ground like seven-inch mirror trays of fox, landing one to two inches thick. At night, they appear as large as oxen, and by day, they move. Eating one branch appoints one as Left Imperial Censor of the Immortal Officials of Great Clarity.

The fifth is the White Righteous Jade Zhi. Splitting open and consuming its core appoints one as Direct Perfected Censor of the Three Offices. Those who consume this zhi are commanded by the Most High to have the Perfected One of the Great Ultimate dispatch the Five Thearchs to bow in audience and appoint them.

During its four seasons, the Swallow Embryo Zhi glows with flowing radiance, its light soaring in paired flight, illuminating the grasses at night. The zhi consumed by Lord Mao was planted by the Perfected Lord of the Great Ultimate of Fangzhu in Qingzhou, not of this kind.

*The Inner Transmission of Lord Mao*

The four varieties of Great Ultimate Concealed Zhi:

Some are four-sided in color, their light illuminating a hundred paces.

One kind is azure, resembling a moon mirror, three layers stacked together, five to six inches tall, called the Great Ultimate Numinous Mirror Concealing Heaven Azure Zhi.

Another is white, like the Dipper star, with seven nodes marked by stars and stems as its framework, three to four feet tall, called the Great Ultimate Concealing Chen Numinous Soul Zhi.

Another is crimson, like a small jujube tree with fruits like *lu*, its brilliance shining brightly, three to four feet tall, called the Mirror Framework Concealing Mystery Great Ultimate Golden Heaven Zhi.

Another is gray-green, like an overturned canopy on the ground, layered and circular, seven to eight inches in diameter, its clear light flowing like a candle, three to four inches tall, called the Great Ultimate Mysterious Moon Reclining Dragon Zhi.

*The Golden Tablet of the Great Tenuity in Jade Script*

Dig six feet into the earth.

Plant one mirror fruit and irrigate it with five *ge* of yellow water; in three years it sprouts grass, bearing peach-like seeds. The Five-Colored Phoenix-Brain Zhi, when its fruit is consumed, ascends to the Great Ultimate, and upon spitting upon the earth transforms into a phoenix, which one may mount to soar—also called the Great Ultimate Concealing Zhi.

*The Purple Text of the Numinous Writ*
When Yin Xi accompanied the Old Master on their travels, they ascended the Hall of Square Zhang on Mount Changyang and beheld the Nine Elderly Men chewing the Nine-Intertwined Zhi. Journeying south, they ascended Mount Suqiu and partook of the Nine-Radiance Zhi.

*The Perfected of the Primordial Above*
In the Land of the Heavenly Mirror, on Phoenix Mountain, grows the Gold-Jade Purple Zhi. The various heavens scatter fragrant blossoms, while the sun and moon irrigate it with numinous radiance; when ingested, the five spirits open, and jade maidens proffer golden trays.

*The Twenty-Four Images of Life*
The Five Zhi: their fragrance pervades the immortal peaks, where numinous branches flourish in the numinous grottoes. Once in ten thousand kalpas they blaze forth, and the various heavens intermingle in wondrous union. Tranquil awakening lingers like a single tree, as grains of sand endure for a single morning.

The Lady Wang, Middle Attendant of Eastern Florescence, wrote in her poem:
*"The Jade Pool irrigates the fields of quartz."*

*The Perfect Writ of the Great Cavern*
The Jade-Fat Zhi grows on the Mountain of Jade, where jade cream flows forth and congeals over ten thousand years into a fat-like substance, resembling the forms of birds and beasts, luminous as moon essence. When blended with the juice of the Heartless Grass, it instantly becomes liquid; consuming one *dou* grants a thousand years of life.

*The Catalog of Numinous Treasure Zhi*
*The Five Sacred Peaks in Pictorial Form*

The Zhi that is born together with Heaven and Earth is placed in the offices of the Thirty-Two Heavens’ Grotto-Courts, where perfected transcendents and flying immortals dwell. The divine herb Jade Zhi upon its heights grants men immortality.

*Wondrous Sayings of the Yellow Emperor and Laozi*

**Stone Zhi**
Grows on secluded mountains by the sea where stones accumulate. Its form has head and tail, four feet—red as coral, white as silver fat, black as lacquer-dyed silk, blue as kingfisher plumes, yellow as gold—radiant and translucent as solid ice. On dark nights, its light is visible from a hundred paces. The largest weigh over ten *jin*. To refine Stone-Image Zhi, pound it thirty-six thousand times; consume a square-inch spoonful, and after finishing one *jin*, one gains a hundred thousand years of life. It also grows on high mountains near water, shaped like plates or bowls, no more than a foot in diameter, with seven apertures called Seven Luminaries or nine apertures called Nine Radiants, all shining like stars. These one hundred twenty kinds are all Stone Zhi, recorded in the *Jade Strategies of the Great One*.

**Wood Zhi**
Pine resin transformed after a thousand years, shaped like a lotus blossom, called Wood Might-Joy. It glows when viewed at night and, when worn, repels weapons. Its root resembles a seated person, seven feet long; when carved, it bleeds. Applied to the feet, one may walk upon water; applied to the body, one becomes invisible. Mixed with giant sesame and used to illuminate the ground at night, if gold or jade treasures lie buried, the light turns azure and droops downward. Consuming ten *jin* grants a thousand years of life. When pine resin ages three thousand years, its bark contains congealed fat shaped like a dragon, called Qi-Node Zhi, weighing ten *jin*; consuming one *jin* grants five hundred years. Fan-Tao Zhi resembles a rising dragon, its blossoms like cinnabar gauze, its fruit like green-black birds, five feet tall, growing on the shady side of famous mountains above flowing streams. Consuming one stalk grants five thousand years. Great Spring Zhi is a parasite on large trees, resembling a lotus flower, with a sweet and pungent taste. Jian-Fruit Zhi is the fruit of the Jian Tree, growing in Du-Guang, its bark like a tassel snake, its fruit like a *yue* bird. When these Zhi are blended and consumed, one ascends in broad daylight.

**Herb Zhi**
Solitary-Sway Zhi moves without wind, its stem red as cinnabar, its root as large as a *kui* measure, or as small as a chicken’s egg. Twelve stems encircle a single large root, which grows on Tiger-Longevity Mountain at Wu Slope, resembling ox horns, three to four feet long, azure in color. Consuming a square-inch spoonful grants a thousand years. Hemp-Mother Zhi has purple blossoms. Pearl Zhi has a yellow stem and red leaves, its fruit like plums, purple, twenty-four strung like beads. White-Tally Zhi resembles a plum, blooming in heavy snow and bearing fruit in late winter. Nine-Bend Vermilion Grass has nine curves, each bearing three fruits. Five-Hearing Zhi resembles a tower, its stem square, its leaves in five colors like an inverted canopy, with sweet dew and purple qi rising several feet. Dragon-Street Zhi sprouts in pairs at three nodes during mid-spring, twelve in total. All Herb Zhi, when consumed, grant either a thousand or two thousand years of life.

**Fungus Zhi**
Shaped like palaces, carriages, dragons, tigers, or flying birds, in five colors without constancy, comprising one hundred ten kinds. Those who consume them ascend as immortals; the middling gain several thousand years, the lesser a thousand years.

**Lotus Fruit**
Also called Water Zhi, paired with the osprey’s head as yin and yang. On the *wu* day of the eighth month, gather lotus seeds; on the morning of the ninth month, gather lotus roots, dry them in the shade by degree for a hundred days, and prepare them. On the *mao* day of the first month at dawn, consume a square-inch spoonful with well-flower water four or five times daily for a hundred days to cure all illnesses; prolonged consumption leads to transcendence.

Though but ten inches long, it cleaves jade.

**Scholars of the Highest Immortality**

Inscribe this upon silver tablets for the longevity of the Upper and Lower Immortals. The Three Great Spirits sigh in timely response: within the Five Marchmounts, the great treasuries of gold, silver, jade marrow, and lapis lazuli burst forth in radiance, illuminating the ten directions. The Eight Sea Spirit-Kings emerge from the azure depths bearing coral trees, five million *li* in height, their seven-jeweled blossoms and leaves overspreading the vast ocean. The heavens of the Three Realms rain fine luminous pearls, while the Five Marchmounts reveal the divine immortal mountain treasuries, their five-hued beauteous jades gleaming with inexhaustible splendor. *Scripture of the Womb-Dwelling Karma*

**Realm of Lapis Lazuli**
It is said the land of this realm is entirely of lapis lazuli.

**Radiant Youths**
Following the sun and moon in their revolutions, three thousand six hundred in crimson robes, they descend to the dark sea and stir the golden essence and purple-light jades. *Three Sovereigns*

**Liberation Through This Scripture**
All within the Three Realms are bound by affinity. The heavens and peoples offer fragrant flowers, seven-jeweled thrones, gold and silver, pearls and jades, coral, and agate. *Original Beginning’s Wisdom, Right Contemplation, and Liberation*

*The Scripture on Dwelling in the Womb*

For the East: azure gauze, ninety feet—alternatively, nine feet.

The four corners together total four hundred eighty feet.

These ten directions’ patterned silks serve as the pledge,
to deliver and ferry the souls of the long night.

The Celestial Kitchen
*The Wisdom of Contemplating the Body*

The Perfected of the Nine Palaces—

The Perfected of Highest Clarity
eastward journeyed to Mulberry Grove, reaching the Capital of the Nine Elder Immortals,

*The Annals of the Three Celestial Lords’ Fiery Deeds*

Commanding the Six Ding Spirits,
divine lads attend in guard.

The Queen Mother
ordered the Left Guard Immortal Lads to array the cloud-bridles in solemn order,

where all the sacred hosts of the ten directions gathered as one.

The Heavenly Worthy manifested in golden splendor,

with tables of the Seven Treasures.

*The Purple Writ Record and Transmission*

In the Lower Heaven of the Northern Direction,
the Land of Broad Cold possesses non-glutinous rice.
Its people are white and bear pearls, called *Yanshu*,
which are placed beneath the cauldron—
their radiance flaring forth like mani jewels.
When their light shines upon the rice, it ripens,
and people from all directions come to partake.

*The Three Sovereigns*

Thirty-six myriad leagues east of Mount Sumeru,
there is a land named Pure Harmony.
Its people eat once every three years,
where rice from the roots grows three feet long,
and its people stand six feet tall.
In that land, one day’s three meals consist of cooked non-glutinous rice,
while another day’s meal comes but once in three years.

*The Cavern Abyss*

The Azure Essence Lord of the Imperial Register

Feasting on essence and swallowing qi,

Orchid wine and golden nectar,

Pepper grows in Shu and Han,

Born with heaven and earth,

*The Five Talismans*

Ginger is born of Great Yang,
hailing from the same homeland as pepper.
It contains the qi of Mars,
hidden deep within mountain recesses.
Turning from yin toward yang,
sealing the demon gate.
Those who consume it long-term
shall have a lifespan as enduring as heaven and earth.

Yin Xi,
following the Venerable Lord northward to ascend the ridge of Empty Grotto,
beheld the Northern Hua Perfected Duke and the Four Hua Immortals,
along with countless lofty perfected ones,
eating the divine melon of Empty Grotto,

Traveling west to the Mountain of the Great Tortoise,

emerald peaches, and purple pears—
their fruits as large as vases.

arhats, and those of the five supernormal powers,

Fragrant flowers, celestial maidens,

A thousand chariots and ten thousand dragons trod the void.
Journeying eastward to ascend the Sun Cavern of Everlasting Yang Mountain,

and scattered the blossoms of the Spring Forest.

*Scroll Five of the Precious Scripture of the Highest Clarity begins*
*Chapter Ten: The Cycles of Time*

The Ten Directional Celestial Worthies
comprehend the past
as if it were an object in the palm.
The Dao is
the root of all things.
The Ten Directional Celestial Worthies,
understanding the dharmas of the future,
see them as if present before the eyes.
The meaning of the fivefold convergence of celestial script—
beneath your feet, the salvation of heaven and humanity unfolds,
the great Dharma expands,
its blessings suffusing the ten directions.

Within the great city,
forty myriad leagues in each of the four directions—east, west, south, and north—
the center is filled with mustard-seed stones,
each likewise forty myriad leagues in extent.
Once every three years, the celestial beings
brush the mustard-seed stones with flying garments
until all the mustard seeds are gathered—
this is called one kalpa,
illustrating the speech of the Hu, Yue, Man, and Yi.
*The Three August Ones*

Heaven and earth complete one formation and one decay—
this is called one kalpa.
Consider a mountain of stone,
four hundred leagues in circumference,
where celestial beings, once every hundred years,
brush the stone with gauze until it is entirely worn away—
one kalpa is thus completed,
and it is as long as this.
*The True One’s Spontaneous Nature*

The Most High Orthodox Unity Perfected One,
Master of the Three Heavens, Zhang Daoling, said:
One kalpa is like an empty city with no one inside,
spanning four hundred leagues in circuit,
forty leagues in height,
filled with mustard seeds.
Once every hundred years, a flying celestial being descends
to take one mustard seed—
when all are exhausted, one kalpa ends.

Heaven’s qi reaches its extreme in Great Yin,
earth’s qi is exhausted in Great Yang.
When yang is agitated, it rebels;
when yin is excessive, it erodes.
The rebellion and erosion of yin and yang
are called the lesser kalpa.
Heaven completes nine thousand nine hundred revolutions for yang erosion,
earth completes nine thousand three hundred revolutions for yin rebellion.
The decay and transformation of heaven and earth
are called the great kalpa.

Once every nine years of heaven and earth,
they face the Perfected One.
*The Arrayed Records of the Nine Mystery Dao Sovereigns*

The Latter Sagely Lord and Mother
dreamed of dark clouds and sun and moon passing through her form to nurture her,
and of a leather-scaled dragon spouting water into the ritual vessel.

Those who obtain the Scripture of Numinous Treasure
may dream of Daoist immortals and celestial beings,
or of cloud chariots, jeweled canopies, dragons, and phoenixes;
or of ascending to immortality and beholding the palaces of the sagely ones,
with their seven treasures of pearls and jade;
or of ascending to heaven and seeing the Heavenly Kings and Celestial Lords.

For inauspicious dreams, recite the incantation:
“O Yellow Gate Divine Master, Purple Portal General,
grasping the halberd and wielding the bell,
dispel the malign currents,
transform misfortune into fortune,
and let life and death know no hindrance.”

Upon encountering an auspicious dream,
upon waking, rub the eyes thirty-four times
and click the teeth thirty-four times.

The incantation reads:
“Supreme High Essence, Radiant Spirits of the Three Emperors,
Scarlet Palace resplendent and clear, auspicious omens reveal their truth.
The Three Origins soften the poised souls, the Heavenly Sovereign bestows the Scripture.
Wherever one turns, harmony prevails, ascending as an immortal to the Upper Clarity,
Ever in the company of Jade Perfected, together gathering in the Purple Court.”

**Section Eleven: Resources and Requisites**

The master of great methods shall establish halls and palaces of the seven treasures, chambers and pavilions, gardens and groves, bathing pools and canopied seats, carvings and adornments of the seven treasures, incense burners and ritual implements. Burn incense of all precious substances, scatter flowers of every renowned kind.

**Karmic Retribution**
Movement and stillness should be worthy of observation.
Attire must follow proper method.

**Crowns of the Divine and Sagely Ones of High Virtue Among the Heavens**
All are bound with white jade and cloud silk, or with seven-hued auroral mist.

**Ninefold Radiance of Essence and Qi**
*Flying Dawn Treasure Crown*: The crown of the Supreme Divine Immortal, Radiant Sovereign of Primordial Qi.

**Chapter Twelve: On Abodes**

The Ninefold Golden Citadel of Kunlun Mountain—
Where the divine and the immortal jointly govern.

The Seven-Treasure Ninefold Citadel of Heaven’s Summit Mountain—
Within stands a seven-treasure hall; atop the hall rises a seven-treasure terrace of ninety thousand tiers. The citadel spans two hundred forty thousand *li* in circumference, thirty-four thousand *li* in height. The terrace towers thirty-six thousand *li* above the citadel, its pavilions, towers, and jeweled chambers arrayed. All heavens burn incense and sweep in attendance; the Great Sage Honored Spirits and the Wondrous-Practice Perfected circle the citadel in reverence; the divine and wondrous jade maidens encircle it; the Primordial Origin hosts surround it; divine dragons and vermilion phoenixes soar and alight about it. *The Inner Writ of the Mysterious and Wondrous*

The Celestial Pond Citadel of Mountain-Reed Land—
A thousand *li* square, atop the citadel stand five golden terraces and twelve jade towers, gates of flowing essence, terraces of luminous azure.

The Purple Tenuity Terrace of the Central Heaven—
Presiding over the opening of the Nine Glooms’ gates, releasing the souls of the Long Night.

The Primordial Terrace of the Void-Transcending Balance in the Central Heaven—
Presiding over the records of heaven and earth’s opening and closing, encompassing the supreme Dao above the Eight Poles.

There is also the Terrace of the Nine Nights.

The Nine-Tiered Jade Capital Terrace of the Luminous Void Bright Hall in the Central Heaven—
Presiding over the rites of Flying Celestial Perfected paying homage.

The Purple Terrace of the Southern Yang Upper Palace in the Dragon-Transforming Brahma-Passing Heaven—
Presiding over the assessment of the weight of merit in attaining the Dao.

The Terrace of the Celestial Rule Perfected of Yuan-Source River and You—
Presiding over the records of those who have entered extinction, guiding those reborn.

The Terrace of Hearing the Wind in the Kunlun Mysterious Orchard—
Where immortals dwell.

*The Grand Celestial Emperor Lord*

The mighty command marshals the host of spirits,
aligning armor and sharpening blades,

where golden clouds of radiant luminance reveal
within the Eight Gates a Jade City and seven-jeweled forests of jasper.

The *Upper Clarity Goldwatch Palace* has four gates.
The Goldwatch stands on the left,
its pillars of gold, its canopy of purple clouds,
engraved with gold inscriptions bearing the names of the soaring immortals.

its pillars of jade, its canopy of green clouds,
engraved with jade inscriptions bearing the names of the Supreme Perfected.

with the Azure Dragon and White Tiger stationed below,
dwelling to left and right.
Celestial beasts of vast form stand guard on either side.

*From* The Cavernous Splendor of Golden Mystery
The Nine-Tiered Terrace.

The Dao and Virtue.

The Jasper Terrace of the Western March—
a hundred leagues in breadth, the seat of the Great Emperor’s governance. *From* The Great Cavern.

The Luminous Perfected is the name of a nine-heaven terrace,
shining resplendent above the Nine Empyreans. Three suns rise there upon the earth, and the cry of the Luminous Perfected Sun is called "Phoenix-Born."

Dragon Mountain is the name of a lofty terrace in the Jade Purity Heaven.
The Golden Chamber stands above the radiant rosy clouds, and the Nine Gates lie within the Jasper Towers.
All these are the lodgings of the Grand Tenuity, the Jade Palaces of the Celestial Emperor.

In the Jade Purity Heaven above, there are Three Passes and Jade Terraces,
governing the southwest corner. The first is the Heavenly Pass, also called the Heavenly Chart and the Heavenly Gate.
The birth-gate of the Nine Lands, the pivot of opening and closing.

Above the Three Passes stands a Jade Terrace, the thoroughfare of the host of immortals.

The First Heavenly Pass—Vermilion Gate and Jade Gatehouse—
supports a nine-tiered Jade Terrace, twelve hundred rods in height.
Purple clouds canopy its summit, streaming lightning illumines its eaves. The Great Void’s Jade Dawn oversees its emptiness. Above, the luminous ones wear flying-morning jade crowns of five-colored insignia, girded with swords and jade pendants. Terrace-borne rosy clouds reflect its chambers; sun and moon shine upon its halls. Three hundred immortals attend each Perfected One.
Upon the terrace stands a Jade Register, bearing the jade name of the Highest August Supreme Perfected, the Supreme Emperor. The ledgers of later sagely perfected ones are kept by the Jade Dawn Overseer.

The Second Heavenly Chart—Vermilion Gate and Jade Gatehouse—
supports a six-tiered Jade Terrace, nine hundred rods in height.
Azure clouds shade its summit; the sun’s cinnabar essence traverses its precincts. The Supreme Lord’s Direct Perfected Jade Gentleman, named Mysterious Earth Earl, wears a dark-morning crown and robes of nine-colored insignia. Upon the Jade Astral Tower, cinnabar radiance and purple canopies luxuriate in its chambers. The hundred harmonies’ fragrance arises in its courtyard. Three hundred perfected ones attend each attendant.
Upon the terrace stands a Golden Register, bearing golden tablets, jade peaches, and twelve scrolls of Purple Phoenix Cinnabar Chapters.

The Third Heavenly Pass—Vermilion Gate and Jade Gatehouse—
supports a three-tiered Jade Terrace, six hundred rods in height.
Purple clouds canopy its summit; sun and moon reflect upon its walls. The Great Emperor’s Perfected Jade Controller, named Unchanging Life, wears a far-advancing crown of seven-colored insignia. He presides over the Jade Astral Tower. The hundred harmonies’ fragrance and self-luminous radiance illumine its chambers. Three hundred perfected immortals attend.
Above stand the Three Pure Treasure Scriptures in three hundred fascicles and the ledgers of perfected ones learning immortality. *From* The Entry and Exit of the Myriad Perfected.

The Supreme Lord’s Seven Treasures and Flowing Rosy Clouds in the Heaven of Level Nurturance within the Jade Capital—
the Cavernous Primordial Terrace governs the radiance of the auspicious clouds in the celestial center. *From* The Seven Luminaries’ Primordial Precepts.

The Palace of Radiant Scenery in the Heaven of Grand Primordiality—
the office generates the ninefold pure qi. The qi-smoke transforms chaotically into vermilion clouds of nine hues. Those who enter its smoke alter their appearance; those who dwell within its smoke undergo a hundred transformations.

The Palace of Myriad Flowers in the Lesser Existence Jade Perfection Heaven—
the domain of the Jade Lord. Here are stored the treasure scriptures of the Supreme Emperor and the hidden writings of the Jade Purity.

The Great Square Knot of the Lesser Existence Palace—
the Jade Radiance Jade Morning Office.

The Circular Flower Palace of the Yellow Thearch—
the Primordial Beginning’s Jasper Hall for summoning guests, located in the Vermilion Brightness Heaven upon the Southern Fire Peak’s Cinnabar Numinous Cavern Palace. *From* The Twenty-Four Lives.

The Vermilion Palace of the Southern Mound—Ninefold Numinous Blessing Hall—
possesses a spontaneous kitchen and divine scriptures that deliver destiny.

The Thirty-First Heaven—Overseer of Immortals, Controller of Horses—
Jade Lads and Jade Maidens, immortals each, thrice monthly attend the Purple Tenuity Palace to erase and discard earthly registers. *From* The Nine Dark Suns’ Record.

The Golden Flower Upper Palace in the Heaven of Harmonious Youth—

The Master’s Register of Life and Death—
the Southern Half-Long-Life Palace within the Primordial Chaos’ Veiled Heaven.

*From* The Supreme Clarity’s Treasured Scripture of the Dao, Scroll Five.
